What you need to make is **not a full Vera clone** and definitely **not a new LLM**.  
You need to build a **stateful Merchant AI Assistant service** that behaves like a better version of Vera under the judge’s API contract.


**What the challenge is actually asking for**
You are building an HTTP bot with 2 big jobs:


1. **Context brain**
- Accept category, merchant, customer, and trigger context over time
- Store latest version correctly
- Use that context later while composing messages


2. **Conversation brain**
- Decide when to proactively message on `/v1/tick`
- Reply intelligently on `/v1/reply`
- Handle multi-turn merchant/customer conversations
- Detect bad patterns like auto-replies, off-topic, and explicit intent transitions


So this is really a mix of:
- context store
- orchestration engine
- message composer
- conversation state machine
- judge-compatible API server


**What output quality matters most**
The judge is not only checking “did your server respond.”  
It is mainly checking whether your messages are:


- specific
- category-correct
- merchant-aware
- trigger-aware
- compelling enough to get a reply


So your system should feel like:
- “I know this merchant”
- “I know why I am messaging now”
- “I know what type of business this is”
- “I know whether to sell, inform, remind, or act”


**What you need to build conceptually**


**1. API layer**
You must expose:
- `/v1/context`
- `/v1/tick`
- `/v1/reply`
- `/v1/healthz`
- `/v1/metadata`


This is the outer shell. Without this, nothing runs.


**2. Context storage**
You need a store for:
- categories
- merchants
- customers
- triggers
- conversations


Important behavior:
- versioned updates
- replace old context with newer version
- keep state across requests
- support incremental updates during test


This is very important because the judge will inject new context mid-run.


**3. Composition engine**
This is the core “Vera-like” part.


Given:
- category
- merchant
- trigger
- optional customer


You must produce:
- `body`
- `cta`
- `send_as`
- `suppression_key`
- `rationale`


This is the real heart of the challenge.


**4. Trigger routing**
Not every trigger should be handled the same way.


You need some routing like:
- research digest -> informative + curiosity
- performance dip -> action-oriented help
- recall due -> customer reminder / booking
- dormant merchant -> re-engagement
- milestone -> congratulatory + next step
- hostile reply -> polite boundary
- explicit “yes, do it” -> action mode immediately


This routing layer is one of the main things that will separate average bots from strong bots.


**5. Conversation state handling**
This challenge is not single-shot only.


You need conversation memory for:
- what message you already sent
- whether merchant replied
- whether merchant is interested
- whether merchant is likely an auto-reply
- whether conversation should end
- what next step is appropriate


You especially need logic for:
- auto-reply detection
- intent transition detection
- graceful exit
- not repeating yourself
- not continuing qualification after a clear yes


**6. Message policy / guardrails**
You need rules that validate your own outputs before returning them.


Examples:
- no hallucinated facts
- no generic “grow your business” fluff
- one primary CTA
- category voice must fit
- honor merchant/customer language
- avoid repetition
- keep body concise
- customer-facing messages only when customer context exists and trigger scope matches


This is very important because the judge will punish generic and wrong-tone replies.


**7. Suppression / de-dup logic**
The problem explicitly mentions `suppression_key`.


You need a mechanism so your bot does not:
- send the same proactive message repeatedly
- send duplicate trigger-driven nudges
- keep spamming on every tick


Restraint is rewarded in this challenge.


**8. Fast enough inference**
You have only 30 seconds per request, and really you should target far below that.


That means your design should be:
- simple retrieval
- limited prompt size
- deterministic generation
- low-latency response path


This challenge is not asking for huge agent loops or tool-heavy autonomous reasoning.


**What your system should probably look like**
At high level:


1. Judge sends context
2. You store it
3. Judge calls `/v1/tick`
4. You inspect active triggers
5. For each trigger:
   - fetch merchant + category + maybe customer
   - decide whether to send
   - choose message strategy
   - compose message
   - validate
   - return action
6. Judge sends merchant reply on `/v1/reply`
7. You:
   - update conversation state
   - classify reply
   - decide `send` / `wait` / `end`
   - compose next move


**What you do not need to build**
You do not need:
- a new LLM
- real WhatsApp integration
- real Google Business Profile tools
- real payment or merchant APIs
- real Vera backend complexity
- full production tool execution system like the repo has


This challenge is much narrower.  
It wants **the decisioning and messaging intelligence**, not the whole production infrastructure.


**Best way to think about it**
This is a **judged composition + conversation orchestration problem**, not a general chatbot problem.


You are being tested on whether you can do these 4 things well:


1. Read structured business context correctly
2. Convert it into the right kind of merchant/customer message
3. React intelligently in follow-up turns
4. Stay operationally reliable under the judge harness


**Main capabilities your bot must show**
If I were reducing the whole challenge to a checklist, it would be this:


- Understand the 4-context framework deeply
- Maintain context versions correctly
- Compose proactive merchant/customer messages
- Use trigger-specific messaging
- Personalize using merchant data
- Match category voice
- Detect auto-replies fast
- Detect “yes, let’s do it” and switch to action mode
- Know when to wait
- Know when to end
- Avoid repetition and spam
- Adapt when context changes mid-test


**Where Vera repo knowledge helps you**
Looking at Vera helps mainly in these ways:
- Vera is orchestration over context, not a standalone model
- real value is in prompts + state + routing + tool/action logic
- merchant state and conversation state matter a lot
- category fit and specific hooks matter more than generic copy
- production pain points become your opportunity:
  - auto-reply handling
  - intent handoff
  - specificity
  - curiosity/social-proof messaging


**What you should design before coding**
You should first design these on paper:


1. Context schema handling
2. Internal store shape
3. Trigger taxonomy
4. Message strategy per trigger type
5. Reply classification categories
6. Conversation state machine
7. Output validation checklist
8. Suppression rules
9. Prompt template(s)
10. Timeout/performance strategy


**Most important insight**
A weak submission will act like:
- “LLM, here is some JSON, write a message.”


A strong submission will act like:
- “I have a structured engine that decides whether to send, why now, what angle to use, how to phrase it, and how to react next.”


That is the real difference.

- components
- data flow
- decision engine
- prompt strategy
- conversation state machine  
all without writing code.

- **The challenge Vera** = a **small, judge-facing, stateful bot** with a strict API contract


So the challenge is asking for a **much narrower slice** of Vera.

  - `/v1/context`
  - `/v1/tick`
  - `/v1/reply`
  - `/v1/healthz`
  - `/v1/metadata`
- stores pushed contexts correctly
- composes proactive messages from:
  - category
  - merchant

- adapts when new context versions are pushed mid-test

So the challenge is much closer to:

Current repo:

End points doubt 1 – 
They expect **5 endpoints**.


**1. `POST /v1/context`**
Purpose: judge pushes new or updated context into your bot.


Input:
```json
{
  "scope": "category" | "merchant" | "customer" | "trigger",
  "context_id": "some_id",
  "version": 3,
  "payload": { "...full context object..." },
  "delivered_at": "2026-04-26T10:00:00Z"
}
```


Expected behavior:
- store context by `(scope, context_id)`
- same version again = no-op / idempotent
- higher version replaces old one
- lower/stale version should be rejected


Success output:
```json
{
  "accepted": true,
  "ack_id": "ack_abc123",
  "stored_at": "2026-04-26T10:00:00.123Z"
}
```


Stale version output:
```json
{
  "accepted": false,
  "reason": "stale_version",
  "current_version": 5
}
```


Bad input output:
```json
{
  "accepted": false,
  "reason": "invalid_scope",
  "details": "..."
}
```


**Sense of this endpoint**
This is your bot’s memory-loader.  
The judge keeps feeding your bot category, merchant, customer, and trigger data over time. Your bot must remember and update it correctly.


---


**2. `POST /v1/tick`**
Purpose: judge wakes your bot up and asks, “based on current context, do you want to proactively message anyone now?”


Input:
```json
{
  "now": "2026-04-26T10:30:00Z",
  "available_triggers": ["trg_1", "trg_2"]
}
```


Expected output:
```json
{
  "actions": [
    {
      "conversation_id": "conv_001",
      "merchant_id": "m_001_drmeera",
      "customer_id": null,
      "send_as": "vera",
      "trigger_id": "trg_2026_04_26_research_digest",
      "template_name": "vera_research_digest_v1",
      "template_params": ["Dr. Meera", "JIDA Oct issue", "..."],
      "body": "Dr. Meera, JIDA's Oct issue landed...",
      "cta": "open_ended",
      "suppression_key": "research:dentists:2026-W17",
      "rationale": "why you are sending this"
    }
  ]
}
```


Can also return:
```json
{
  "actions": []
}
```


Expected behavior:
- inspect current stored context
- look at active triggers
- decide whether anything is worth sending
- return zero or more proactive message actions
- must return within 30s


**Sense of this endpoint**
This is the proactive messaging brain.  
The judge is checking whether your bot can decide:
- should I send something?
- to whom?
- because of which trigger?
- with what exact message?


---


**3. `POST /v1/reply`**
Purpose: judge sends a merchant/customer reply to one of your earlier messages and asks what your next move is.


Input:
```json
{
  "conversation_id": "conv_001",
  "merchant_id": "m_001_drmeera",
  "customer_id": null,
  "from_role": "merchant",
  "message": "Yes, send me the abstract",
  "received_at": "2026-04-26T10:45:00Z",
  "turn_number": 2
}
```


Expected output must be one of 3 types:


Send next message:
```json
{
  "action": "send",
  "body": "Sending now — also drafted a 90-sec patient-ed WhatsApp...",
  "cta": "open_ended",
  "rationale": "why this is the next best response"
}
```


Wait:
```json
{
  "action": "wait",
  "wait_seconds": 1800,
  "rationale": "Merchant asked for time; back off"
}
```


End conversation:
```json
{
  "action": "end",
  "rationale": "Merchant not interested; gracefully exiting"
}
```


Expected behavior:
- use conversation history/state
- interpret merchant intent
- handle auto-replies, interest, rejection, questions, hostility
- return the next move synchronously within 30s


**Sense of this endpoint**
This is the conversation-handling brain.  
The judge is testing whether your bot can continue a real chat, not just send one nice first message.


---


**4. `GET /v1/healthz`**
Purpose: liveness check.


Expected output:
```json
{
  "status": "ok",
  "uptime_seconds": 3600,
  "contexts_loaded": {
    "category": 5,
    "merchant": 50,
    "customer": 200,
    "trigger": 100
  }
}
```


Expected behavior:
- return 200
- show service is alive
- show how many contexts are currently loaded


**Sense of this endpoint**
This is just operational health.  
The judge uses it to ensure your service is up and actually storing context.


---


**5. `GET /v1/metadata`**
Purpose: bot identity / submission info.


Expected output:
```json
{
  "team_name": "Team Alpha",
  "team_members": ["Alice", "Bob"],
  "model": "claude-opus-4-7",
  "approach": "single-prompt composer with retrieval over digest items",
  "contact_email": "team@example.com",
  "version": "1.2.0",
  "submitted_at": "2026-04-26T08:00:00Z"
}
```


**Sense of this endpoint**
This is informational only.  
It tells the judge who submitted the bot and what model/approach is being used.


---


**Overall endpoint behavior they want**


- `/v1/context`
  - bot should behave like a **stateful context store**


- `/v1/tick`
  - bot should behave like a **proactive campaign/engagement engine**


- `/v1/reply`
  - bot should behave like a **smart conversation manager**


- `/v1/healthz`
  - bot should behave like a **reliable service**


- `/v1/metadata`
  - bot should behave like a **submission identity card**


**In one line**
They want a bot that can:
- remember pushed context,
- decide when to initiate a message,
- continue the conversation intelligently,
- and stay operationally reliable.

**Core Vera logic**

"""
Vera Sales Agent


Orchestration-driven sales agent for converting merchants into Vera subscribers.
Uses direct vera-mcp tools for GBP data — no specialist indirection.


5-State Architecture:
- unassociated: No GBP linked — pitch onboarding
- associated-non-paying: GBP linked, no subscription — demo capabilities
- associated-paying: Active trial or subscription — do work, retain
- associated-expired-payment: Payment lapsed — show missed opportunities
- churned: Declined 5x or cancelled — gentle winback


State stored in Redis: vera:sales:{merchant_id} (90-day TTL)


Architecture:
- State detection via vera-mcp (gbp_resolve_merchant + vera_get_subscription_status)
- Orchestrator pre-fetches data per state BEFORE LLM runs
- LLM gets pre-fetched data in system prompt → crafts sales pitches
- State-aware tool filtering: only tools relevant to current state are exposed
"""


import os
import re
import json
import asyncio
import logging
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from datetime import datetime


from employee_agents.base.employee_agent import EmployeeAgent
from agents.vera.sales_prompts import get_vera_sales_prompt, DEFAULT_PRICING
from utility.http_mcp_client import HTTPMCPClient
from utility.message_protocol import MessageProtocol
from utility.metrics import increment_tool_call
from utility.redis_config import get_redis_client
from utility.constants import DEFAULT_VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL


try:
    from tools.merchant_utilities import get_merchant_details
except ImportError:
    get_merchant_details = None


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


WRITE_CLAIM_PATTERNS = [
    r"\bho gaya\b",
    r"\bdone\b",
    r"\bposted\b",
    r"\bpublished\b",
    r"publish kar (rahi|diya|dungi)",
    r"post kar (rahi|diya|dungi)",
    r"reply (kar rahi|post kar rahi|post kar diya|daal rahi|dal rahi)",
]




# ─── Constants ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────




# Language configuration per region
REGION_LANGUAGE = {
    "IN": "hinglish",
    "DEFAULT": "english",
}




# ─── 5-State Model ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────


class State:
    UNASSOCIATED = "unassociated"
    ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING = "associated-non-paying"
    ASSOCIATED_PAYING = "associated-paying"
    ASSOCIATED_EXPIRED_PAYMENT = "associated-expired-payment"
    CHURNED = "churned"




# Legacy 7-state → new 5-state migration map
LEGACY_STATE_MAP = {
    "UNASSOCIATED": "unassociated",
    "ONBOARDING_PENDING": "unassociated",
    "ONBOARDING_COMPLETE": "associated-non-paying",
    "TRIAL_ACTIVE": "associated-paying",
    "SUBSCRIPTION_ACTIVE": "associated-paying",
    "SUBSCRIPTION_EXPIRED": "associated-expired-payment",
    "CHURNED": "churned",
}

class VeraSalesAgent(EmployeeAgent):
    """
    Vera Sales Agent — orchestration-driven merchant sales lifecycle.


    Key design:
    - _detect_state() calls vera-mcp live (cached 1hr in Redis) to determine merchant state
    - Orchestrator pre-fetches all data the LLM needs for the current state
    - get_tools() exposes only state-appropriate tools
    - _handle_tool_call() enforces state-based tool access
    """


    agent_type = "VeraSalesAgent"
    MAX_AGENT_ITERATIONS = 5


    # Direct vera-mcp tools for sales (focused subset)
    VERA_SALES_MCP_TOOLS = [
        # GBP Connection & Onboarding
        "gbp_resolve_merchant",
        "gbp_get_onboarding_url",
        "gbp_check_merchant_access",
        "gbp_check_onboarding_status",
        # Unassociated merchant data (public GBP health report)
        "get_unassociated_merchant_data",
        "get_aggregated_unassociated_merchant_data",
        # Reviews (strongest sales lever)
        "gbp_list_reviews",
        "gbp_get_review",
        "gbp_get_review_stats",
        "gbp_reply_to_review",
        "gbp_generate_review_reply",
        # Profile & Insights
        "gbp_get_profile_completeness",
        "gbp_get_insights",
        "gbp_get_performance_summary",
        "gbp_get_search_keywords",
        # Posts
        "gbp_create_post",
        # Banners
        "vera_list_banner_templates",
        "vera_get_banner_options",
        "vera_generate_banner",
        "vera_store_merchant_banner",
        "vera_list_merchant_banners",
        "vera_delete_merchant_banner",
        # Subscription
        "vera_get_subscription_status",
        "vera_create_subscription",
        # Payment
        "vera_create_payment_link",
        "vera_check_payment_status",
        "vera_get_dashboard_login",
        # Offers
        "vera_get_applicable_offers",
        "vera_store_offer",
        "vera_update_offer",
        "vera_deactivate_offer",
        "vera_get_merchant_offer",
        "vera_list_merchant_offers",
        "vera_pause_offer",
        "vera_resume_offer",
        # Publish offer approved in chat (tracks in MongoDB + updates weekly pipeline)
        "vera_publish_offer_from_chat",
        # Unassociated merchant tools (public GBP data + health report card)
        "create_gbp_profile_summary",
        "get_unassociated_merchant_data",
        "get_aggregated_unassociated_merchant_data",
    ]


    # Focused tool groups for topic-based narrowing
    REVIEW_FOCUS_TOOLS = {
        "gbp_list_reviews",
        "gbp_get_review",
        "gbp_get_review_stats",
        "gbp_generate_review_reply",

        "gbp_get_insights",

    }
    POST_FOCUS_TOOLS = {
        "gbp_create_post",
        "gbp_get_performance_summary",
        "gbp_get_search_keywords",
        "gbp_get_insights",
    }
    BANNER_FOCUS_TOOLS = {
        "vera_list_banner_templates",
        "vera_get_banner_options",
        "vera_generate_banner",
        "vera_store_merchant_banner",
        "vera_list_merchant_banners",
        "vera_delete_merchant_banner",
    }
    PAYMENT_FOCUS_TOOLS = {
        "vera_create_payment_link",
        "vera_check_payment_status",
        "vera_get_dashboard_login",
        "vera_get_applicable_offers",
        "vera_store_offer",
        "vera_update_offer",
        "vera_deactivate_offer",
        "vera_get_merchant_offer",
        "vera_list_merchant_offers",
        "vera_pause_offer",
        "vera_resume_offer",
    }
    TOPIC_DEFAULT = "reviews"


    # Merchant-support MCP tools allowed for this agent
    MERCHANT_MCP_ALLOWED_TOOLS = [
        "get_top_merchants_by_locality",
        "get_delivery_stats_by_locality",
    ]


    # Redis key prefix and TTL
    REDIS_KEY_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:"
    REDIS_TTL_DAYS = 90


    # Redis-backed free write tracking — counted across ALL states, blocked only in non-paying
    REDIS_WRITE_KEY_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:writes:"
    REDIS_WRITE_TTL_SECONDS = 2 * 86400  # 2 days
    REDIS_WRITE_MAX = 1
    REDIS_HEALTH_REPORT_PREFIX = "vera:health_report:"
    REDIS_HEALTH_CARD_PREFIX = "vera:health_card:"
    REDIS_HEALTH_TTL_SECONDS = 6 * 3600  # 6 hours


    # All tools that modify GBP data, create content, or store records
    WRITE_TOOLS = {
        # Reviews

        "gbp_update_categories", "gbp_update_attributes",
        # Photo pipeline
        "vera_process_photo_batch",
        # Place actions
        "gbp_create_place_action", "gbp_update_place_action", "gbp_delete_place_action",
        # Food menus
        "gbp_update_food_menus",

        "vera_generate_banner", "vera_store_merchant_banner", "vera_delete_merchant_banner",
        # Offers
        "vera_store_offer", "vera_update_offer", "vera_deactivate_offer",
        "vera_pause_offer", "vera_resume_offer",
    }


    # Redis-backed payment tracking
    REDIS_PAYMENT_KEY_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:payment:"
    REDIS_PAYMENT_TTL_SECONDS = 1 * 86400  # 1 day


    def __init__(self, agent_id: str):
        # Follow VeraManager init pattern exactly:
        from agents.base_agent import BaseAgent
        from employee_agents.base.agent_memory import AgentMemory
        BaseAgent.__init__(self, agent_id)


        # EmployeeAgent attributes (same as VeraManager)
        self._chat_client = None
        self._sop_config = None
        self._mcp_client = None
        self._bq_execution_count = 0
        self.memory = AgentMemory(agent_id)
        self._query_start_time = None
        self.PROGRESS_UPDATE_ENABLED = False


        # Anti-repetition guards
        self._sent_messages = set()
        self._iteration_count = 0


        # Direct vera-mcp client — NO VeraManager specialist indirection
        vera_mcp_url = os.getenv('VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL', DEFAULT_VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL)
        self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Connecting to vera-mcp at: {vera_mcp_url}")
        self.vera_mcp_client = HTTPMCPClient(
            server_url=vera_mcp_url,
            tool_prefix="",
            timeout=30
        )
        self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = None


        # Redis client for state management
        self._redis = get_redis_client()


        # Region/language config (can be overridden per-request via metadata)
        self._region = "IN"
        self._language = REGION_LANGUAGE.get(self._region, "english")
        self._pricing = DEFAULT_PRICING
        self._pricing_cache: Dict[str, Any] = {}


        # Orchestration state (set before each LLM call)
        self._current_state = State.UNASSOCIATED
        self._orchestration_data = {}


        self.logger.info("VeraSalesAgent initialized")
        increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "initialization", "success")


    # ─── MCP Response Parsing ────────────────────────────────────────


    @staticmethod
    def _parse_mcp_result(result) -> Any:
        """
        Extract actual data from HTTPMCPClient.call_tool() response.


        call_tool() returns {"status": "success", "data": "<json string or raw>"} or
        {"status": "error", "error": "..."}.  The vera-mcp server ALSO wraps its
        responses in {"status": "success", "data": {...}}, so responses are often
        double-wrapped.  This method recursively unwraps until it reaches the
        actual payload.
        """
        if not isinstance(result, dict):
            return result
        if result.get("status") == "error":
            return None
        data = result.get("data", result)
        if isinstance(data, str):
            try:
                data = json.loads(data)
            except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
                return data
        # Recursively unwrap if data is itself a {"status": "success", "data": ...} wrapper
        if isinstance(data, dict) and "data" in data and "status" in data:
            return VeraSalesAgent._parse_mcp_result(data)
        return data


    @classmethod
    def _get_tool_execution_status(cls, tool_result: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        """
        Derive the semantic tool outcome, not just the transport wrapper status.


        vera-mcp tools often return a JSON string payload such as
        {"status":"error", ...} inside an outer {"status":"success","data":"..."}
        envelope. Treating the outer status as authoritative causes false
        "reply posted" confirmations for failed writes.
        """
        payload = tool_result.get("result", {}) if isinstance(tool_result, dict) else {}
        if not isinstance(payload, dict):
            return ""


        transport_status = str(payload.get("status", "")).strip().lower()
        if transport_status in {"error", "blocked", "skipped"}:
            return transport_status
        if transport_status in {"success", "completed"}:
            parsed = cls._parse_mcp_result(payload)
            if isinstance(parsed, dict):
                parsed_status = str(parsed.get("status", "")).strip().lower()
                if parsed_status in {"error", "failed", "failure"}:
                    return "error"
                if parsed_status in {"blocked", "skipped"}:
                    return parsed_status
                if parsed_status in {"success", "completed"}:
                    return "success"
            return "success"
        return transport_status


    @classmethod
    def _tool_result_succeeded(cls, tool_result: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """Return True only when the tool payload itself reports success."""
        return cls._get_tool_execution_status(tool_result) == "success"


    # ─── MCP Tool Management ──────────────────────────────────────────


    async def _fetch_pricing(self, region: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Fetch pricing for the given region from vera-mcp. Falls back to DEFAULT_PRICING on error.


        Cached per region for the agent's lifetime — same pattern as _prefetch_mcp_tools.
        """
        if region in self._pricing_cache:
            return self._pricing_cache[region]
        try:
            raw = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("vera_get_pricing", {"country_code": region})
            data = self._parse_mcp_result(raw)
            plans_list = data.get("plans", [])
            result = {
                "trial_price": data.get("trial_amount"),
                "currency_symbol": data.get("currency_symbol", DEFAULT_PRICING["currency_symbol"]),
                "plans": {p["id"]: p["numeric_price"] for p in plans_list},
            }
            self._pricing_cache[region] = result
            return result
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning("[VeraSalesAgent] _fetch_pricing failed (%s), using default", exc)
            return DEFAULT_PRICING


    async def _prefetch_mcp_tools(self):
        """Pre-fetch vera-mcp tools. Must be called before get_tools()."""
        if self._vera_mcp_tools_cache is not None:
            return
        try:
            await self.vera_mcp_client.get_tools()
            self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = self.vera_mcp_client.filter_allowed_tools(
                self.VERA_SALES_MCP_TOOLS
            )
            self.logger.info(
                f"[VeraSalesAgent] Discovered {len(self._vera_mcp_tools_cache)} sales MCP tools"
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Failed to discover vera-mcp tools: {e}")
            self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = []


    def get_tools(self) -> list:
        """Build tool list from scratch — state-aware, Vera persona. Never calls super()."""
        # Vera's communicate_to_user (NOT Ayushi)
        tools = [
            {
                "type": "function",
                "name": "communicate_to_user",
                "description": (
                    "Send a message to the merchant. You are Priya — a sharp, confident salesgirl from magicpin "
                    "who sells Vera (Google Business Profile management product). Use natural Hinglish (or English based on region), "
                    "feminine forms, short punchy messages. MAX 3-4 lines for WhatsApp. "
                    "Use *bold* for key numbers. Always set all_concerns_answered=true."
                ),
                "parameters": {
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "message": {"type": "string", "description": "The message to send to the merchant"},
                        "metadata": {
                            "type": "object",
                            "properties": {
                                "agent_id": {"type": "string"},
                                "conversation_id": {"type": "string"},
                            },
                        },
                        "media": {
                            "type": "object",
                            "description": "Optional media payload (image/video/document).",
                            "properties": {
                                "type": {"type": "string"},
                                "url": {"type": "string"},
                                "caption": {"type": "string"},
                            },
                        },
                        "all_concerns_answered": {
                            "type": "boolean",
                            "description": "Always set to true for Vera sales messages.",
                        },
                    },
                    "required": ["message", "all_concerns_answered"],
                },
            }
        ]


        # Get current state's allowed tools
        state = getattr(self, '_current_state', State.UNASSOCIATED)
        config = STATE_CONFIG.get(state, STATE_CONFIG[State.UNASSOCIATED])
        allowed_vera_tools = set(config["available_tools"]) - {"communicate_to_user"}


        # Narrow tools based on current topic to reduce LLM confusion.
        # Default to reviews for associated-non-paying unless merchant explicitly asks for another capability.
        current_topic = ""
        if hasattr(self, "_current_state") and state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING:
            current_topic = self._resolve_active_topic(
                (getattr(self, 'current_metadata', None) or {}).get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id", "")
            )


        if current_topic == "reviews":
            allowed_vera_tools = allowed_vera_tools & (self.REVIEW_FOCUS_TOOLS | self.PAYMENT_FOCUS_TOOLS)
        elif current_topic == "posts":
            allowed_vera_tools = allowed_vera_tools & (self.POST_FOCUS_TOOLS | self.PAYMENT_FOCUS_TOOLS)
        elif current_topic == "banners":
            allowed_vera_tools = allowed_vera_tools & (self.BANNER_FOCUS_TOOLS | self.PAYMENT_FOCUS_TOOLS)


        # If free write already exhausted (non-paying), remove write tools from list
        free_write_exhausted = getattr(self, "_merchant_sub_state", "") == "free_write_used"
        if free_write_exhausted and state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING:
            allowed_vera_tools = allowed_vera_tools - set(self.WRITE_TOOLS)


        # Add vera-mcp tools filtered by state
        if self._vera_mcp_tools_cache:
            for tool in self._vera_mcp_tools_cache:
                if tool.get("name") in allowed_vera_tools:
                    tools.append(tool)


        # Add introduce_vera_if_not_done_already tool for associated-non-paying
        if state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING:
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Adding introduce_vera_if_not_done_already tool for state=%s", state)
            tools.append({
                "type": "function",
                "name": "introduce_vera_if_not_done_already",
                "description": "Check if Priya (you) has introduced herself and Vera (the product) to this merchant. Call this FIRST before any other action. If not introduced, introduce yourself as Priya from magicpin selling Vera. If already introduced, proceed to capability demo.",
                "parameters": {
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "merchant_id": {"type": "string", "description": "The merchant ID"},
                    },
                    "required": ["merchant_id"],
                },
            })


        # Add merchant-mcp tools per state config
        merchant_mcp_tools = config.get("merchant_mcp_tools", [])
        if merchant_mcp_tools and self._get_merchant_mcp_tools():
            allowed_merchant = set(merchant_mcp_tools)
            for tool in self._get_merchant_mcp_tools():
                if tool.get("name") in allowed_merchant:
                    tools.append(tool)


        # [LOG #1] Tool list sent to LLM
        mid = (getattr(self, 'current_metadata', None) or {}).get('context_data', {}).get('merchant_id', 'unknown')
        tool_names = [t.get('name', '?') for t in tools]
        self.logger.info(f"[VERA_TOOLS] mid={mid} state={state} tools=[{', '.join(tool_names)}] count={len(tools)}")


        return tools


    @staticmethod
    def _extract_draft_text(draft_payload: Any) -> str:
        """Extract the usable reply draft text from an MCP payload."""
        if not draft_payload:
            return ""
        if isinstance(draft_payload, str):
            return draft_payload
        if isinstance(draft_payload, dict):
            for key in ("draft_reply", "draft", "reply_text", "text"):
                value = draft_payload.get(key)
                if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip():
                    return value.strip()
            data = draft_payload.get("data")
            if isinstance(data, dict):
                return VeraSalesAgent._extract_draft_text(data)
        return ""


    def _resolve_active_topic(self, merchant_id: str) -> str:
        """Choose the active topic with a deterministic review-first default."""
        state_data = self._get_merchant_state(str(merchant_id)) or {}
        current_topic = state_data.get("current_topic", "")
        if current_topic:
            return current_topic


        return self.TOPIC_DEFAULT


    @staticmethod
    def _claims_write_completion(message: str) -> bool:
        """Detect text that implies a write already happened or is underway."""
        if not message:
            return False
        lowered = message.lower()
        return any(re.search(pattern, lowered) for pattern in WRITE_CLAIM_PATTERNS)


    # ─── Redis State Management ───────────────────────────────────────


    def _get_redis_key(self, merchant_id: str) -> str:
        """Build Redis key for merchant sales state."""
        return f"{self.REDIS_KEY_PREFIX}{merchant_id}"


    def _get_cached_json(self, key: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        """Fetch cached JSON from Redis, if present."""
        try:
            raw = self._redis.get(key)
            if not raw:
                return None
            if isinstance(raw, bytes):
                raw = raw.decode("utf-8")
            return json.loads(raw)
        except Exception:
            return None


    def _set_cached_json(self, key: str, payload: dict, ttl: int) -> None:
        """Store JSON payload in Redis with TTL."""
        try:
            self._redis.setex(key, ttl, json.dumps(payload))
        except Exception:
            pass


    def _get_merchant_state(self, merchant_id: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Get merchant sales state from Redis."""
        try:
            data = self._redis.get(self._get_redis_key(merchant_id))
            if data:
                return json.loads(data)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Redis get failed: {e}")
        return None


    def _set_merchant_state(self, merchant_id: str, state_data: Dict):
        """Set merchant sales state in Redis with 90-day TTL."""
        try:
            key = self._get_redis_key(merchant_id)
            state_data["updated_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self._redis.setex(
                key,
                self.REDIS_TTL_DAYS * 86400,
                json.dumps(state_data)
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Redis set failed: {e}")


    # ─── Free Write Tracking (Redis-backed) ─────────────────────────────


    def _get_write_count(self, merchant_id: str) -> int:
        """Get the number of write actions used by this merchant from Redis."""
        try:
            val = self._redis.get(f"{self.REDIS_WRITE_KEY_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            return int(val) if val else 0
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Redis get write count failed: {e}")
            return 0


    def _increment_write_count(self, merchant_id: str):
        """Increment write count in Redis with 2-day TTL via pipeline."""
        try:
            key = f"{self.REDIS_WRITE_KEY_PREFIX}{merchant_id}"
            pipe = self._redis.pipeline()
            pipe.incr(key)
            pipe.expire(key, self.REDIS_WRITE_TTL_SECONDS)
            pipe.execute()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Redis incr write count failed: {e}")


    # ─── Payment Tracking (Redis-backed, 1-day TTL) ─────────────────────


    def _get_payment_data(self, merchant_id: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """Get stored payment data (link, txn_id) from Redis."""
        try:
            data = self._redis.get(f"{self.REDIS_PAYMENT_KEY_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            if data:
                return json.loads(data)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Redis get payment data failed: {e}")
        return None


    def _set_payment_data(self, merchant_id: str, payment_data: Dict):
        """Store payment data in Redis with 1-day TTL."""
        try:
            key = f"{self.REDIS_PAYMENT_KEY_PREFIX}{merchant_id}"
            payment_data["updated_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self._redis.setex(
                key,
                self.REDIS_PAYMENT_TTL_SECONDS,
                json.dumps(payment_data),
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Redis set payment data failed: {e}")


    # ─── State Trace Logging (MongoDB via vera-mcp) ─────────────────




    # ─── State Detection (async, MCP-backed, Redis-cached 1hr) ────────


    async def _detect_state(self, merchant_id: str) -> dict:
        """
        Detect merchant state by calling vera-mcp live, cached in Redis (1hr).
        Returns dict with 'state', 'place_id', 'has_gbp', 'subscription_status', 'decline_count'.
        """
        import time as _time
        t0 = _time.monotonic()
        self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=detect_state merchant_id={merchant_id} status=started")


        # Check Redis cache first
        cached = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id)
        if cached:
            raw_state = cached.get("state", "")
            # Legacy migration: convert UPPERCASE states to kebab-case
            if raw_state in LEGACY_STATE_MAP:
                new_state = LEGACY_STATE_MAP[raw_state]
                cached["state"] = new_state
                cached["legacy_migrated_from"] = raw_state
                self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, cached)
                self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Migrated legacy state: {raw_state} -> {new_state}")


            # Check if detection data is fresh (< 1 hour)
            detection_ts = cached.get("detection_ts")
            if detection_ts:
                try:
                    dt = datetime.fromisoformat(detection_ts)
                    age_seconds = (datetime.now() - dt).total_seconds()
                    if age_seconds < 3600:  # 1 hour cache
                        self.logger.info(
                            f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=detect_state merchant_id={merchant_id} status=cache_hit "
                            f"state={cached.get('state')} age_seconds={int(age_seconds)} "
                            f"has_gbp={cached.get('has_gbp')} decline_count={cached.get('decline_count', 0)}"
                        )
                        return cached
                except (ValueError, TypeError):
                    pass


        # Call vera-mcp to detect state live
        detection_data = {"state": State.UNASSOCIATED, "decline_count": (cached or {}).get("decline_count", 0)}


        try:
            # Check decline count first
            decline_count = detection_data["decline_count"]
            if decline_count >= 5:
                detection_data["state"] = State.CHURNED
                detection_data["detection_ts"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
                self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, {**(cached or {}), **detection_data})
                return detection_data


            # Call gbp_resolve_merchant
            raw_resolve = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_resolve_merchant", {"merchant_id": merchant_id})
            resolve_result = self._parse_mcp_result(raw_resolve)
            has_gbp = False
            place_id = ""
            location_name = ""
            if isinstance(resolve_result, dict):
                place_id = resolve_result.get("place_id", "")
                location_name = resolve_result.get("location_name") or ""
                # has_gbp = True only when we have a location_name (managed by mxconnect).
                # A bare place_id (access_type=public) means we know the Google listing
                # but do NOT have management access — merchant needs OAuth first.
                has_gbp = bool(location_name)
            elif isinstance(resolve_result, str):
                if "location_name" in resolve_result:
                    has_gbp = True


            detection_data["has_gbp"] = has_gbp
            detection_data["place_id"] = place_id
            detection_data["location_name"] = location_name


            if not has_gbp:
                detection_data["state"] = State.UNASSOCIATED
            else:
                # Has GBP — check subscription
                try:
                    raw_sub = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("vera_get_subscription_status", {"merchant_id": merchant_id})
                    sub_data = self._parse_mcp_result(raw_sub)
                    sub_status = ""
                    if isinstance(sub_data, dict):
                        sub_status = sub_data.get("status", "").lower()
                    elif isinstance(sub_data, str):
                        sub_lower = sub_data.lower()
                        for s in ["trial_active", "active", "expired", "cancelled"]:
                            if s in sub_lower:
                                sub_status = s
                                break


                    detection_data["subscription_status"] = sub_status


                    if sub_status in ("active", "trial_active"):
                        detection_data["state"] = State.ASSOCIATED_PAYING
                    elif sub_status == "expired":
                        detection_data["state"] = State.ASSOCIATED_EXPIRED_PAYMENT
                    elif sub_status == "cancelled":
                        detection_data["state"] = State.CHURNED
                    else:
                        detection_data["state"] = State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Subscription check failed: {e}")
                    detection_data["state"] = State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING


            detection_data["detection_ts"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            # Merge with existing cached data to preserve decline_count etc.
            merged = {**(cached or {}), **detection_data}
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, merged)
            duration_ms = int((_time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
            self.logger.info(
                f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=detect_state merchant_id={merchant_id} status=success "
                f"state={detection_data.get('state')} has_gbp={detection_data.get('has_gbp')} "
                f"place_id={detection_data.get('place_id', '')} location_name={detection_data.get('location_name', '')} "
                f"subscription={detection_data.get('subscription_status', '')} decline_count={detection_data.get('decline_count', 0)} "
                f"source=live duration_ms={duration_ms}"
            )




            return merged


        except Exception as e:
            duration_ms = int((_time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=detect_state merchant_id={merchant_id} status=exception error={e} duration_ms={duration_ms}")
            # Fall back to cached state or default
            if cached:
                return cached
            detection_data["detection_ts"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, detection_data)
            return detection_data


    # ─── Orchestrator Methods ─────────────────────────────────────────


    # OAuth redirect message patterns for state detection.
    # IMPORTANT: Must match EVERY _wa_redirect() message in vera-mcp/src/oauth.py.
    # All matching is case-insensitive (msg.lower()).
    OAUTH_SUCCESS_PATTERNS = [
        "i have provided google profile access",  # New access granted
        "google profile is connected with you",   # Already connected
    ]


    OAUTH_FAILURE_PATTERNS = [
        # _get_invite_error_message() outputs:
        "don't have owner access",                # 403 PERMISSION_DENIED
        "listing was not found on google",        # 404 NOT_FOUND
        "google is busy right now",               # 429 RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED
        "there was an error from google",         # 500 INTERNAL
        "access setup failed",                    # Default fallback
        # Token exchange / account listing errors:
        "error connecting to google",             # Token exchange failed
        "issue with google login",                # Google returned non-access_denied error
        "no business profile found",              # No accounts found
        "profiles could not be loaded",           # Account listing exception
        "no business location found",             # No locations found
        "location could not be selected",         # Invalid picker selection
        # Consent screen errors:
        "access was denied",                      # access_denied (user clicked Deny)
    ]


    def _detect_oauth_redirect_message(self, message: str) -> str:
        """Detect OAuth redirect WhatsApp messages and return type: 'success', 'already_connected', 'failure', or ''."""
        if not message:
            return ""
        msg_lower = message.lower()
        if "pehle se connected hai" in msg_lower:
            return "already_connected"
        for p in self.OAUTH_SUCCESS_PATTERNS:
            if p in msg_lower:
                return "success"
        for p in self.OAUTH_FAILURE_PATTERNS:
            if p in msg_lower:
                return "failure"
        return ""


    async def _orchestrate_introduction(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> dict:
        """Pre-fetch for unassociated: onboarding URL + cached health data (for speed)."""
        import time as _time
        t0 = _time.monotonic()
        self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=orchestrate_introduction merchant_id={merchant_id} status=started")


        async def _fetch_onboarding_url():
            try:
                raw = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                    "gbp_get_onboarding_url", {"merchant_id": merchant_id}
                )
                return self._parse_mcp_result(raw)
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=fetch_onboarding_url merchant_id={merchant_id} status=failed error={e}")
                return None


        onboarding_url = await _fetch_onboarding_url()


        # Fetch health report (cached in Redis for fast reuse)
        health_report = self._get_cached_json(f"{self.REDIS_HEALTH_REPORT_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
        if not health_report:
            try:
                raw = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                    "get_aggregated_unassociated_merchant_data", {"merchant_id": merchant_id}
                )
                health_report = self._parse_mcp_result(raw)
                if isinstance(health_report, dict):
                    self._set_cached_json(f"{self.REDIS_HEALTH_REPORT_PREFIX}{merchant_id}", health_report, self.REDIS_HEALTH_TTL_SECONDS)
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=fetch_health_report merchant_id={merchant_id} status=failed error={e}")
                health_report = None


        # Fetch health card (cached in Redis for fast reuse)
        health_summary = self._get_cached_json(f"{self.REDIS_HEALTH_CARD_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
        if not health_summary:
            try:
                raw = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                    "create_gbp_profile_summary", {"merchant_id": str(merchant_id)}
                )
                health_summary = self._parse_mcp_result(raw)
                if isinstance(health_summary, dict):
                    self._set_cached_json(f"{self.REDIS_HEALTH_CARD_PREFIX}{merchant_id}", health_summary, self.REDIS_HEALTH_TTL_SECONDS)
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=fetch_health_card merchant_id={merchant_id} status=failed error={e}")
                health_summary = None


        duration_ms = int((_time.monotonic() - t0) * 1000)
        self.logger.info(
            f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=orchestrate_introduction merchant_id={merchant_id} status=done "
            f"has_onboarding_url={onboarding_url is not None} duration_ms={duration_ms}"
        )


        return {
            "onboarding_url": onboarding_url,
            "health_report": health_report,
            "health_summary": health_summary,
        }


    def _get_gbp_args(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> dict:
        """Build args for GBP tools: prefer location_name, fallback to merchant_id."""
        location_name = detection_data.get("location_name", "")
        if location_name:
            return {"location_name": location_name}
        return {"merchant_id": merchant_id}


    async def _show_review_capability(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> Optional[dict]:
        """Demo: fetch recent reviews + latest unanswered review + draft reply."""
        try:
            gbp_args = self._get_gbp_args(merchant_id, detection_data)
            raw_reviews = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_list_reviews", gbp_args)
            parsed_data = self._parse_mcp_result(raw_reviews)
            # Parse reviews to find unanswered ones
            reviews = []
            if isinstance(parsed_data, list):
                reviews = parsed_data
            elif isinstance(parsed_data, dict):
                reviews = parsed_data.get("reviews", [parsed_data])


            # Find unanswered review (check both "reply" and "reviewReply" — Google API uses reviewReply)
            unanswered = [
                r for r in reviews
                if isinstance(r, dict) and not r.get("reply") and not r.get("reviewReply")
            ]


            result = {
                "total_reviews": len(reviews),
                "unanswered_count": len(unanswered),
                "recent_reviews": reviews[:15],
                "latest_unanswered": None,
                "draft_reply": None,
                "review_stats": None,
            }


            if unanswered:
                latest = unanswered[0]
                result["latest_unanswered"] = latest


                # Generate draft reply — needs review_text (str) and rating (int)
                review_text = latest.get("comment", latest.get("text", ""))
                star_rating_raw = latest.get("starRating", latest.get("rating", ""))
                review_id = latest.get("review_id") or latest.get("reviewId") or latest.get("name")
                # Convert Google API star ratings ("ONE"..."FIVE") to int
                _star_map = {"ONE": 1, "TWO": 2, "THREE": 3, "FOUR": 4, "FIVE": 5}
                if isinstance(star_rating_raw, str) and star_rating_raw in _star_map:
                    star_rating = _star_map[star_rating_raw]
                else:
                    try:
                        star_rating = int(star_rating_raw) if star_rating_raw else 0
                    except (ValueError, TypeError):
                        star_rating = 0
                if star_rating > 0:
                    try:
                        draft_args = {
                            "review_text": review_text or "(no text, rating only)",
                            "rating": star_rating,
                            "merchant_name": self._extract_merchant_name(),
                            "reviewer_name": latest.get("reviewer", {}).get("displayName", latest.get("reviewer_name", "")),
                        }
                        raw_draft = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_generate_review_reply", draft_args)
                        result["draft_reply"] = self._parse_mcp_result(raw_draft)
                        # Draft generated — included in orchestration data for prompt
                    except Exception as e:
                        self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Draft reply generation failed: {e}")


            # Also get review stats
            try:
                raw_stats = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_get_review_stats", gbp_args)
                result["review_stats"] = self._parse_mcp_result(raw_stats)
            except Exception:
                pass


            return result
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Review capability fetch failed: {e}")
            return None


    def _extract_merchant_name(self) -> str:
        """Best-effort merchant name for draft generation and prompt context."""
        context_data = (getattr(self, "current_metadata", None) or {}).get("context_data", {})
        merchant_data = context_data.get("merchant_data") or {}
        if isinstance(merchant_data, dict):
            name = (
                merchant_data.get("merchantName")
                or merchant_data.get("merchant_name")
                or merchant_data.get("name")
            )
            if name:
                return str(name)
        return ""


    async def _show_post_capability(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> Optional[dict]:
        """Demo: fetch performance data for post suggestion."""
        try:
            gbp_args = self._get_gbp_args(merchant_id, detection_data)
            raw_perf = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_get_performance_summary", gbp_args)
            return {"performance_summary": self._parse_mcp_result(raw_perf)}
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Post capability fetch failed: {e}")
            return None


    async def _show_banner_capability(self, merchant_id: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        """Demo: fetch available banner templates for this merchant's category."""
        try:
            raw = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("vera_get_banner_options", {"merchant_id": str(merchant_id)})
            return self._parse_mcp_result(raw)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Banner capability fetch failed: {e}")
            return None


    async def _orchestrate_show_capability(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> dict:
        """Pre-fetch for associated-non-paying: parallel capability demos."""
        place_id = detection_data.get("place_id", "")
        location_name = detection_data.get("location_name", "")


        review_data, post_data, locality_data, banner_data = await asyncio.gather(
            self._show_review_capability(merchant_id, detection_data),
            self._show_post_capability(merchant_id, detection_data),
            self._fetch_locality_data(merchant_id),
            self._show_banner_capability(merchant_id),
            return_exceptions=True,
        )


        return {
            "review_capability": review_data if not isinstance(review_data, Exception) else None,
            "post_capability": post_data if not isinstance(post_data, Exception) else None,
            "locality_data": locality_data if not isinstance(locality_data, Exception) else None,
            "banner_capability": banner_data if not isinstance(banner_data, Exception) else None,
            "google_maps_review_url": self._build_google_maps_review_url(place_id),
            "location_name": location_name,
        }


    async def _orchestrate_do_work(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> dict:
        """Pre-fetch for associated-paying: review stats + performance + current offer."""
        gbp_args = self._get_gbp_args(merchant_id, detection_data)
        location_name = detection_data.get("location_name", "")
        raw_stats = None
        raw_perf = None
        raw_offer = None
        try:
            raw_stats, raw_perf, raw_offer = await asyncio.gather(
                self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_get_review_stats", gbp_args),
                self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_get_performance_summary", gbp_args),
                self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("vera_get_merchant_offer", {"merchant_id": merchant_id}),
                return_exceptions=True,
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Do-work orchestration failed: {e}")


        return {
            "review_stats": self._parse_mcp_result(raw_stats) if not isinstance(raw_stats, (Exception, type(None))) else None,
            "performance_summary": self._parse_mcp_result(raw_perf) if not isinstance(raw_perf, (Exception, type(None))) else None,
            "current_offer": self._parse_mcp_result(raw_offer) if not isinstance(raw_offer, (Exception, type(None))) else None,
            "location_name": location_name,
        }


    async def _orchestrate_show_missed_opportunities(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> dict:
        """Pre-fetch for expired: review stats showing gap."""
        gbp_args = self._get_gbp_args(merchant_id, detection_data)
        location_name = detection_data.get("location_name", "")
        raw_stats = None
        raw_perf = None
        try:
            raw_stats, raw_perf = await asyncio.gather(
                self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_get_review_stats", gbp_args),
                self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("gbp_get_performance_summary", gbp_args),
                return_exceptions=True,
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Missed-opportunities orchestration failed: {e}")


        return {
            "review_stats": self._parse_mcp_result(raw_stats) if not isinstance(raw_stats, (Exception, type(None))) else None,
            "performance_summary": self._parse_mcp_result(raw_perf) if not isinstance(raw_perf, (Exception, type(None))) else None,
            "location_name": location_name,
        }


    async def _orchestrate_winback(self, merchant_id: str, detection_data: dict) -> dict:
        """Pre-fetch for churned: minimal context."""
        return {}


    # ─── Locality Data Helper ─────────────────────────────────────────


    async def _fetch_locality_data(self, merchant_id: str) -> Optional[Any]:
        """Fetch locality/competitor data from merchant-support-mcp."""
        from agents.base_agent import BaseAgent
        try:
            await self._ensure_merchant_mcp_tools()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] action=fetch_locality_data merchant_id={merchant_id} status=init_failed error={e}")
            return None
        if BaseAgent._merchant_mcp_client is None:
            return None
        try:
            raw_result = await BaseAgent._merchant_mcp_client.call_tool(
                "get_delivery_stats_by_locality", {"merchant_id": merchant_id}
            )
            return self._parse_mcp_result(raw_result)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Locality data fetch failed: {e}")
            return None


    # ─── Google Maps URL Builder ──────────────────────────────────────


    @staticmethod
    def _build_google_maps_review_url(place_id: str) -> str:
        if not place_id:
            return ""
        return f"https://search.google.com/local/reviews?placeid={place_id}"


    # ─── Source & Tone Detection ──────────────────────────────────────


    def _get_source(self) -> str:
        """Detect source channel from metadata."""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_metadata') and self.current_metadata:
            return self.current_metadata.get("source", "whatsapp")
        return "whatsapp"


    def _detect_tone(self, message: str) -> list:
        """Detect tone indicators — language-aware version."""
        if not message:
            return []
        message_lower = message.lower()
        detected = []


        indicators = get_tone_indicators(self._language)
        for tone, keywords in indicators.items():
            if any(kw in message_lower for kw in keywords):
                detected.append(tone)
        return detected


    def _get_region_from_metadata(self) -> str:
        """Extract region from metadata, default to IN."""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_metadata') and self.current_metadata:
            region = (
                self.current_metadata.get("region")
                or self.current_metadata.get("context_data", {}).get("region")
            )
            if region:
                return region.upper()
        return "IN"


    def _get_region_from_metadata_dict(self, metadata: Dict) -> str:
        """Extract region from a metadata dict, default to IN."""
        region = (
            metadata.get("region")
            or metadata.get("context_data", {}).get("region")
        )
        if region:
            return region.upper()
        return "IN"


    # ─── Merchant Context Pre-fetch ───────────────────────────────────


    def _get_merchant_context_block(self) -> str:
        """
        Pre-fetch merchant details and inject into system prompt.
        Mirrors TestSalesAgent._get_merchant_context_block() pattern.
        """
        merchant_id = ""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_metadata') and self.current_metadata:
            merchant_id = str(
                self.current_metadata.get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id")
                or self.current_metadata.get("merchant_id")
                or ""
            )
        if not merchant_id or get_merchant_details is None:
            return ""


        try:
            data = get_merchant_details(merchant_id=int(merchant_id))
            if not data or data.get("httpStatus") != 200:
                return ""


            m = data.get("merchant", {})
            if not m:
                return ""


            parts = []
            for key, label in [
                ("merchantName", "Name"),
                ("locality", "Locality"),
                ("city", "City"),
                ("category", "Category"),
            ]:
                val = m.get(key)
                if val:
                    parts.append(f"- {label}: {val}")


            if not parts:
                return ""


            block = "\n\nMERCHANT CONTEXT (use this to personalise your pitch):\n" + "\n".join(parts)
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Injected merchant context for mid={merchant_id}")
            return block


        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Failed to fetch merchant context: {e}")
            return ""


    # ─── System Prompt ────────────────────────────────────────────────


    def _get_system_prompt(self) -> str:
        """Build state-aware system prompt with orchestration data."""
        merchant_id = ""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_metadata') and self.current_metadata:
            merchant_id = str(
                self.current_metadata.get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id")
                or self.current_metadata.get("merchant_id")
                or ""
            )


        state = getattr(self, '_current_state', State.UNASSOCIATED)
        orchestration_data = getattr(self, '_orchestration_data', {})


        state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) if merchant_id else None
        decline_count = (state_data or {}).get("decline_count", 0)


        tone = ""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_message') and self.current_message:
            detected_tones = self._detect_tone(self.current_message)
            if detected_tones:
                tone = ", ".join(detected_tones)


        chat_history_context = ""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_chat_history') and self.current_chat_history:
            chat_history_context = "\n\nCONVERSATION HISTORY (last 6 messages):\n"
            for msg in self.current_chat_history[-6:]:
                role = msg.get("role", "")
                content = msg.get("content", "")[:200]
                chat_history_context += f"{role.upper()}: {content}\n"
            chat_history_context += "\nIMPORTANT: Read the conversation history above. DO NOT repeat information already shared.\n"
            self.logger.info(
                "[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] chat_history for LLM (%d msgs): %s",
                len(self.current_chat_history),
                chat_history_context[:500],
            )


        source = self._get_source()


        # Pre-compute intro status so LLM knows upfront (no tool call needed)
        intro_already_done = self._check_intro_already_done()


        # Check if free write has been exhausted for non-paying merchants
        free_write_exhausted = getattr(self, '_merchant_sub_state', '') == 'free_write_used'


        # Check if onboarding link was already sent (Redis + chat history fallback)
        link_sent = False
        if merchant_id and state == State.UNASSOCIATED:
            state_data_for_link = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            link_sent = state_data_for_link.get("sub_state") == "link_sent"
            if not link_sent:
                # Fallback: check chat history for link patterns
                link_sent = self._check_link_sent_from_chat_history()


        # Check if health card image was already sent (unassociated state)
        health_card_sent = False
        if merchant_id and state == State.UNASSOCIATED:
            hc_state = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            health_card_sent = hc_state.get("health_card_sent", False)


        # Check current conversation topic for sequential flow (associated-non-paying)
        current_topic = ""
        if merchant_id and state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING:
            current_topic = self._resolve_active_topic(merchant_id)


        # Check if capabilities were already listed (for associated-non-paying state)
        capabilities_pitched = self._check_capabilities_pitched() if state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING else False


        # Check for pending payment context
        payment_pending = False
        payment_link = ""
        if merchant_id and state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING:
            payment_data = self._get_payment_data(merchant_id)
            if payment_data and payment_data.get("payment_link"):
                payment_pending = True
                payment_link = payment_data["payment_link"]


        # Check offer status for paying merchants
        offer_set = False
        offer_text = ""
        if merchant_id and state in (State.ASSOCIATED_PAYING, State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING):
            offer_state = (state_data or {}).get("sub_state", "")
            offer_set = offer_state == "offer_set"
            offer_text = (state_data or {}).get("offer_text", "")


        prompt = get_vera_sales_prompt(
            state=state,
            merchant_id=merchant_id,
            source=source,
            tone=tone,
            chat_history_context=chat_history_context,
            pricing_config=self._pricing,
            language=self._language,
            decline_count=decline_count,
            orchestration_data=orchestration_data,
            intro_already_done=intro_already_done,
            free_write_exhausted=free_write_exhausted,
            payment_pending=payment_pending,
            payment_link=payment_link,
            link_sent=link_sent,
            capabilities_pitched=capabilities_pitched,
            offer_set=offer_set,
            offer_text=offer_text,
            health_card_sent=health_card_sent,
            current_topic=current_topic,
        )


#         # Inject AdSales handoff context if this merchant was transferred from AdSales
#         try:
#             if merchant_id:
#                 handoff_raw = self._redis.get(f"vera:handoff:{merchant_id}")
#                 if handoff_raw:
#                     prompt += (
#                         "\n\nADSALES HANDOFF CONTEXT:\n"
#                         "This merchant was just transferred from the magicpin ad sales team (Ananya). "
#                         "They have already paid for the ₹499/month trial and completed the Magic9 offer setup. "
#                         "Your ONLY job is to pitch the FREE Google Business Profile management service "
#                         "and get them to connect their GBP using the onboarding link. "
#                         "Do NOT re-explain what magicpin is or discuss ad pricing — go straight to GBP pitch. "
#                         "The merchant is already warm and engaged.\n"
#                     )
#         except Exception as handoff_err:
#             self.logger.warning("[VeraSalesAgent] Handoff context injection failed: %s", handoff_err)


        prompt += self._get_merchant_context_block()


        self.logger.info(
            f"[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] Final prompt: state={state}, merchant_id={merchant_id}, "
            f"orchestration_keys={list(orchestration_data.keys())}, prompt_len={len(prompt)}"
        )


        return prompt


    # ─── Input Handling ───────────────────────────────────────────────


    async def handle_batch_input(self, batch_input: Dict) -> List[Dict]:
        """Override for batch path — detect state + orchestrate before LLM."""
        # Pre-fetch MCP tools BEFORE any LLM call
        await self._prefetch_mcp_tools()


        # Reset anti-repetition guards
        self._sent_messages = set()
        self._iteration_count = 0
        self._write_tool_called = False  # Track if a write tool was actually invoked this turn
        self._last_write_url = ""


        # Extract metadata
        metadata = batch_input.get("metadata", {})
        context_data = metadata.get("context_data", {})
        if not context_data.get("merchant_id"):
            mid = metadata.get("merchant_id")
            if mid:
                context_data["merchant_id"] = mid
                metadata["context_data"] = context_data


        # Set region/language from metadata
        self._region = self._get_region_from_metadata_dict(metadata)
        self._language = REGION_LANGUAGE.get(self._region, "english")
        self._pricing = await self._fetch_pricing(self._region)


        # Store last message for tone detection
        messages = batch_input.get("messages", [])
        if messages:
            self.current_message = messages[-1].get("message", "")


            self.logger.info(
                "[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] batch current_message (first 300 chars): '%s'",
                (self.current_message or "")[:300],
            )


        # Extract merchant_id from message text if not in context_data
        if not context_data.get("merchant_id") and self.current_message:
            msg_text = self.current_message.strip()
            # Try exact digit match first (message is just the ID)
            if msg_text.isdigit() and len(msg_text) >= 5:
                context_data["merchant_id"] = int(msg_text)
                metadata["context_data"] = context_data
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Extracted merchant_id=%s from message (exact)", msg_text)
            else:
                # Try regex: find 7+ digit number in message text
                match = re.search(r'\b(\d{7,})\b', msg_text)
                if match:
                    context_data["merchant_id"] = int(match.group(1))
                    metadata["context_data"] = context_data
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Extracted merchant_id=%s from message (regex)", match.group(1))


        # Store metadata and chat history EARLY so orchestration checks can use it
        self.current_metadata = metadata
        self.current_chat_history = metadata.get("chat_history", [])
        self.logger.info(
            "[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] batch chat_history loaded: %d messages",
            len(self.current_chat_history),
        )


        # Detect OAuth redirect messages
        oauth_type = self._detect_oauth_redirect_message(getattr(self, 'current_message', ''))
        if oauth_type:
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Batch: OAuth redirect detected: type={oauth_type}")


        # Reset guards (same as handle_input — without this, the hallucination guard is blind)
        self._sent_messages = set()
        self._iteration_count = 0
        self._write_tool_called = False
        self._last_write_url = ""


        # Run state detection + orchestration
        merchant_id = str(context_data.get("merchant_id", ""))
        if merchant_id:
            # If OAuth success, force state re-detection
            if oauth_type in ("success", "already_connected"):
                state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
                state_data.pop("detection_ts", None)
                self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)


            detection_data = await self._detect_state(merchant_id)
            self._current_state = detection_data.get("state", State.UNASSOCIATED)


            # Run orchestrator
            if oauth_type == "failure":
                self._orchestration_data = {"oauth_failure": True, "oauth_redirect_type": "failure"}
                self._merchant_sub_state = ""
            else:
                config = STATE_CONFIG.get(self._current_state, STATE_CONFIG[State.UNASSOCIATED])
                orchestrator_name = config["orchestrator"]
                orchestrator = getattr(self, orchestrator_name)
                self._orchestration_data = await orchestrator(merchant_id, detection_data)
                if oauth_type:
                    self._orchestration_data["oauth_redirect_type"] = oauth_type
                # Check if free write was already used (sub-state)
                state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id)
                self._merchant_sub_state = (state_data or {}).get("sub_state", "")
        else:
            self._current_state = State.UNASSOCIATED
            self._orchestration_data = {}
            self._merchant_sub_state = ""


        self.logger.info(
            f"[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] Batch: state={self._current_state}, sub_state={self._merchant_sub_state}, "
            f"orchestration_keys={list(self._orchestration_data.keys())}"
        )


        # Now call parent — _get_system_prompt() will use self._current_state and self._orchestration_data
        return await super().handle_batch_input(batch_input)


    async def handle_input(self, agent_input: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Override to detect state + orchestrate before LLM."""
        self.logger.info(
            f"[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] handle_input called. "
            f"message='{agent_input.get('message', '')[:100]}', "
            f"agent_type_in_metadata='{agent_input.get('metadata', {}).get('agent_type', 'N/A')}', "
            f"source='{agent_input.get('metadata', {}).get('source', 'N/A')}', "
            f"context_data_keys={list(agent_input.get('metadata', {}).get('context_data', {}).keys())}"
        )


        # Pre-fetch MCP tools BEFORE any LLM call
        await self._prefetch_mcp_tools()


        # Reset guards
        self._sent_messages = set()
        self._iteration_count = 0
        self._write_tool_called = False  # Track if a write tool was actually invoked this turn


        # Store message/metadata/chat_history EARLY so orchestration and prompt-building can use them
        self.current_message = agent_input.get("message", "")
        self.current_metadata = agent_input.get("metadata", {})
        self.current_chat_history = self.current_metadata.get("chat_history", [])
        self.logger.info(
            "[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] current_message (first 300 chars): '%s'",
            (self.current_message or "")[:300],
        )
        self.logger.info(
            "[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] metadata keys: %s, button_text=%s, message_type=%s, chat_history=%d msgs",
            list(self.current_metadata.keys()),
            self.current_metadata.get("button_text"),
            self.current_metadata.get("message_type"),
            len(self.current_chat_history),
        )


        # Set region/language from metadata
        self._region = self._get_region_from_metadata()
        self._language = REGION_LANGUAGE.get(self._region, "english")
        self._pricing = await self._fetch_pricing(self._region)


        # Detect tone
        detected_tones = self._detect_tone(self.current_message)
        if detected_tones:
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Detected tones: {detected_tones}")


        # Extract merchant_id from message if not in context_data
        context_data = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {})
        if not context_data.get("merchant_id"):
            message = self.current_message.strip()
            if message.isdigit() and len(message) >= 5:
                context_data["merchant_id"] = int(message)
                agent_input["metadata"]["context_data"] = context_data
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Extracted merchant_id=%s from message (exact)", message)
            else:
                match = re.search(r'\b(\d{7,})\b', message)
                if match:
                    context_data["merchant_id"] = int(match.group(1))
                    agent_input["metadata"]["context_data"] = context_data
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Extracted merchant_id=%s from message (regex)", match.group(1))


        # Ensure merchant_id in context_data from metadata fallback
        if not agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id"):
            mid = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("merchant_id")
            if mid:
                context_data = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {})
                context_data["merchant_id"] = mid
                agent_input["metadata"]["context_data"] = context_data


        # Detect OAuth redirect messages (merchant returning from OAuth flow)
        oauth_type = self._detect_oauth_redirect_message(self.current_message)
        if oauth_type:
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] OAuth redirect detected: type={oauth_type}")


        # Run state detection + orchestration
        merchant_id = str(agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id", ""))
        if merchant_id:
            # If OAuth success/already_connected, force state re-detection (bypass cache)
            if oauth_type in ("success", "already_connected"):
                self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] OAuth success — clearing cached state for fresh detection")
                state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
                state_data.pop("detection_ts", None)  # Force re-detect
                self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)


            detection_data = await self._detect_state(merchant_id)
