            self._current_state = detection_data.get("state", State.UNASSOCIATED)


            # If OAuth failure message, keep state as-is and inject failure context
            if oauth_type == "failure":
                self._orchestration_data = {"oauth_failure": True}
                self._merchant_sub_state = ""
            else:
                config = STATE_CONFIG.get(self._current_state, STATE_CONFIG[State.UNASSOCIATED])
                orchestrator_name = config["orchestrator"]
                orchestrator = getattr(self, orchestrator_name)
                self._orchestration_data = await orchestrator(merchant_id, detection_data)
                # Check if free write was already used (sub-state)
                state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id)
                self._merchant_sub_state = (state_data or {}).get("sub_state", "")


            # Inject OAuth redirect context into orchestration data
            if oauth_type:
                self._orchestration_data["oauth_redirect_type"] = oauth_type
        else:
            self._current_state = State.UNASSOCIATED
            self._orchestration_data = {}
            self._merchant_sub_state = ""


        self.logger.info(
            f"[VERA_SALES_DEBUG] state={self._current_state}, sub_state={self._merchant_sub_state}, "
            f"oauth_type={oauth_type}, orchestration_keys={list(self._orchestration_data.keys())}"
        )


        return await super().handle_input(agent_input)


    # ─── Tool Call Handling ────────────────────────────────────────────


    async def _handle_tool_call(self, message: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Override with state enforcement + anti-repetition + MCP routing."""
        tool_name = message.get("name")
        tool_args = message.get("arguments", {})


        # [LOG #5] LLM response — log each tool call the LLM decided to make
        _log_mid = (getattr(self, 'current_metadata', None) or {}).get('context_data', {}).get('merchant_id', 'unknown')
        self.logger.info(f"[VERA_LLM_RESPONSE] mid={_log_mid} tool_call={tool_name} args_keys={list(tool_args.keys()) if isinstance(tool_args, dict) else '?'}")


        self._iteration_count += 1


        if self._iteration_count > self.MAX_AGENT_ITERATIONS:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Max iterations ({self.MAX_AGENT_ITERATIONS}) reached")
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "anti_loop", "max_iterations_reached")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                {"status": "blocked", "reason": "Max iterations reached"}
            )


        # State enforcement — reject tools not allowed in current state
        current_state = getattr(self, '_current_state', State.UNASSOCIATED)
        config = STATE_CONFIG.get(current_state, STATE_CONFIG[State.UNASSOCIATED])
        allowed = set(config["available_tools"]) | set(config.get("merchant_mcp_tools", []))


        if tool_name not in allowed:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Tool {tool_name} blocked in state {current_state}")
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "state_enforcement", f"blocked_{tool_name}")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                {"status": "blocked", "reason": f"Tool {tool_name} not available in state {current_state}"}
            )


        # Anti-repetition for communicate_to_user
        if tool_name == "communicate_to_user":
            user_message = tool_args.get("message", "")
            if (
                current_state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING
                and not getattr(self, "_write_tool_called", False)
                and self._claims_write_completion(user_message)
            ):
                self.logger.warning("[VeraSalesAgent] Blocking premature write-claim message without successful tool call")
                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    self.current_session_id,
                    tool_name,
                    {
                        "status": "blocked",
                        "reason": "Do not claim a review reply or post is done without first calling the write tool successfully.",
                    },
                )
            message_hash = hash(user_message[:200])
            if message_hash in self._sent_messages:
                self.logger.warning("[VeraSalesAgent] Blocking duplicate message")
                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                    {"status": "already_sent", "message": "Message already sent"}
                )
            self._sent_messages.add(message_hash)
            if "all_concerns_answered" in tool_args:
                tool_args["all_concerns_answered"] = True
            # If a write tool succeeded this turn, ensure the Google Maps URL is shared
            last_url = getattr(self, "_last_write_url", "")
            if getattr(self, "_write_tool_called", False) and last_url and last_url not in user_message:
                tool_args["message"] = f"{user_message}\nHo gaya! Yahan dekh sakte hain: {last_url}"
                self._last_write_url = ""


        # Handle local introduce_vera tool
        if tool_name == "introduce_vera_if_not_done_already":
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] introduce_vera_if_not_done_already called, routing to local handler")
            return self._handle_introduce_vera()


        # Free write enforcement — counted across ALL states, blocked in non-paying
        mid = str(
            (getattr(self, 'current_metadata', None) or {}).get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id")
            or (getattr(self, 'current_metadata', None) or {}).get("merchant_id")
            or ""
        )


        # [LOG #2] Write tool tracking
        if tool_name in self.WRITE_TOOLS:
            self.logger.info(f"[VERA_WRITE] mid={mid} tool={tool_name} — WRITE TOOL CALLED")


        if tool_name in self.WRITE_TOOLS and current_state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING:
            write_count = self._get_write_count(mid) if mid else 0
            if write_count >= self.REDIS_WRITE_MAX:
                # [LOG #4] Free write blocked — exhausted
                self.logger.info(f"[VERA_FREE_WRITE] mid={mid} tool={tool_name} action=blocked_exhausted")
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Free write limit reached (count=%d, state=%s) for merchant %s, blocking %s", write_count, current_state, mid, tool_name)
                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                    {
                        "status": "blocked",
                        "reason": (
                            "Free write action already used. Pitch the trial NOW.\n\n"
                            "PITCH THIS to the merchant:\n"
                            f"Ab puri service chalu karte hain! Sirf {self._pricing['currency_symbol']} {self._pricing['trial_price'] or self._pricing['plans']['starter']} mein start karo:\n"
                            "- Daily smart review replies — trust badhega\n"
                            "- Weekly Google Posts — fresh content, zyada visibility\n"
                            "- Photos upload aur optimize — profile attractive\n"
                            "- Profile audit — hours, menu, description sab correct\n"
                            "- Performance insights — views, calls, directions sab track\n"
                            "- Search keywords — log kaise dhundh rahe hain\n\n"
                            f"{self._pricing['currency_symbol']} {self._pricing['trial_price'] or self._pricing['plans']['starter']} mein start, phir {self._pricing['currency_symbol']} {self._pricing['plans']['starter']}/month autopay. Cancel anytime.\n"
                            "Call vera_create_payment_link to generate the payment link and share it."
                        ),
                    }
                )
            else:
                # [LOG #4] Free write consumed
                self.logger.info(f"[VERA_FREE_WRITE] mid={mid} tool={tool_name} action=consumed")
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Allowing free write action: %s (count=%d, state=%s) for merchant %s", tool_name, write_count, current_state, mid)


        # Auto-inject transaction_id and merchant_id for payment status check from Redis
        if tool_name == "vera_check_payment_status" and mid:
            if not tool_args.get("merchant_id") and mid:
                tool_args["merchant_id"] = mid
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Auto-injected merchant_id=%s for payment status check", mid)
            if not tool_args.get("transaction_id"):
                payment_data = self._get_payment_data(mid)
                if payment_data and payment_data.get("transaction_id"):
                    tool_args["transaction_id"] = payment_data["transaction_id"]
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Auto-injected transaction_id=%s for merchant %s", tool_args["transaction_id"], mid)
                else:
                    return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                        self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                        {"status": "error", "reason": "No payment link has been created yet. Call vera_create_payment_link first to generate a payment link."}
                    )


        # Return cached payment link if still valid (1-day TTL)
        if tool_name == "vera_create_payment_link" and mid:
            cached = self._get_payment_data(mid)
            if cached and cached.get("payment_link") and cached.get("status") != "regenerate":
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Returning cached payment link for merchant %s", mid)
                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                    {"status": "success", "data": {
                        "payment_link": cached["payment_link"],
                        "transaction_id": cached["transaction_id"],
                        "merchant_id": mid,
                        "amount": self._pricing.get("trial_price"),
                        "recurring_amount": self._pricing["plans"]["starter"],
                        "cached": True,
                    }}
                )


        # Route vera MCP tools
        if tool_name in self.VERA_SALES_MCP_TOOLS:
            result = await self._handle_vera_mcp_tool(tool_name, tool_args)
            self._handle_post_tool_state_update(tool_name, tool_args, result)


            # After a successful gbp_reply_to_review, inject Google Maps URL into the result
            if tool_name == "gbp_reply_to_review" and self._tool_result_succeeded(result):
                maps_url = getattr(self, '_orchestration_data', {}).get("google_maps_review_url", "")
                if maps_url:
                    inner = result.get("result", {}) if isinstance(result, dict) else {}
                    result = MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                        self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                        {
                            "status": "success",
                            "data": inner,
                            "google_maps_url": maps_url,
                            "IMPORTANT": f"Reply posted! NOW share this Google Maps URL with the merchant so they can see it live: {maps_url}",
                        }
                    )


            # After a successful write action: always increment count (across all states)
            if tool_name in self.WRITE_TOOLS and mid:
                if self._tool_result_succeeded(result):
                    self._write_tool_called = True  # Mark that a real write tool was invoked
                    # Cache URL for proof-of-post messaging
                    url = ""
                    inner_result = result.get("result", {}) if isinstance(result, dict) else {}
                    if isinstance(result, dict):
                        url = result.get("google_maps_url") or ""
                        if not url:
                            inner = result.get("result", {})
                            if isinstance(inner, dict):
                                url = inner.get("google_maps_url") or inner.get("maps_url") or inner.get("location_url") or ""
                    if url:
                        self._last_write_url = url
                    self._increment_write_count(mid)
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Write count incremented for merchant %s (state=%s, tool=%s)", mid, current_state, tool_name)
                    # Mark sub_state for non-paying merchants so prompt knows to pitch
                    if current_state == State.ASSOCIATED_NON_PAYING:
                        state_data = self._get_merchant_state(mid) or {}
                        state_data["sub_state"] = "free_write_used"
                        self._set_merchant_state(mid, state_data)
                        self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] sub_state set to free_write_used for merchant %s", mid)


            # Store payment data in dedicated Redis key after successful payment link creation
            if tool_name == "vera_create_payment_link" and mid:
                raw_data = result.get("result", {}) if isinstance(result, dict) else {}
                parsed_payment = self._parse_mcp_result(raw_data)
                if isinstance(parsed_payment, dict) and parsed_payment.get("payment_link"):
                    self._set_payment_data(mid, {
                        "payment_link": parsed_payment["payment_link"],
                        "transaction_id": parsed_payment.get("transaction_id", ""),
                        "merchant_id": mid,
                        "status": "pending",
                    })
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Payment data stored in Redis for merchant %s (1-day TTL): txn=%s", mid, parsed_payment.get("transaction_id", ""))


            return result


        # Route merchant-support MCP tools
        if tool_name in config.get("merchant_mcp_tools", []):
            return await self._handle_merchant_mcp_tool_call(tool_name, tool_args)


        # All other tools -> parent
        return await super()._handle_tool_call(message)


    def _check_intro_already_done(self) -> bool:
        """Quick check if Vera intro was already done (for system prompt injection)."""
        # Check for AdSales handoff — merchant already knows magicpin from Ananya
        try:
            context_data = (getattr(self, 'current_metadata', None) or {}).get("context_data", {})
            merchant_id = str(context_data.get("merchant_id", ""))
            if merchant_id:
                handoff_data = self._redis.get(f"vera:handoff:{merchant_id}")
                if handoff_data:
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] _check_intro_already_done: TRUE (AdSales handoff detected)")
                    return True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.warning("[VeraSalesAgent] AdSales handoff check failed: %s", e)


        intro_keywords = ["priya", "vera", "google business profile", "gbp management", "gbp manage"]


        # Check current message for template
        current_msg = (getattr(self, 'current_message', '') or '').lower()
        if 'template:' in current_msg:
            for kw in intro_keywords:
                if kw in current_msg:
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] _check_intro_already_done: TRUE (template contains '%s')", kw)
                    return True


        # Check assistant messages in chat history
        chat_history = getattr(self, 'current_chat_history', []) or []
        for msg in chat_history:
            if msg.get("role") == "assistant":
                content = (msg.get("content") or "").lower()
                for kw in intro_keywords:
                    if kw in content:
                        self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] _check_intro_already_done: TRUE (assistant msg contains '%s')", kw)
                        return True


        self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] _check_intro_already_done: FALSE")
        return False


    def _check_link_sent_from_chat_history(self) -> bool:
        """Fallback: check chat history for onboarding link patterns (in case Redis lost the data)."""
        link_keywords = ["magp.in/", "/oauth/authorize", "connect karo", "google profile connect",
                         "link tap karo", "sign in karo", "gmail se sign in"]
        chat_history = getattr(self, 'current_chat_history', []) or []
        for msg in chat_history:
            if msg.get("role") == "assistant":
                content = (msg.get("content") or "").lower()
                for kw in link_keywords:
                    if kw in content:
                        self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] _check_link_sent_from_chat_history: TRUE (found '%s')", kw)
                        return True
        return False


    def _check_capabilities_pitched(self) -> bool:
        """Check if Vera's capability list was already sent in chat history."""
        cap_keywords = ["reviews ka reply", "posts create", "photos upload", "hours, description",
                        "insights", "kar sakti hoon", "sab kar sakti", "ye sab kar",
                        "review replies", "google posts", "performance"]


        chat_history = getattr(self, 'current_chat_history', []) or []
        for msg in chat_history:
            if msg.get("role") == "assistant":
                content = (msg.get("content") or "").lower()
                matches = sum(1 for kw in cap_keywords if kw in content)
                if matches >= 3:  # At least 3 capability keywords in one message = capabilities were pitched
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] _check_capabilities_pitched: TRUE (%d keywords matched)", matches)
                    return True


        self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] _check_capabilities_pitched: FALSE")
        return False


    def _handle_introduce_vera(self) -> Dict:
        """Check chat history AND current message for prior Priya/Vera introduction."""
        chat_history = getattr(self, 'current_chat_history', []) or []
        self.logger.info(
            "[VeraSalesAgent] _handle_introduce_vera: checking %d messages in chat history",
            len(chat_history),
        )


        intro_keywords = ["priya", "vera", "google business profile", "gbp management", "gbp manage"]
        already_introduced = False
        matched_keyword = None


        # Check if the current user message contains a template that already introduced Vera
        # (message-server sends "Template: ...\nMerchant: ..." on first reply)
        current_msg = (getattr(self, 'current_message', '') or '').lower()
        if 'template:' in current_msg:
            for kw in intro_keywords:
                if kw in current_msg:
                    already_introduced = True
                    matched_keyword = kw
                    self.logger.info(
                        "[VeraSalesAgent] _handle_introduce_vera: found keyword '%s' in template message",
                        kw,
                    )
                    break


        # Check assistant messages in chat history
        if not already_introduced:
            for msg in chat_history:
                if msg.get("role") == "assistant":
                    content = (msg.get("content") or "").lower()
                    for kw in intro_keywords:
                        if kw in content:
                            already_introduced = True
                            matched_keyword = kw
                            snippet = content[:80]
                            self.logger.info(
                                "[VeraSalesAgent] _handle_introduce_vera: found keyword '%s' in assistant msg: '%s...'",
                                kw, snippet,
                            )
                            break
                    if already_introduced:
                        break


        if already_introduced:
            self.logger.info(
                "[VeraSalesAgent] _handle_introduce_vera: result=already_introduced (matched='%s')",
                matched_keyword,
            )
            result = {
                "status": "already_introduced",
                "message": (
                    "You (Priya) have already introduced yourself and Vera via the template message. "
                    "SKIP introduction entirely. DIRECTLY answer the merchant's question or request. "
                    "If they asked to see reviews, show reviews. If they asked a question, answer it. "
                    "Do NOT re-introduce yourself."
                ),
            }
        else:
            self.logger.info(
                "[VeraSalesAgent] _handle_introduce_vera: result=introduce (no intro keywords found in %d assistant msgs)",
                sum(1 for m in chat_history if m.get("role") == "assistant"),
            )
            result = {
                "status": "introduce",
                "message": (
                    "You have NOT introduced yourself yet. Introduce yourself briefly as Priya from magicpin "
                    "and what Vera does (Google Business Profile management). BUT if the merchant asked a specific "
                    "question or made a request, ANSWER THAT in the same message — do not send an intro-only reply. "
                    "Keep intro to 1-2 lines, then address their request. Do NOT pitch pricing or trial yet."
                ),
            }


        self.logger.info(
            "[VeraSalesAgent] _handle_introduce_vera: returning status=%s",
            result["status"],
        )
        return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
            self.current_session_id, "introduce_vera_if_not_done_already", result
        )


    async def _handle_vera_mcp_tool(self, tool_name: str, tool_args: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Call vera-mcp directly via HTTPMCPClient — returns raw JSON data."""
        try:
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraSalesAgent] Calling vera-mcp: {tool_name}")
            result = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool(tool_name, tool_args)
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name, result
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraSalesAgent] vera-mcp call failed: {tool_name} - {e}")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                {"status": "error", "error": f"Tool call failed: {str(e)}"}
            )


    def _handle_post_tool_state_update(self, tool_name: str, tool_args: Dict, result: Dict):
        """Update Redis state based on tool results (simplified for 5-state model)."""
        merchant_id = str(tool_args.get("merchant_id", ""))
        if not merchant_id and hasattr(self, 'current_metadata') and self.current_metadata:
            merchant_id = str(
                self.current_metadata.get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id", "")
            )
        if not merchant_id:
            return


        # Everything below only applies on semantic success
        if not self._tool_result_succeeded(result):
            return


        # Track current_topic for sequential conversation flow
        if tool_name in ("gbp_list_reviews", "gbp_get_review", "gbp_batch_get_reviews",
                         "gbp_generate_review_reply", "gbp_reply_to_review", "gbp_get_review_stats"):
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            if not state_data.get("current_topic"):
                state_data["current_topic"] = "reviews"
                self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] current_topic set to reviews for merchant %s", merchant_id)


        if tool_name in ("gbp_create_post", "gbp_list_posts", "gbp_get_post",
                         "gbp_update_post", "gbp_delete_post", "gbp_get_post_insights"):
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            state_data["current_topic"] = "posts"
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] current_topic set to posts for merchant %s", merchant_id)


        if tool_name == "gbp_get_onboarding_url":
            # Track that the onboarding link was sent (for anti-repetition in unassociated state)
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            state_data["sub_state"] = "link_sent"
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] sub_state set to link_sent for merchant %s", merchant_id)


        elif tool_name == "vera_create_subscription":
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            state_data["state"] = State.ASSOCIATED_PAYING
            state_data["previous_state"] = self._current_state
            state_data["transition_trigger"] = "subscription_created"
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self._current_state = State.ASSOCIATED_PAYING
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Transition: -> associated-paying (subscription_created)")


        elif tool_name == "vera_create_payment_link":
            # Store payment link in state data — no state transition yet (wait for payment)
            # Unwrap double-wrapped MCP response (data may be a JSON string)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Payment raw result_data type=%s, value=%s", type(result_data).__name__, str(result_data)[:500])
            parsed = self._parse_mcp_result(result_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Payment parsed type=%s, value=%s", type(parsed).__name__, str(parsed)[:500])
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            if isinstance(parsed, dict):
                state_data["payment_link"] = parsed.get("payment_link", "")
                state_data["payment_txn_id"] = parsed.get("transaction_id", "")
                state_data["payment_status"] = "pending"
                self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Payment link created: link=%s, txn=%s", state_data["payment_link"], state_data["payment_txn_id"])
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)


        elif tool_name == "vera_check_payment_status":
            # If payment is successful, transition to paying state
            # Unwrap double-wrapped MCP response
            parsed_status = self._parse_mcp_result(result_data)
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            if isinstance(parsed_status, dict):
                payment_status = parsed_status.get("status", "")
                state_data["payment_status"] = payment_status
                # Update dedicated payment Redis key with latest status
                payment_cache = self._get_payment_data(merchant_id)
                if payment_cache:
                    payment_cache["status"] = payment_status
                    self._set_payment_data(merchant_id, payment_cache)
                if payment_status in ("SUCCESS", "COMPLETED", "success", "completed"):
                    state_data["state"] = State.ASSOCIATED_PAYING
                    state_data["previous_state"] = self._current_state
                    state_data["transition_trigger"] = "payment_completed"
                    self._current_state = State.ASSOCIATED_PAYING
                    self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Transition: -> associated-paying (payment_completed)")
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)


        elif tool_name == "vera_store_offer":
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            parsed = self._parse_mcp_result(result_data)
            if isinstance(parsed, dict):
                state_data["sub_state"] = "offer_set"
                state_data["offer_text"] = parsed.get("title", tool_args.get("title", ""))
                state_data["offer_type"] = parsed.get("offer_type", tool_args.get("offer_type", ""))
                state_data["offer_audience"] = parsed.get("audience", tool_args.get("audience", "new_user"))
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Offer stored for merchant %s: %s", merchant_id, state_data.get("offer_text"))


        elif tool_name == "vera_update_offer":
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            if tool_args.get("title"):
                state_data["offer_text"] = tool_args["title"]
            if tool_args.get("offer_type"):
                state_data["offer_type"] = tool_args["offer_type"]
            if tool_args.get("audience"):
                state_data["offer_audience"] = tool_args["audience"]
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Offer updated for merchant %s", merchant_id)


        elif tool_name == "vera_deactivate_offer":
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            state_data["sub_state"] = "offer_deactivated"
            state_data.pop("offer_text", None)
            state_data.pop("offer_type", None)
            state_data.pop("offer_audience", None)
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Offer deactivated for merchant %s", merchant_id)


        elif tool_name == "vera_pause_offer":
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            state_data["sub_state"] = "offer_paused"
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Offer paused for merchant %s", merchant_id)


        elif tool_name == "vera_resume_offer":
            state_data = self._get_merchant_state(merchant_id) or {}
            state_data["sub_state"] = "offer_set"
            self._set_merchant_state(merchant_id, state_data)
            self.logger.info("[VeraSalesAgent] Offer resumed for merchant %s", merchant_id)

            ],

            ],
            "declining": [
                "nahi chahiye", "no thanks", "nahi", "baad mein",

        return {

"""
Vera Social Media Manager Agent


Manages merchant Google Business Profile via WhatsApp.
Uses vera-mcp tools via HTTPMCPClient for GBP API operations.


Modeled after MerchantMasterV1WinbackAgent:
- Same init pattern (BaseAgent.__init__ + manual EmployeeAgent attrs)
- Anti-repetition guards (_sent_messages, _iteration_count)
- Tone detection from MerchantMasterAgentV2
- WhatsApp-adaptive prompt


Key difference from WinbackAgent:
- Uses MCP tools directly (no specialist routing)
- Calls vera-mcp service for all GBP operations
- Handles photo uploads from WhatsApp
"""


import os
import json
import logging
import asyncio
import traceback
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional


from employee_agents.base.employee_agent import EmployeeAgent
from agents.vera.core_prompts import get_vera_whatsapp_prompt, DEFAULT_VERA_PRICING
from utility.http_mcp_client import HTTPMCPClient
from utility.message_protocol import MessageProtocol
from utility.metrics import increment_tool_call
from utility.constants import DEFAULT_VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class VeraManager(EmployeeAgent):
    """
    Vera Social Media Agent - manages merchant GBP/social media via WhatsApp.


    Flow: merchant WhatsApp msg -> botops -> this agent -> vera-mcp tools -> response
    """
    agent_type = "VeraManager"
    MAX_AGENT_ITERATIONS = 5
    ONBOARDING_MODE = os.getenv("VERA_ONBOARDING_MODE", "auto_reply_first")
    SPECIALIST_TYPE = "Vera"


    # All 51 vera-mcp tools
    VERA_MCP_ALLOWED_TOOLS = [
        # Reviews (7)
        "gbp_list_reviews", "gbp_get_review", "gbp_batch_get_reviews",
        "gbp_reply_to_review", "gbp_delete_review_reply",
        "gbp_get_review_stats", "gbp_generate_review_reply",
        # Posts (6)
        "gbp_create_post", "gbp_list_posts", "gbp_get_post",
        "gbp_update_post", "gbp_delete_post", "gbp_get_post_insights",
        # Photos (8)
        "gbp_upload_photos", "gbp_list_media", "gbp_get_media",
        "gbp_update_media", "gbp_delete_media", "gbp_set_cover_photo",
        "gbp_list_customer_photos", "gbp_get_customer_photo",

        "gbp_list_locations", "gbp_get_location", "gbp_search_location",
        "gbp_resolve_merchant", "gbp_get_google_updated_location", "gbp_batch_get_locations",
        # OAuth Onboarding (3)
        "gbp_get_onboarding_url", "gbp_check_merchant_access", "gbp_check_onboarding_status",

        "gbp_create_place_action", "gbp_list_place_actions",
        "gbp_update_place_action", "gbp_delete_place_action",
        # Notifications (2)
        "gbp_get_notification_settings", "gbp_update_notification_settings",
        # Food Menus (2)
        "gbp_get_food_menus", "gbp_update_food_menus",
        # Photo Pipeline (4)
        "vera_enhance_photo",
        "vera_score_photo_quality", "vera_process_photo_batch",
    ]


    # Default tone indicators (Hinglish — English + Hindi keywords)
    TONE_INDICATORS = {
        "happy": ["thank", "great", "awesome", "nice", "good", "shukriya", "dhanyavaad", "badiya"],
        "confused": ["samajh nahi", "kaise", "how", "kya hai", "explain", "batao", "nahi pata"],
        "requesting": ["kar do", "please", "help", "chahiye", "kardo", "update", "dikhao"],
        "urgent": ["jaldi", "urgent", "abhi", "now", "turant", "immediately"],
        "frustrated": ["kaam nahi", "problem", "issue", "galat", "wrong", "nahi ho raha"],
    }

    TONE_INDICATORS_BY_LANGUAGE = {
        "hinglish": {
            "happy": ["thank", "great", "awesome", "nice", "good", "shukriya", "dhanyavaad", "badiya", "mast", "accha"],
            "confused": ["samajh nahi", "kaise", "how", "kya hai", "explain", "batao", "nahi pata", "confused"],

    class MerchantState:
        ONBOARDING_PENDING = "onboarding_pending"
        ONBOARDING_PITCHED = "onboarding_pitched"
        TRIAL_ACTIVE = "trial_active"

    def __init__(self, agent_id: str):
        # Follow WinbackAgent init pattern exactly:
        from agents.base_agent import BaseAgent
        from employee_agents.base.agent_memory import AgentMemory
        BaseAgent.__init__(self, agent_id)


        # EmployeeAgent attributes (same as winback)
        self._chat_client = None
        self._sop_config = None
        self._mcp_client = None
        self._bq_execution_count = 0
        self.memory = AgentMemory(agent_id)
        self._query_start_time = None
        self.PROGRESS_UPDATE_ENABLED = False


        # Anti-repetition guards (from winback)
        self._sent_messages = set()
        self._iteration_count = 0


        # Vera MCP client
        vera_mcp_url = os.getenv('VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL', DEFAULT_VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL)
        self.logger.info(f"[VeraManager] Connecting to vera-mcp at: {vera_mcp_url}")
        self.vera_mcp_client = HTTPMCPClient(
            server_url=vera_mcp_url,
            tool_prefix="",
            timeout=30
        )
        self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = None
        self._pricing = DEFAULT_VERA_PRICING
        self._pricing_cache: Dict[str, Any] = {}


        # Photo pipeline
        from agents.vera import PhotoStorage, PhotoEnhancer, PhotoCaptioner, PhotoScorer
        self.photo_storage = PhotoStorage()
        self.photo_enhancer = PhotoEnhancer(auto_enhance=True)
        self.photo_captioner = PhotoCaptioner()
        self.photo_scorer = PhotoScorer()


        # Specialist mode attributes (used when called via subscribe_ask_channel)
        self._specialist_response = None
        self._running_as_specialist = False
        self._specialist_actions = []


        self.logger.info("VeraManager initialized")
        increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "initialization", "success")


    @classmethod
    def subscribe_ask_channel(cls, subscriber_agent_class=None):
        """Broadcast Vera specialist capabilities for other agents to subscribe."""
        tool_name = f"ask_{cls.SPECIALIST_TYPE.lower()}"
        return {
            "tool": {
                "type": "function",
                "name": tool_name,
                "description": (
                    "Ask the Vera specialist to perform Google Business Profile operations. "
                    "Use for: checking GBP connection, getting reviews/stats, replying to reviews, "
                    "getting insights/performance, checking profile completeness, creating posts, "
                    "listing/managing photos, getting onboarding URL, checking subscription status, "
                    "starting trial, creating subscription. Pass a natural language query describing what you need."
                ),
                "parameters": {
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "query": {
                            "type": "string",
                            "description": "What you need from the merchant's Google Business Profile. Be specific."
                        },
                        "merchant_id": {
                            "type": "string",
                            "description": "The merchant's ID"
                        }
                    },
                    "required": ["query", "merchant_id"]
                }
            },
            "handler": cls._handle_ask
        }


    @classmethod
    async def _handle_ask(cls, master_agent, args: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Handle query from a master agent (e.g., VeraSalesAgent)."""
        query = args.get("query", "")
        merchant_id = str(args.get("merchant_id", ""))
        context = args.get("context", {})


        agent_id = f"vera_specialist_{merchant_id}"
        specialist = cls(agent_id)


        # Copy context from master agent
        specialist.current_session_id = getattr(master_agent, 'current_session_id', None)
        specialist.current_context = getattr(master_agent, 'current_context', {})
        specialist.current_chat_history = getattr(master_agent, 'current_chat_history', [])
        specialist.current_metadata = getattr(master_agent, 'current_metadata', {})


        return await specialist.run(merchant_id, query, context)


    async def run(self, merchant_id, query: str, context: Optional[Dict] = None) -> Dict:
        """Run as specialist — handle a query and return structured response."""
        self._running_as_specialist = True
        self._specialist_response = None
        self._specialist_actions = []


        try:
            session_id = (context or {}).get("session_id") or \
                         self.current_session_id or \
                         f"vera_specialist_{merchant_id}"


            agent_input = {
                "type": "agent_input",
                "session_id": session_id,
                "message": f"Merchant ID: {merchant_id}\n\nQuery: {query}",
                "metadata": {
                    "source": "specialist",
                    **({"chat_history": self.current_chat_history} if self.current_chat_history else {}),
                    "context_data": {
                        "merchant_id": merchant_id,
                        **(context or {})
                    }
                }
            }


            await self.handle_input(agent_input)
            return self.get_response()
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraManager] Specialist error: {e}")
            return {"status": "error", "response": f"Error: {str(e)}"}
        finally:
            self._running_as_specialist = False


    def get_response(self) -> Dict:
        """Get specialist response after processing."""
        response = self._specialist_response or {
            "status": "error",
            "response": "No response generated"
        }
        if self._specialist_actions:
            response["actions"] = self._specialist_actions
        return response


    def _get_source(self) -> str:
        """Detect source channel from metadata."""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_metadata') and self.current_metadata:
            return self.current_metadata.get("source", "whatsapp")
        return "whatsapp"


    def _detect_tone(self, message: str, language: str = "hinglish") -> list:
        """Detect tone indicators in merchant message.


        Args:
            message: The merchant's message text
            language: Language for keyword sets ('hinglish' or 'english')
        """
        if not message:
            return []
        message_lower = message.lower()
        detected = []
        indicators = self.TONE_INDICATORS_BY_LANGUAGE.get(language, self.TONE_INDICATORS)
        for tone, keywords in indicators.items():
            if any(kw in message_lower for kw in keywords):
                detected.append(tone)
        return detected


    def _get_system_prompt(self) -> str:
        """Get system prompt - always WhatsApp for Vera."""
        return self._get_vera_whatsapp_prompt()


    def _get_vera_whatsapp_prompt(self) -> str:
        """Build Vera WhatsApp system prompt with context injection."""
        # Inject merchant_id
        merchant_id = ""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_metadata') and self.current_metadata:
            mid = (self.current_metadata.get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id")
                   or self.current_metadata.get("merchant_id"))
            if mid:
                merchant_id = f"\nCURRENT MERCHANT_ID: {mid}\nALWAYS use this merchant_id when calling any tool that needs it.\n"


        # Tone detection
        tone_context = ""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_message') and self.current_message:
            detected_tones = self._detect_tone(self.current_message)
            if detected_tones:
                tone_context = f"\nDETECTED TONE: {', '.join(detected_tones)}"


        # Chat history context
        chat_history_context = ""
        if hasattr(self, 'current_chat_history') and self.current_chat_history:
            chat_history_context = "\n\nCONVERSATION HISTORY (last 6 messages):\n"
            for msg in self.current_chat_history[-6:]:
                role = msg.get("role", "")
                content = msg.get("content", "")[:150]
                chat_history_context += f"{role.upper()}: {content}\n"


        return get_vera_whatsapp_prompt(
            merchant_id=merchant_id,
            tone_context=tone_context,
            chat_history_context=chat_history_context,
            onboarding_mode=self.ONBOARDING_MODE,
            source=self._get_source(),
            pricing_config=self._pricing,
        )


    def get_tools(self) -> list:
        """Get base tools + Vera MCP tools (must call _prefetch_mcp_tools first)."""
        base_tools = super().get_tools()
        return base_tools + (self._vera_mcp_tools_cache or [])


    async def _fetch_pricing(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Fetch pricing from vera-mcp. Falls back to DEFAULT_VERA_PRICING on error.


        Cached for the agent's lifetime — same pattern as _prefetch_mcp_tools.
        VeraManager is IN-only so no region key needed.
        """
        if "IN" in self._pricing_cache:
            return self._pricing_cache["IN"]
        try:
            raw = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool("vera_get_pricing", {"country_code": "IN"})
            data = raw.get("data", raw) if isinstance(raw, dict) else {}
            plans_list = data.get("plans", [])
            result = {
                "currency_symbol": data.get("currency_symbol", DEFAULT_VERA_PRICING["currency_symbol"]),
                "plans": {p["id"]: p["numeric_price"] for p in plans_list} or DEFAULT_VERA_PRICING["plans"],
            }
            self._pricing_cache["IN"] = result
            return result
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning("[VeraManager] _fetch_pricing failed (%s), using default", exc)
            return DEFAULT_VERA_PRICING


    async def _prefetch_mcp_tools(self):
        """Async pre-fetch of MCP tools. Must be called before get_tools()."""
        if self._vera_mcp_tools_cache is not None:
            return
        try:
            await self.vera_mcp_client.get_tools()
            self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = self.vera_mcp_client.filter_allowed_tools(
                self.VERA_MCP_ALLOWED_TOOLS
            )
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraManager] Discovered {len(self._vera_mcp_tools_cache)} vera-mcp tools")
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraManager] Failed to discover vera-mcp tools: {e}")
            self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = []


    async def handle_batch_input(self, batch_input: Dict) -> List[Dict]:
        """Override to prefetch vera-mcp tools for batch path (Google Chat consumer).


        Without this, handle_batch_input goes straight to BaseAgent which calls
        _process_agent_input -> get_tools() without ever calling _prefetch_mcp_tools,
        so _vera_mcp_tools_cache stays None and the agent gets zero vera MCP tools.
        """
        # Pre-fetch MCP tools and pricing BEFORE any LLM call happens
        await self._prefetch_mcp_tools()
        self._pricing = await self._fetch_pricing()


        # Reset anti-repetition guards
        self._sent_messages = set()
        self._iteration_count = 0


        # Extract merchant_id from batch metadata for system prompt injection
        metadata = batch_input.get("metadata", {})
        context_data = metadata.get("context_data", {})
        if not context_data.get("merchant_id"):
            mid = metadata.get("merchant_id")
            if mid:
                context_data["merchant_id"] = mid
                metadata["context_data"] = context_data


        # Store last message for tone detection in system prompt
        messages = batch_input.get("messages", [])
        if messages:
            self.current_message = messages[-1].get("message", "")


        return await super().handle_batch_input(batch_input)


    async def handle_input(self, agent_input: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Override to reset guards, handle photos, extract merchant_id."""
        # Pre-fetch MCP tools and pricing (async - must happen before get_tools() is called)
        await self._prefetch_mcp_tools()
        self._pricing = await self._fetch_pricing()


        # Reset guards
        self._sent_messages = set()
        self._iteration_count = 0


        # Store message/metadata early
        self.current_message = agent_input.get("message", "")
        self.current_metadata = agent_input.get("metadata", {})


        # Detect tone
        detected_tones = self._detect_tone(self.current_message)
        if detected_tones:
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraManager] Detected tones: {detected_tones}")


        # Extract merchant_id from message if it's just a number
        message = self.current_message.strip()
        if message.isdigit():
            merchant_id = int(message)
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraManager] Detected merchant ID in message: {merchant_id}")
            context_data = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {})
            context_data["merchant_id"] = merchant_id
            agent_input["metadata"]["context_data"] = context_data


        # Extract merchant_id from metadata
        if not agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {}).get("merchant_id"):
            mid = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("merchant_id")
            if mid:
                context_data = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {})
                context_data["merchant_id"] = mid
                agent_input["metadata"]["context_data"] = context_data


        # Attribute engage: if merchant is replying after a proactive followup, log the engage event.
        # on_merchant_reply reads last_followup_sub_tier from the snapshot and is a no-op when empty.
        context_data = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {})
        _mid = str(context_data.get("merchant_id") or self.current_metadata.get("merchant_id") or "")
        if _mid:
            try:
                from agents.vera.followup.dispatch_log import on_merchant_reply
                _sid = agent_input.get("session_id")
                _ticket_id = int(_sid) if _sid and str(_sid).isdigit() else None
                on_merchant_reply(_mid, ticket_id=_ticket_id)
            except Exception:
                pass


        # Handle photo messages
        context_data = agent_input.get("metadata", {}).get("context_data", {})
        photos = context_data.get("photos", [])
        if photos:
            merchant_id = context_data.get("merchant_id", "")
            try:
                processed_results = await asyncio.get_event_loop().run_in_executor(
                    None, self._process_photos_batch, photos, str(merchant_id), context_data
                )
                if processed_results:
                    photo_summary = self._format_photo_summary(processed_results)
                    agent_input['message'] += f"\n\n[Photo Processing Results]\n{photo_summary}"
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"[VeraManager] Error processing photos: {e}")


        return await super().handle_input(agent_input)


    async def _handle_tool_call(self, message: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Override to add anti-repetition + route vera MCP tools."""
        tool_name = message.get("name")
        tool_args = message.get("arguments", {})


        # Increment iteration counter
        self._iteration_count += 1


        # Max iterations check
        if self._iteration_count > self.MAX_AGENT_ITERATIONS:
            self.logger.warning(f"[VeraManager] Max iterations ({self.MAX_AGENT_ITERATIONS}) reached")
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "anti_loop", "max_iterations_reached")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                {"status": "blocked", "reason": "Max iterations reached"}
            )


        # Anti-repetition for communicate_to_user
        if tool_name == "communicate_to_user":
            user_message = tool_args.get("message", "")
            message_hash = hash(user_message[:200])
            if message_hash in self._sent_messages:
                self.logger.warning("[VeraManager] Blocking duplicate message")
                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                    {"status": "already_sent", "message": "Message already sent"}
                )
            self._sent_messages.add(message_hash)


            # Force all_concerns_answered=true
            if "all_concerns_answered" in tool_args:
                tool_args["all_concerns_answered"] = True


        # When running as specialist, capture communicate_to_user as response
        if tool_name == "communicate_to_user" and self._running_as_specialist:
            message_text = tool_args.get("message", "")
            if message_text and not self._specialist_response:
                self._specialist_response = {
                    "status": "resolved",
                    "response": message_text,
                    "query_answered": True
                }
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                {"status": "captured", "message": "Response captured for master agent"}
            )


        # Route vera MCP tools
        if tool_name in self.VERA_MCP_ALLOWED_TOOLS:
            return await self._handle_vera_mcp_tool(tool_name, tool_args)


        # All other tools -> parent
        return await super()._handle_tool_call(message)


    async def _handle_vera_mcp_tool(self, tool_name: str, tool_args: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Call vera-mcp via HTTPMCPClient."""
        try:
            self.logger.info(f"[VeraManager] Calling vera-mcp tool: {tool_name}")
            result = await self.vera_mcp_client.call_tool(tool_name, tool_args)
            # Track actions when running as specialist
            if self._running_as_specialist:
                self._specialist_actions.append({
                    "tool": tool_name,
                    "success": not (isinstance(result, dict) and result.get("status") == "error")
                })
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name, result
            )
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"[VeraManager] vera-mcp tool call failed: {tool_name} - {e}")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id, tool_name,
                {"status": "error", "error": f"Tool call failed: {str(e)}"}
            )


    def _process_photos_batch(self, photos: List[Dict], merchant_id: str, context: Dict) -> List[Dict]:
        """Process batch of photos through enhancement pipeline."""
        if not photos or not merchant_id:
            return []


        MAX_PHOTOS_PER_BATCH = 10
        if len(photos) > MAX_PHOTOS_PER_BATCH:
            photos = photos[:MAX_PHOTOS_PER_BATCH]


        results = []
        merchant_context = {
            'merchant_id': merchant_id,
            'merchant_name': context.get('merchant_name', ''),
            'category': context.get('category', ''),
            'location': context.get('location', '')
        }


        for photo_info in photos:
            try:
                gcs_path = photo_info.get('gcs_path')
                photo_id = photo_info.get('photo_id')
                if not gcs_path or not photo_id:
                    continue


                mime_type = photo_info.get('mime_type', '')
                ALLOWED_IMAGE_TYPES = ['image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/png', 'image/webp']
                if mime_type and mime_type.lower() not in ALLOWED_IMAGE_TYPES:
                    continue


                file_size = photo_info.get('file_size', 0)
                MAX_FILE_SIZE = 10 * 1024 * 1024
                if file_size > MAX_FILE_SIZE:
                    continue


                raw_photo = self.photo_storage.download_photo(gcs_path)
                if not raw_photo:
                    continue


                enhanced_photo, enhancement_metadata = self.photo_enhancer.enhance_photo(raw_photo)
                quality_score, quality_metrics = self.photo_scorer.score_photo(enhanced_photo)


                caption = ""
                if merchant_context.get('merchant_name'):
                    try:
                        caption = self.photo_captioner.generate_caption(
                            enhanced_photo, merchant_context, use_vision=True
                        )
                    except Exception:
                        pass


                enhanced_gcs_path = self.photo_storage.upload_photo(
                    photo_data=enhanced_photo, merchant_id=merchant_id,
                    photo_id=photo_id, photo_type='enhanced',
                    metadata={'quality_score': quality_score, 'caption': caption}
                )


                if enhanced_gcs_path:
                    results.append({
                        'photo_id': photo_id,
                        'enhanced_gcs_path': enhanced_gcs_path,
                        'quality_score': quality_score,
                        'caption': caption,
                        'enhancement_metadata': enhancement_metadata
                    })
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"[VeraManager] Error processing photo: {e}")
                continue
        return results


    def _format_photo_summary(self, results: List[Dict]) -> str:
        """Format photo processing results for LLM context."""
        if not results:
            return "No photos processed successfully."


        summary_lines = [f"Successfully processed {len(results)} photo(s):"]
        for idx, result in enumerate(results, 1):
            score = result.get('quality_score', 0)
            caption = result.get('caption', 'N/A')
            summary_lines.append(f"\nPhoto {idx}:")
            summary_lines.append(f"  - Quality Score: {score:.1f}/100")
            if caption:
                summary_lines.append(f"  - Caption: {caption}")


        avg_score = sum(r.get('quality_score', 0) for r in results) / len(results)
        if avg_score >= 70:
            summary_lines.append(f"\nOverall: Excellent quality (avg {avg_score:.1f}/100) - ready for upload!")
        elif avg_score >= 50:
            summary_lines.append(f"\nOverall: Good quality (avg {avg_score:.1f}/100)")
        else:
            summary_lines.append(f"\nOverall: Acceptable quality (avg {avg_score:.1f}/100) - suggest retaking in better lighting")
        return "\n".join(summary_lines)










- [agents/vera/agent.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/agents/vera/agent.py)


"""
VeraAgent - Google Business Profile Management Agent


AI agent for managing merchant Google Business Profile presence:
- Profile optimization (hours, description, photos)
- Review monitoring and responses
- Insights tracking (views, calls, directions)
- Content creation (Google Posts)


Phase 1: GBP Only (Instagram/Facebook in Phase 2)


Subscription: Rs 499/month via UPI Autopay (cancel anytime)
"""


import os
import logging
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
from agents.base_agent import BaseAgent
from utility.http_mcp_client import HTTPMCPClient
from utility.constants import DEFAULT_VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL
from services.llm import get_llm_provider
from agents.vera.core_prompts import (
    get_vera_system_prompt,
    get_vera_config,
    get_onboarding_prompt,
    get_daily_prompt,
    get_weekly_prompt,
    get_monthly_report_prompt
)


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class VeraAgent(BaseAgent):
    """
    VeraAgent - AI assistant for Google Business Profile management.


    Manages 7k merchant GBP listings via mxconnect@magicpin.in account.


    Capabilities:
    - Profile optimization (hours, description, categories, photos)
    - Review management (monitoring, replies)
    - Content creation (Google Business Posts)
    - Performance insights (views, searches, calls, directions)


    MCP Integration:
    - Uses HTTPMCPClient to connect to Vera MCP server
    - Accesses 8 GBP tools via MCP (list, claim, update, photos, reviews, reply, insights, posts)
    """


    agent_type = "VeraAgent"


    def __init__(self, agent_id: str):
        """
        Initialize VeraAgent.


        Args:
            agent_id: Unique agent identifier
        """
        super().__init__(agent_id)


        # Get configuration
        self.config = get_vera_config()


        # Initialize MCP client for GBP tools (vera-mcp K8s service)
        mcp_server_url = os.getenv(
            'VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL',
            self.config.get('mcp_server_url', DEFAULT_VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL),
        )
        logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Connecting to vera-mcp at: {mcp_server_url}")


        self.mcp_client = HTTPMCPClient(
            server_url=mcp_server_url,
            tool_prefix="",  # No prefix - use original tool names
            timeout=30
        )


        # Discover MCP tools
        try:
            self.mcp_tools = self.mcp_client.get_tools_sync()
            tool_names = [t.get("name", "") for t in self.mcp_tools]
            logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Discovered {len(self.mcp_tools)} tools from {mcp_server_url}: {tool_names[:5]}{'...' if len(tool_names) > 5 else ''}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"[VeraAgent] Failed to discover MCP tools from {mcp_server_url}: {e}", exc_info=True)
            self.mcp_tools = []


        self.logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Initialized with ID {agent_id}")


    def get_tools(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        Get all available tools for VeraAgent.


        Combines base agent tools with GBP MCP tools.


        Returns:
            List of tool definitions in OpenAI function format
        """
        # Get base agent tools (communicate_to_user, etc.)
        base_tools = super().get_tools()


        # Add MCP tools
        all_tools = base_tools + self.mcp_tools


        return all_tools


    def get_system_prompt(self, workflow: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
        """
        Get system prompt for VeraAgent.


        Args:
            workflow: Optional workflow name (onboarding, daily, weekly, monthly_report)


        Returns:
            System prompt string
        """
        base_prompt = get_vera_system_prompt()


        # Add workflow-specific prompt if specified
        if workflow:
            workflow_prompts = {
                "onboarding": get_onboarding_prompt(),
                "daily": get_daily_prompt(),
                "weekly": get_weekly_prompt(),
                "monthly_report": get_monthly_report_prompt()
            }


            workflow_prompt = workflow_prompts.get(workflow, "")
            if workflow_prompt:
                base_prompt += f"\n\n## Current Task\n\n{workflow_prompt}"


        return base_prompt


    async def handle_mcp_tool_call(
        self,
        tool_name: str,
        arguments: Dict[str, Any]
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Handle MCP tool call asynchronously.


        Args:
            tool_name: Name of MCP tool to call
            arguments: Tool arguments


        Returns:
            Tool execution result
        """
        try:
            logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Calling MCP tool: {tool_name} args={arguments}")
            result = await self.mcp_client.call_tool(tool_name, arguments)
            status = result.get("status", "unknown") if isinstance(result, dict) else "ok"
            logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] MCP tool result: {tool_name} -> status={status}")
            return result


        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"[VeraAgent] MCP tool call failed: {tool_name} - {e}", exc_info=True)
            return {
                "status": "error",
                "error": f"Tool call failed: {str(e)}"
            }


    def is_mcp_tool(self, tool_name: str) -> bool:
        """
        Check if a tool is an MCP tool.


        Args:
            tool_name: Tool name to check


        Returns:
            True if tool is from MCP server
        """
        return any(t.get("name") == tool_name for t in self.mcp_tools)


    def process_workflow(
        self,
        workflow: str,
        merchant_id: str,
        merchant_context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
        max_iterations: int = 10
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Process a Vera workflow with full tool-use loop.


        Calls LLM in a loop: LLM decides which tools to call, we execute them,
        feed results back, until LLM produces a final text response (no more tool calls).


        Args:
            workflow: Workflow name (onboarding, daily, weekly, monthly_report)
            merchant_id: Merchant ID
            merchant_context: Optional merchant context (name, location, etc.)
            max_iterations: Safety limit on tool call rounds


        Returns:
            Workflow execution result
        """
        import asyncio
        import json


        logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Processing workflow '{workflow}' for merchant {merchant_id}")


        try:
            # Get workflow-specific system prompt
            system_prompt = self.get_system_prompt(workflow=workflow)


            # Build user message with merchant context
            user_message = f"Execute {workflow} workflow for merchant {merchant_id}."
            if merchant_context:
                context_str = json.dumps(merchant_context, default=str) if isinstance(merchant_context, dict) else str(merchant_context)
                user_message += f"\n\nMerchant Context:\n{context_str}"


            # Prepare messages for LLM
            messages = [
                {"role": "system", "content": system_prompt},
                {"role": "user", "content": user_message}
            ]


            # Get available tools
            tools = self.get_tools()
            model = os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL_NAME", "gpt-4o")
            all_tool_calls = []


            # Tool-use loop: keep calling LLM until it produces a final response
            for iteration in range(max_iterations):
                logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Iteration {iteration + 1}/{max_iterations}")


                response = self.llm_provider.create_response(
                    model=model,
                    messages=messages,
                    tools=tools,
                    temperature=0.7
                )


                # Check if LLM wants to call tools
                tool_calls = getattr(response, 'tool_calls', None)
                if not tool_calls:
                    # No tool calls — LLM has produced its final response
                    final_content = getattr(response, 'content', '') or ''
                    logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Workflow complete after {iteration + 1} iterations")
                    break


                # Process tool calls
                # Add assistant message with tool calls to conversation
                assistant_msg = {"role": "assistant", "content": None, "tool_calls": []}
                for tc in tool_calls:
                    tc_id = tc.get("id", f"call_{iteration}_{len(assistant_msg['tool_calls'])}")
                    assistant_msg["tool_calls"].append({
                        "id": tc_id,
                        "type": "function",
                        "function": tc.get("function", tc)
                    })
                messages.append(assistant_msg)


                # Execute each tool call and add results
                for tc in tool_calls:
                    tc_id = tc.get("id", f"call_{iteration}")
                    func_info = tc.get("function", tc)
                    tool_name = func_info.get("name", "")
                    tool_args_raw = func_info.get("arguments", {})


                    # Parse arguments if string
                    if isinstance(tool_args_raw, str):
                        try:
                            tool_args = json.loads(tool_args_raw)
                        except json.JSONDecodeError:
                            tool_args = {}
                    else:
                        tool_args = tool_args_raw


                    logger.info(f"[VeraAgent] Calling tool: {tool_name}")


                    # Execute tool
                    if self.is_mcp_tool(tool_name):
                        # Use event loop safely
                        try:
                            loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
                        except RuntimeError:
                            loop = None


                        if loop and loop.is_running():
                            # Already in async context — use run_in_executor or nest_asyncio
                            import concurrent.futures
                            with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor() as pool:
                                result = pool.submit(
                                    asyncio.run,
                                    self.handle_mcp_tool_call(tool_name, tool_args)
                                ).result()
                        else:
                            result = asyncio.run(
                                self.handle_mcp_tool_call(tool_name, tool_args)
                            )
                    else:
                        # Handle base agent tools (communicate_to_user, etc.)
                        result = self._execute_base_tool(tool_name, tool_args)


                    all_tool_calls.append({"tool": tool_name, "result": result})


                    # Add tool result to conversation
                    result_str = json.dumps(result, default=str) if isinstance(result, dict) else str(result)
                    messages.append({
                        "role": "tool",
                        "tool_call_id": tc_id,
                        "content": result_str
                    })
            else:
                # Hit max iterations
                logger.warning(f"[VeraAgent] Hit max iterations ({max_iterations}) for workflow '{workflow}'")
                final_content = "Workflow completed (max iterations reached)"


            return {
                "status": "success",
                "workflow": workflow,
                "merchant_id": merchant_id,
                "response": final_content,
                "tool_calls": all_tool_calls,
                "iterations": min(iteration + 1, max_iterations) if 'iteration' in dir() else 0
            }


        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"[VeraAgent] Workflow processing failed: {e}")
            return {
                "status": "error",
                "workflow": workflow,
                "merchant_id": merchant_id,
                "error": str(e)
            }


    def _execute_base_tool(self, tool_name: str, tool_args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Execute a non-MCP base agent tool."""
        try:
            if tool_name == "communicate_to_user":
                message = tool_args.get("message", "")
                self.communicate_to_user(message)
                return {"status": "success", "message_sent": True}
            else:
                return {"status": "error", "error": f"Unknown tool: {tool_name}"}
        except Exception as e:
            return {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}


    def onboard_merchant(
        self,
        merchant_id: str,
        merchant_context: Dict[str, Any]
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Onboard a merchant to Vera GBP management.


        Args:
            merchant_id: Merchant ID
            merchant_context: Merchant details (name, location, category, etc.)


        Returns:
            Onboarding result
        """
        return self.process_workflow(
            workflow="onboarding",
            merchant_id=merchant_id,
            merchant_context=merchant_context
        )


    def daily_review_management(
        self,
        merchant_id: str,
        merchant_context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Execute daily review management for a merchant.


        Args:
            merchant_id: Merchant ID
            merchant_context: Optional merchant context


        Returns:
            Daily workflow result
        """
        return self.process_workflow(
            workflow="daily",
            merchant_id=merchant_id,
            merchant_context=merchant_context
        )


    def weekly_content_creation(
        self,
        merchant_id: str,
        merchant_context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Execute weekly content creation for a merchant.


        Args:
            merchant_id: Merchant ID
            merchant_context: Optional merchant context


        Returns:
            Weekly workflow result
        """
        return self.process_workflow(
            workflow="weekly",
            merchant_id=merchant_id,
            merchant_context=merchant_context
        )


    def monthly_report(
        self,
        merchant_id: str,
        merchant_context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Generate monthly presence report for a merchant.


        Args:
            merchant_id: Merchant ID
            merchant_context: Optional merchant context


        Returns:
            Monthly report result
        """
        return self.process_workflow(
            workflow="monthly_report",
            merchant_id=merchant_id,
            merchant_context=merchant_context
        )
