        self._merchant_id = ""
        self._merchant_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
        self._offers: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
        self._category = ""
        self._merchant_name = ""
        self._merchant_phone = ""
        self._qualification_data: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        self._language = "english"
        self._customer_phone = ""
        self._stage_timeline: List[Dict] = []
        self._lead_handed_off = False
        self._offer_inquiry_mode = False
        self._offer_context: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        self._jd_info: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
        self._turn_count: int = 0
        self._links_merchant_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None  # From vera_get_merchant_by_links


        # Outbound campaign metadata (set from metadata fields, persisted in Redis)
        self._outbound_mode: bool = False
        self._agent_tone: str = "FRIENDLY"
        self._context_dump: str = ""
        self._social_links: Dict[str, str] = {}
        self._campaign: str = ""
        self._template_name: str = ""
        self._customer_profile: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
        self._lead_user_id: str = ""
        self._lead_auth_user_token: str = ""
        self._lead_user_name: str = ""
        self._lead_user_email: str = ""
        self._lead_user_profile: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        self._lead_identity_attempted: bool = False
        self._lead_id: str = ""
        self._lead_sync_snapshot: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        self._lead_last_synced_fingerprint: str = ""


        logger.info("[CI_] Initialized")
        increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "initialization", "success")


    def _state_key(self, session_id: str) -> str:
        return f"{REDIS_STATE_PREFIX}{session_id}"


    def _load_state(self, session_id: str) -> None:
        try:
            raw = self._redis.get(self._state_key(session_id))
            if not raw:
                return
            if isinstance(raw, bytes):
                raw = raw.decode("utf-8")
            state = json.loads(raw)
            self._stage = state.get("stage", "identify")
            self._merchant_id = state.get("merchant_id", "")
            self._merchant_data = state.get("merchant_data")
            self._offers = state.get("offers", [])
            self._category = state.get("category", "")
            self._merchant_name = state.get("merchant_name", "")
            self._merchant_phone = state.get("merchant_phone", "")
            self._qualification_data = state.get("qualification_data", {})
            self._language = state.get("language", "english")
            self._stage_timeline = state.get("stage_timeline", [])
            self._lead_handed_off = state.get("lead_handed_off", False)
            self._offer_inquiry_mode = state.get("offer_inquiry_mode", False)
            self._offer_context = state.get("offer_context", {})
            self._jd_info = state.get("jd_info")
            self._turn_count = state.get("turn_count", 0)
            self._links_merchant_data = state.get("links_merchant_data")
            self._outbound_mode = state.get("outbound_mode", False)
            self._agent_tone = state.get("agent_tone", "FRIENDLY")
            self._context_dump = state.get("context_dump", "")
            self._social_links = state.get("social_links", {})
            self._campaign = state.get("campaign", "")
            self._template_name = state.get("template_name", "")
            self._customer_profile = state.get("customer_profile")
            self._lead_user_id = state.get("lead_user_id", "")
            self._lead_auth_user_token = state.get("lead_auth_user_token", "")
            self._lead_user_name = state.get("lead_user_name", "")
            self._lead_user_email = state.get("lead_user_email", "")
            self._lead_user_profile = state.get("lead_user_profile", {})
            self._lead_identity_attempted = bool(state.get("lead_identity_attempted", False))
            self._lead_id = state.get("lead_id", "")
            self._lead_sync_snapshot = state.get("lead_sync_snapshot", {})
            self._lead_last_synced_fingerprint = state.get("lead_last_synced_fingerprint", "")
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.error("[CI_] Redis load state failed: %s", exc)


    def _save_state(self, session_id: str) -> None:
        try:
            state = {
                "stage": self._stage,
                "merchant_id": self._merchant_id,
                "merchant_data": self._merchant_data,  # Full data — avoids MCP re-fetch every turn
                "offers": self._offers,
                "category": self._category,
                "merchant_name": self._merchant_name,
                "merchant_phone": self._merchant_phone,
                "qualification_data": self._qualification_data,
                "language": self._language,
                "stage_timeline": self._stage_timeline,
                "lead_handed_off": self._lead_handed_off,
                "offer_inquiry_mode": self._offer_inquiry_mode,
                "offer_context": self._offer_context,
                "jd_info": self._jd_info,
                "turn_count": self._turn_count,
                "links_merchant_data": self._links_merchant_data,
                "outbound_mode": self._outbound_mode,
                "agent_tone": self._agent_tone,
                "context_dump": self._context_dump,
                "social_links": self._social_links,
                "campaign": self._campaign,
                "template_name": self._template_name,
                "customer_profile": self._customer_profile,
                "lead_user_id": self._lead_user_id,
                "lead_auth_user_token": self._lead_auth_user_token,
                "lead_user_name": self._lead_user_name,
                "lead_user_email": self._lead_user_email,
                "lead_user_profile": self._lead_user_profile,
                "lead_identity_attempted": self._lead_identity_attempted,
                "lead_id": self._lead_id,
                "lead_sync_snapshot": self._lead_sync_snapshot,
                "lead_last_synced_fingerprint": self._lead_last_synced_fingerprint,
            }
            self._redis.setex(
                self._state_key(session_id),
                REDIS_STATE_TTL,
                json.dumps(state, default=str),
            )
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.error("[CI_] Redis save state failed: %s", exc)


    async def _load_merchant_data(self, merchant_id: str) -> None:
        if self._merchant_data and self._merchant_id == merchant_id:
            # Merchant data cached — still fetch JD info if missing
            if self._jd_info is None:
                try:
                    result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                        "vera_get_merchant_jd_info",
                        {"merchant_id": merchant_id},
                    )
                    jd_data = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
                    crawled = None
                    if isinstance(jd_data, dict):
                        crawled = jd_data.get("crawledResponse") or jd_data.get("data", {}).get("crawledResponse")
                    if crawled:
                        self._jd_info = crawled
                        logger.info("[CI_] JD info loaded (cached path): name=%s", crawled.get("name", "?"))
                except Exception as exc:
                    logger.warning("[CI_] vera_get_merchant_jd_info (cached path) failed: %s", exc)
            return


        self._merchant_id = merchant_id
        logger.info("[CI_] Loading merchant data: %s", merchant_id)
        _merchant_loaded = False


        # Try vera_get_customer_info_pack first (single call, all data)
        try:
            result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                "vera_get_customer_info_pack",
                {"merchant_id": merchant_id},
            )
            data = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
            # info_pack may return {merchant_data: {business_info:...}, offers:...} or {business_info:...}
            inner = data.get("merchant_data", data) if isinstance(data, dict) else data
            has_biz = (isinstance(data, dict) and data.get("business_info")) or (isinstance(inner, dict) and inner.get("business_info"))
            if isinstance(data, dict) and data.get("status") != "error" and has_biz:
                self._merchant_data = inner
                self._offers = data.get("offers", [])
                biz = self._merchant_data.get("business_info", {})
                self._merchant_name = biz.get("name", "")
                self._category = biz.get("category", biz.get("primary_type", ""))
                if not self._category:
                    self._category = self._resolve_category_from_types(biz)
                self._merchant_phone = biz.get("phone", biz.get("formatted_phone_number", ""))
                logger.info("[CI_] Loaded via info_pack: %s", self._merchant_name)
                _merchant_loaded = True
            else:
                logger.info("[CI_] info_pack returned empty/error, falling back")
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.warning("[CI_] vera_get_customer_info_pack failed: %s", exc)


        if not _merchant_loaded:
            # Fallback: get_unassociated_merchant_data
            try:
                result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                    "get_unassociated_merchant_data",
                    {"merchant_id": merchant_id},
                )
                data = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
                if isinstance(data, dict) and data.get("status") != "error":
                    self._merchant_data = data
                    biz = data.get("business_info", {})
                    self._merchant_name = biz.get("name", "")
                    self._category = biz.get("category", biz.get("primary_type", ""))
                    if not self._category:
                        self._category = self._resolve_category_from_types(biz)
                    self._merchant_phone = biz.get("phone", biz.get("formatted_phone_number", ""))
                    logger.info("[CI_] Loaded via unassociated_data: %s", self._merchant_name)
            except Exception as exc:
                logger.warning("[CI_] get_unassociated_merchant_data failed: %s", exc)


            # Load offers separately (only needed when info_pack didn't supply them)
            try:
                result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                    "vera_list_merchant_offers",
                    {"merchant_id": merchant_id},
                )
                offers_data = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
                if isinstance(offers_data, list):
                    self._offers = offers_data
                elif isinstance(offers_data, dict):
                    self._offers = offers_data.get("offers", [])
            except Exception as exc:
                logger.warning("[CI_] vera_list_merchant_offers failed: %s", exc)


        # Load JD business info (supplemental — may return empty/error, non-blocking)
        try:
            result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                "vera_get_merchant_jd_info",
                {"merchant_id": merchant_id},
            )
            jd_data = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
            crawled = None
            if isinstance(jd_data, dict):
                crawled = jd_data.get("crawledResponse") or jd_data.get("data", {}).get("crawledResponse")
            if crawled:
                self._jd_info = crawled
                logger.info("[CI_] JD info loaded: name=%s", crawled.get("name", "?"))
            else:
                logger.info("[CI_] JD info empty/unavailable for mid=%s", merchant_id)
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.warning("[CI_] vera_get_merchant_jd_info failed: %s", exc)


    async def _load_offer_details(self, offer_id: str) -> None:
        """Fetch rich offer data via vera_get_posted_offer_by_id and store in offer_context."""
        if not offer_id or offer_id.lower() in ("", "tempid"):
            logger.info("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] skipped: offer_id empty or tempid (offer_id=%s)", offer_id)
            return
        if self._offer_context.get("offer_details"):
            logger.info("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] skipped: already cached for oid=%s", offer_id)
            return
        logger.info("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] invoking vera_get_posted_offer_by_id request offer_id=%s", offer_id)
        try:
            result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                "vera_get_posted_offer_by_id",
                {"offer_id": offer_id},
            )
            logger.info("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] raw_response repr=%s", repr(str(result)[:500]))
            data = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
            logger.info("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] parsed_data keys=%s", list(data.keys()) if isinstance(data, dict) else type(data).__name__)
            # After unwrapping: {"offer_id": ..., "merchant_id": ..., "suggestion": {...}}
            if isinstance(data, dict):
                suggestion = data.get("suggestion", {})
                if suggestion:
                    self._offer_context["offer_details"] = suggestion
                    logger.info(
                        "[CI_OFFER_TOOL] SUCCESS oid=%s title=%s value=%s end_date=%s pitch=%s",
                        offer_id,
                        suggestion.get("title", "?"),
                        suggestion.get("value", "?"),
                        suggestion.get("end_date", "?"),
                        repr(suggestion.get("merchant_pitch", "")[:100]),
                    )
                else:
                    logger.warning("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] EMPTY suggestion for oid=%s full_data=%s", offer_id, data)
            else:
                logger.warning("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] UNEXPECTED shape oid=%s type=%s data=%s", offer_id, type(data).__name__, repr(str(data)[:300]))
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.warning("[CI_OFFER_TOOL] FAILED oid=%s error=%s", offer_id, exc)


    async def _load_merchant_by_links(self) -> None:
        """Fetch merchant context from JD / Google links via vera_get_merchant_by_links.


        Used in outbound mode when merchant provides their JD/Google listing URLs.
        Data is cached in _links_merchant_data for the session lifetime.
        """
        if self._links_merchant_data is not None:
            return  # Already loaded


        jd_url = self._social_links.get("justdial", "")
        google_url = self._social_links.get("google", "")
        if not jd_url and not google_url:
            return  # Nothing to fetch


        args: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if jd_url:
            args["justdial_url"] = jd_url
        if google_url:
            args["google_url"] = google_url


        try:
            result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                "vera_get_merchant_by_links",
                args,
            )
            data = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
            if isinstance(data, dict) and data.get("status") != "error":
                self._links_merchant_data = data
                logger.info(
                    "[CI_LINKS] merchant_by_links loaded: jd=%s google=%s keys=%s",
                    bool(jd_url), bool(google_url),
                    list(data.keys())[:6],
                )
            else:
                logger.info("[CI_LINKS] merchant_by_links returned no usable data: %s", data)
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.warning("[CI_LINKS] vera_get_merchant_by_links failed: %s", exc)


    async def _load_customer_profile(self, merchant_id: str, customer_phone: str) -> None:
        """Fetch CRM profile for this customer+merchant pair via vera_get_customer_merchant_profile.


        Non-blocking — failure means no profile context, not a hard error.
        """
        if self._customer_profile is not None:
            return  # Already loaded this session ({} means attempted but no profile)
        if not merchant_id or not customer_phone:
            return


        # Strip country prefix for cleaner log, pass full number to MCP
        _phone_clean = customer_phone.lstrip("+")
        try:
            raw_result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                "vera_get_customer_merchant_profile",
                {"merchant_id": merchant_id, "customer_phone": _phone_clean},
            )
            logger.info(
                "[CI_PROFILE] raw_result: mid=%s phone=%s status=%s keys=%s",
                merchant_id, _phone_clean,
                raw_result.get("status") if isinstance(raw_result, dict) else type(raw_result).__name__,
                list(raw_result.keys()) if isinstance(raw_result, dict) else "n/a",
            )
            # Guardrail hit: tool not registered on MCP server yet
            if isinstance(raw_result, dict) and raw_result.get("status") == "skipped":
                # Negative cache to avoid repeated retries every turn.
                self._customer_profile = {}
                logger.warning(
                    "[CI_PROFILE] GUARDRAIL BLOCKED: vera_get_customer_merchant_profile not found on MCP server. "
                    "Tool may not be deployed yet. mid=%s phone=%s error=%s",
                    merchant_id, _phone_clean, raw_result.get("error"),
                )
                return


            data = self._parse_mcp_result(raw_result)
            logger.info(
                "[CI_PROFILE] parsed_data: type=%s status=%s has_phone=%s",
                type(data).__name__,
                data.get("status") if isinstance(data, dict) else "n/a",
                bool(data.get("phone")) if isinstance(data, dict) else False,
            )
            if isinstance(data, dict) and data.get("status") not in ("error", "skipped") and data.get("phone"):
                self._customer_profile = data
                logger.info(
                    "[CI_PROFILE] loaded: mid=%s phone=%s name=%s segment=%s tags=%s",
                    merchant_id, _phone_clean,
                    data.get("name", "?"), data.get("segment", "?"),
                    data.get("tags", []),
                )
                # Pre-fill qualification data from profile (only if not already collected)
                if not self._qualification_data.get("customer_name") and data.get("name"):
                    self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = data["name"]
                    logger.info("[CI_PROFILE] pre-filled customer_name from profile: %s", data["name"])
                # Override language from profile preferred_language if not yet set explicitly
                if data.get("preferred_language"):
                    _ISO_LANG = {
                        "ENGLISH": "english", "HINDI": "hindi", "HINGLISH": "hinglish",
                        "MARATHI": "marathi", "TAMIL": "tamil", "TELUGU": "telugu", "KANNADA": "kannada",
                    }
                    _prof_lang = _ISO_LANG.get(data["preferred_language"].upper(), "")
                    if _prof_lang:
                        self._language = _prof_lang
                        logger.info("[CI_PROFILE] language set from profile: %s", _prof_lang)
            else:
                # Negative cache to avoid repeated retries every turn.
                self._customer_profile = {}
                logger.warning(
                    "[CI_PROFILE] no usable profile: mid=%s phone=%s status=%s has_phone=%s raw_data=%s",
                    merchant_id, _phone_clean,
                    data.get("status") if isinstance(data, dict) else "n/a",
                    bool(data.get("phone")) if isinstance(data, dict) else False,
                    repr(str(data)[:300]),
                )
        except Exception as exc:
            # Negative cache to avoid repeated retries every turn.
            self._customer_profile = {}
            logger.warning("[CI_PROFILE] vera_get_customer_merchant_profile failed: mid=%s phone=%s error=%s", merchant_id, _phone_clean, exc)


    @staticmethod
    def _parse_mcp_result(result: Any) -> Any:
        """Unwrap MCP result envelope."""
        if not isinstance(result, dict):
            return result
        if result.get("status") == "error":
            return result
        data = result.get("data", result)
        if isinstance(data, str):
            try:
                data = json.loads(data)
            except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
                return data
        if isinstance(data, dict) and "data" in data and "status" in data:
            return CustomerIncomingAgent._parse_mcp_result(data)
        return data


    @staticmethod
    def _resolve_category_from_types(biz_info: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        """Extract category from GBP types array when category field is empty."""
        types = biz_info.get("types", [])
        # Skip generic types; prefer specific business types
        skip = {"point_of_interest", "establishment", "political", "locality"}
        for t in types:
            if t and t not in skip:
                return t.replace("_", " ")
        return ""


    def _advance_stage(self, merchant_id_known: bool = False, lead_registered: bool = False,
                       has_customer_message: bool = False) -> str:
        current = self._stage


        if current == "identify" and merchant_id_known:
            self._stage = "greet"
        elif current == "greet" and (self._merchant_data or self._links_merchant_data):
            self._stage = "assist_qualify"
        elif current == "assist_qualify":
            if lead_registered:
                self._stage = "handoff"
        elif current == "handoff" and lead_registered:
            self._stage = "closed"
        elif current == "closed" and has_customer_message:
            # Customer sent a new message after close — reopen to keep answering
            self._stage = "assist_qualify"


        if self._stage != current:
            logger.info("[CI_] Stage: %s → %s", current, self._stage)
            self._stage_timeline.append({
                "from": current, "to": self._stage,
                "trigger": f"mid={merchant_id_known} lr={lead_registered} cm={has_customer_message}",
                "at": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
            })
            # Cap timeline at 20 entries
            if len(self._stage_timeline) > 20:
                self._stage_timeline = self._stage_timeline[-20:]


        return self._stage


    def _get_system_prompt(self) -> str:
        """Build stage-specific system prompt."""
        _oc = self._offer_context if self._offer_inquiry_mode else None
        logger.info(
            "[CI_PROMPT_CTX] session=%s offer_inquiry_mode=%s offer_context_passed=%s "
            "offer_details_present=%s title=%s end_date=%s",
            getattr(self, "current_session_id", "?"),
            self._offer_inquiry_mode,
            bool(_oc),
            bool((_oc or {}).get("offer_details")),
            (_oc or {}).get("offer_title", "?"),
            ((_oc or {}).get("offer_details") or {}).get("end_date", "?"),
        )
        prompt = get_customer_incoming_prompt(
            stage=self._stage,
            merchant_id=self._merchant_id,
            merchant_name=self._merchant_name,
            category=self._category,
            merchant_data=self._merchant_data,
            offers=self._offers,
            qualification_data=self._qualification_data,
            customer_phone=getattr(self, "_customer_phone", ""),
            language=self._language,
            offer_context=self._offer_context if self._offer_inquiry_mode else None,
            jd_info=self._jd_info,
            turn_count=self._turn_count,
            outbound_mode=self._outbound_mode,
            agent_tone=self._agent_tone,
            context_dump=self._context_dump,
            social_links=self._social_links,
            campaign=self._campaign,
            links_merchant_data=self._links_merchant_data,
            customer_profile=self._customer_profile,
        )
        if self.current_session_id:
            state_key = self._qualification_state_key(self.current_session_id)
            prompt += (
                "\n\nTOOL STATE KEY (MANDATORY FOR update_qualification_data):\n"
                f"- state_key: {state_key}\n"
                "- Always pass this exact state_key in every update_qualification_data call."
            )
        return prompt


    @staticmethod
    def _qualification_state_key(session_id: str) -> str:
        return f"{CI_QUAL_STATE_PREFIX}{session_id}"


    def get_tools(self) -> List[Dict]:
        """Return base tools + agent tools + allowlisted vera-mcp tools."""
        base_tools = super().get_tools()
        # Override communicate_to_user description for customer-concierge context
        for tool in base_tools:
            if tool.get("name") == "communicate_to_user":
                tool["description"] = (
                    "Send a message to the customer via WhatsApp. Keep messages concise (2-3 lines). "
                    "Be friendly and helpful. You represent the merchant, not magicpin or Vera. "
                    "Never mention Vera, Google Business Profile, or subscriptions."
                )
                break


        provider_name = ""
        try:
            provider_name = (self.llm_provider.get_provider_name() or "").lower()
        except Exception:
            provider_name = ""
        is_agent_gateway = provider_name == "agent_gateway"


        tools = list(base_tools)
        # Agent-local tools are not usable by AGENT_GATEWAY (gateway executes only MCP tools).
        if not is_agent_gateway:
            tools.extend([REGISTER_QUALIFIED_LEAD_TOOL, FETCH_MERCHANT_DATA_TOOL])
        existing_names = {t.get("name") for t in tools if isinstance(t, dict)}


        # Add allowlisted vera-mcp tools (MerchantAgent style: discover + filter).
        if self._vera_mcp_tools_cache:
            for tool in self._vera_mcp_tools_cache:
                name = tool.get("name", "")
                if name in self.ALLOWED_VERA_MCP_TOOLS and name not in existing_names:
                    # Preserve rich tool-calling guidance for qualification updates,
                    # even when the schema source is MCP.
                    if name == "update_qualification_data":
                        tool = {
                            **tool,
                            "description": UPDATE_QUALIFICATION_TOOL.get("description", tool.get("description", "")),
                            "parameters": UPDATE_QUALIFICATION_TOOL.get("parameters", tool.get("parameters", {})),
                        }
                    tools.append(tool)
                    existing_names.add(name)
        else:
            # Fallback while cache is cold (non-gateway providers only).
            if not is_agent_gateway and "update_qualification_data" not in existing_names:
                tools.append(UPDATE_QUALIFICATION_TOOL)


        if (
            self._offer_inquiry_mode
            and not is_agent_gateway
            and "vera_publish_offer_from_chat" not in existing_names
        ):
            tools.append(VERA_PUBLISH_OFFER_TOOL)
        return tools


    async def _prefetch_mcp_tools(self) -> None:
        """Discover vera-mcp tool schemas so get_tools can expose allowlisted tools."""
        if self._vera_mcp_tools_cache is not None:
            return
        try:
            await self._vera_mcp_client.get_tools()
            allowed = set(self.ALLOWED_VERA_MCP_TOOLS)
            if self._offer_inquiry_mode:
                allowed.add("vera_publish_offer_from_chat")
            self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = self._vera_mcp_client.filter_allowed_tools(sorted(allowed))
            logger.info("[CI_] Discovered %d vera-mcp tools", len(self._vera_mcp_tools_cache))
        except Exception as exc:
            # Keep as None so the next turn retries discovery.
            self._vera_mcp_tools_cache = None
            logger.warning("[CI_] Failed to discover vera-mcp tools: %s", exc)


    async def _handle_tool_call(self, message: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Intercept agent-specific tools before delegating to parent."""
        tool_name = message.get("name", "")
        tool_args = message.get("arguments", {})
        logger.info("[CI_TOOL] tool=%s args=%s", tool_name, json.dumps(tool_args, default=str)[:200])


        if tool_name == "register_qualified_lead":
            return await self._handle_register_lead(tool_args)


        if tool_name == "update_qualification_data":
            return await self._handle_update_qualification(tool_args)


        if tool_name == "fetch_merchant_data":
            return await self._handle_fetch_merchant_data(tool_args)


        if tool_name == "vera_publish_offer_from_chat":
            result = await self._handle_mcp_tool(tool_name, tool_args)
            logger.info("[CI_PUBLISH_OFFER] session=%s response=%s", self.current_session_id, json.dumps(result, default=str)[:500])
            return result


        # Vera MCP tools (if any slip through)
        if tool_name in ("vera_get_customer_info_pack", "get_unassociated_merchant_data", "vera_list_merchant_offers"):
            return await self._handle_mcp_tool(tool_name, tool_args)


        return await super()._handle_tool_call(message)


    def _merge_qualification_data(self, updates: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[str]:
        """Merge qualification fields into session state and return updated field names."""
        updatable = ("service_interest", "visit_date", "party_size", "preferred_time", "urgency", "notes")
        updated = []
        for field in updatable:
            value = (updates.get(field) or "").strip()
            if not value:
                continue
            existing = (self._qualification_data.get(field) or "").strip()
            merged_value = value
            if field == "service_interest" and existing and value.lower() not in existing.lower():
                # Append new services rather than overwrite
                merged_value = f"{existing}, {value}"
            elif field == "service_interest" and existing and existing.lower() in value.lower():
                # New value is richer/superset of existing
                merged_value = value
            elif field == "notes":
                merged_value = self._merge_notes(existing, value)


            if merged_value != existing:
                self._qualification_data[field] = merged_value
                updated.append(field)
        return updated


    async def _handle_update_qualification(self, tool_args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Call MCP update_qualification_data tool, then merge normalized fields locally."""
        updates = dict(tool_args or {})
        if not updates.get("state_key") and self.current_session_id:
            updates["state_key"] = self._qualification_state_key(self.current_session_id)
        try:
            raw = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool("update_qualification_data", updates)
            parsed = self._parse_mcp_result(raw)
            if isinstance(parsed, dict):
                normalized = parsed.get("normalized")
                if isinstance(normalized, dict):
                    updates = normalized
                elif isinstance(parsed.get("updates"), dict):
                    updates = parsed["updates"]
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "update_qualification_data", "success")
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.warning("[CI_QUAL_UPDATE] MCP tool failed, falling back to raw args: %s", exc)
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "update_qualification_data", "error")


        updated = self._merge_qualification_data(updates)
        if updated:
            self._qualification_data["lead_score"] = self._calculate_lead_score()
            logger.info(
                "[CI_QUAL_UPDATE] session=%s updated=%s score=%s data=%s",
                self.current_session_id, updated, self._qualification_data["lead_score"],
                json.dumps({k: self._qualification_data[k] for k in updated}, default=str),
            )


        return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
            self.current_session_id,
            "update_qualification_data",
            {"status": "saved", "updated_fields": updated, "lead_score": self._qualification_data.get("lead_score", "cool")},
        )


    async def _pull_qualification_state_from_mcp(self, session_id: str) -> None:
        """Fetch latest qualification state persisted via MCP/gateway and merge locally."""
        if not session_id:
            return
        state_key = self._qualification_state_key(session_id)
        try:
            raw = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(
                "vera_get_qualification_state",
                {"state_key": state_key},
            )
            parsed = self._parse_mcp_result(raw)
            if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
                return
            qualification = parsed.get("qualification_data")
            if not isinstance(qualification, dict):
                return
            updated = self._merge_qualification_data(qualification)
            if updated:
                self._qualification_data["lead_score"] = self._calculate_lead_score()
                logger.info(
                    "[CI_QUAL_PULL] session=%s updated=%s state_key=%s",
                    session_id,
                    updated,
                    state_key,
                )
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.warning("[CI_QUAL_PULL] failed session=%s state_key=%s error=%s", session_id, state_key, exc)


    def _get_lead_init_source(self) -> str:
        """Resolve leads/init source (fixed to google for all sync calls)."""
        return CI_LEAD_INIT_SOURCE


    def _bootstrap_customer_identity(self) -> None:
        """Fetch/capture high-value user identity once per session using noOtp."""
        if not self._customer_phone:
            return


        # Skip repeated noOtp calls once we have identity or already attempted this session.
        if (self._lead_user_id and self._lead_auth_user_token) or self._lead_identity_attempted:
            if not self._qualification_data.get("customer_name") and self._lead_user_name:
                self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = self._lead_user_name
                self._qualification_data.pop("name_asked_count", None)
            return


        self._lead_identity_attempted = True
        identity = login_or_create_user_identity(
            customer_phone=self._customer_phone,
            existing_user_id=self._lead_user_id,
            existing_auth_user_token=self._lead_auth_user_token,
        )
        if identity.get("status") != "success":
            logger.warning(
                "[CI_IDENTITY] noOtp identity fetch failed phone=%s error=%s",
                self._customer_phone,
                identity.get("error", "unknown"),
            )
            return


        self._lead_user_id = str(identity.get("user_id") or self._lead_user_id or "").strip()
        self._lead_auth_user_token = str(
            identity.get("auth_user_token") or self._lead_auth_user_token or ""
        ).strip()
        self._lead_user_name = str(identity.get("name") or self._lead_user_name or "").strip()
        self._lead_user_email = str(identity.get("email") or self._lead_user_email or "").strip()
        profile = identity.get("profile")
        if isinstance(profile, dict) and profile:
            self._lead_user_profile = profile


        if not self._qualification_data.get("customer_name") and self._lead_user_name:
            self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = self._lead_user_name
            self._qualification_data.pop("name_asked_count", None)


        logger.info(
            "[CI_IDENTITY] captured user identity phone=%s user_id=%s token_present=%s name_present=%s",
            self._customer_phone,
            self._lead_user_id,
            bool(self._lead_auth_user_token),
            bool(self._lead_user_name),
        )


    @staticmethod
    def _merge_csv_values(existing: str, new: str) -> str:
        """Merge comma-separated values while preserving order and uniqueness."""
        merged: List[str] = []
        seen = set()
        for raw in (existing, new):
            for part in str(raw or "").split(","):
                token = part.strip()
                if not token:
                    continue
                key = token.lower()
                if key in seen:
                    continue
                seen.add(key)
                merged.append(token)
        return ", ".join(merged)


    @staticmethod
    def _merge_notes(existing: str, new: str) -> str:
        """Merge notes while avoiding duplicated/replayed content."""
        existing_norm = str(existing or "").strip()
        new_norm = str(new or "").strip()
        if not existing_norm:
            return new_norm
        if not new_norm:
            return existing_norm


        existing_l = existing_norm.lower()
        new_l = new_norm.lower()
        if new_l == existing_l or new_l in existing_l:
            return existing_norm
        if existing_l in new_l:
            return new_norm
        return f"{existing_norm}; {new_norm}"


    @staticmethod
    def _is_plausible_customer_name(name: str) -> bool:
        """Heuristic guard so intent phrases are not captured as names."""
        candidate = str(name or "").strip()
        if not candidate:
            return False
        if len(candidate) > 40:
            return False
        if re.search(r"\d", candidate):
            return False


        words = [w for w in re.split(r"\s+", candidate) if w]
        if not (1 <= len(words) <= 4):
            return False


        lower = candidate.lower()
        non_name_markers = {
            "stay", "hostel", "pg", "room", "sharing", "double", "triple",
            "today", "tomorrow", "monday", "tuesday", "wednesday", "thursday",
            "friday", "saturday", "sunday", "week", "month", "year",
            "visit", "booking", "book", "enquiry", "inquiry", "interested",
            "looking", "need", "want", "price", "cost",
        }
        if any(marker in lower for marker in non_name_markers):
            return False


        # Allow alphabets + common punctuation used in names.
        if not re.match(r"^[A-Za-z\u0900-\u097F][A-Za-z\u0900-\u097F\s\.\-']*$", candidate):
            return False
        return True


    @classmethod
    def _extract_customer_name_from_notes(cls, notes: str) -> str:
        """Parse `Customer name: X` style fragments from notes."""
        text = str(notes or "")
        matches = re.findall(
            r"(?:customer\s*name\s*[:\-]\s*)([A-Za-z\u0900-\u097F][A-Za-z\u0900-\u097F\s\-']{0,38})(?=[\.;,\n]|$)",
            text,
            flags=re.IGNORECASE,
        )
        for candidate in reversed(matches):
            c = candidate.strip(" .;,\n\t")
            if cls._is_plausible_customer_name(c):
                return c
        return ""


    @staticmethod
    def _pick_hottest_lead_score(existing: str, current: str) -> str:
        rank = {"cool": 1, "warm": 2, "hot": 3}
        e = str(existing or "").strip().lower()
        c = str(current or "").strip().lower()
        if rank.get(c, 0) >= rank.get(e, 0):
            return c or e or "cool"
        return e or c or "cool"


    @staticmethod
    def _is_generic_user_ask(user_ask: str) -> bool:
        return str(user_ask or "").strip().lower() in ("", "general enquiry")


    @staticmethod
    def _is_generic_lead_summary(summary: str) -> bool:
        return str(summary or "").strip().lower() in ("", "customer reached out with an enquiry")


    @staticmethod
    def _normalize_for_lead_fingerprint(value: Any) -> Any:
        if isinstance(value, dict):
            normalized = {}
            for key in sorted(value.keys()):
                normalized[str(key)] = CustomerIncomingAgent._normalize_for_lead_fingerprint(value[key])
            return normalized
        if isinstance(value, list):
            return [CustomerIncomingAgent._normalize_for_lead_fingerprint(item) for item in value]
        if isinstance(value, str):
            return value.strip()
        return value


    def _build_lead_sync_fingerprint(self, payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        fingerprint_payload = {
            "merchant_id": payload.get("merchant_id", ""),
            "customer_phone": payload.get("customer_phone", ""),
            "customer_name": payload.get("customer_name", ""),
            "offer_id": payload.get("offer_id", ""),
            "offer_title": payload.get("offer_title", ""),
            "source": payload.get("source", ""),
            "service_interest": payload.get("service_interest", ""),
            "visit_date": payload.get("visit_date", ""),
            "party_size": payload.get("party_size", ""),
            "lead_score": payload.get("lead_score", ""),
            "notes": payload.get("notes", ""),
            "context_id": payload.get("context_id", ""),
            "lead_summary": payload.get("lead_summary", ""),
            "user_ask": payload.get("user_ask", ""),
            "qualification_data": payload.get("qualification_data", {}),
        }
        normalized = self._normalize_for_lead_fingerprint(fingerprint_payload)
        serialized = json.dumps(normalized, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":"), ensure_ascii=False, default=str)
        return hashlib.sha256(serialized.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()


    def _build_lead_sync_payload(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Build a merge-safe leads/init payload so previously captured data is never dropped."""
        snapshot = self._lead_sync_snapshot if isinstance(self._lead_sync_snapshot, dict) else {}
        snapshot_qual = snapshot.get("qualification_data")
        snapshot_qual = snapshot_qual if isinstance(snapshot_qual, dict) else {}


        current_qual = {k: v for k, v in self._qualification_data.items() if v and k != "name_asked_count"}
        merged_qual: Dict[str, Any] = dict(snapshot_qual)
        merged_qual.update(current_qual)


        service_interest = self._merge_csv_values(
            str(snapshot.get("service_interest", "")),
            str(current_qual.get("service_interest", "")),
        )
        if not service_interest:
            service_interest = str(merged_qual.get("service_interest", "")).strip()
        if service_interest:
            merged_qual["service_interest"] = service_interest


        notes = str(merged_qual.get("notes", "")).strip()
        preferred_time = str(merged_qual.get("preferred_time", "")).strip()
        if preferred_time and preferred_time not in notes:
            notes = self._merge_notes(notes, f"preferred_time: {preferred_time}")
        if notes:
            merged_qual["notes"] = notes


        customer_name = str(merged_qual.get("customer_name") or snapshot.get("customer_name", "")).strip()
        if not self._is_plausible_customer_name(customer_name):
            note_name = self._extract_customer_name_from_notes(notes)
            if note_name:
                customer_name = note_name
            elif self._is_plausible_customer_name(self._lead_user_name):
                customer_name = self._lead_user_name.strip()
        if customer_name:
            merged_qual["customer_name"] = customer_name
            self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = customer_name


        visit_date = str(merged_qual.get("visit_date") or snapshot.get("visit_date", "")).strip()
        party_size = str(merged_qual.get("party_size") or snapshot.get("party_size", "")).strip()


        lead_score = self._pick_hottest_lead_score(snapshot.get("lead_score", ""), self._calculate_lead_score())
        self._qualification_data["lead_score"] = lead_score
        # Keep qualificationData.lead_score aligned with root leadScore in leads/init payload.
        merged_qual["lead_score"] = lead_score


        context_id_current = str(self.current_source_session_id or self.current_session_id or "").strip()
        context_id = context_id_current or str(snapshot.get("context_id", "")).strip()


        lead_summary_current = self._build_lead_summary()
        lead_summary_existing = str(snapshot.get("lead_summary", "")).strip()
        if self._is_generic_lead_summary(lead_summary_current) and lead_summary_existing:
            lead_summary = lead_summary_existing
        else:
            lead_summary = lead_summary_current or lead_summary_existing


        user_ask_current = self._build_user_ask()
        user_ask_existing = str(snapshot.get("user_ask", "")).strip()
        if self._is_generic_user_ask(user_ask_current) and user_ask_existing:
            user_ask = user_ask_existing
        else:
            user_ask = user_ask_current or user_ask_existing


        offer_id = str((self._offer_context or {}).get("offer_id", "") or snapshot.get("offer_id", "")).strip()
        offer_title = str((self._offer_context or {}).get("offer_title", "") or snapshot.get("offer_title", "")).strip()
        if not offer_title:
            offer_title = service_interest


        payload = {
            "merchant_id": self._merchant_id,
            "offer_id": offer_id,
            "offer_title": offer_title,
            "customer_name": customer_name,
            "customer_phone": self._customer_phone,
            "visit_date": visit_date,
            "party_size": party_size,
            "source": self._get_lead_init_source(),
            "service_interest": service_interest,
            "lead_score": lead_score,
            "notes": notes,
            "context_id": context_id,
            "lead_summary": lead_summary,
            "user_ask": user_ask,
            "qualification_data": merged_qual,
        }
        self._lead_sync_snapshot = {
            **payload,
            "qualification_data": dict(merged_qual),
        }
        return payload


    def _sync_lead_init(self, reason: str, require_signal: bool = False) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Create/update lead through register_lead (create-user + leads/init)."""
        if not self._merchant_id or not self._customer_phone:
            return {"status": "skipped", "reason": "missing_merchant_or_phone"}


        payload = self._build_lead_sync_payload()
        fingerprint = self._build_lead_sync_fingerprint(payload)
        if self._lead_last_synced_fingerprint and fingerprint == self._lead_last_synced_fingerprint:
            logger.info(
                "[CI_LEAD_INIT] reason=%s skipped unchanged payload mid=%s phone=%s lead_id=%s",
                reason,
                self._merchant_id,
                self._customer_phone,
                self._lead_id,
            )
            return {
                "status": "skipped",
                "reason": "unchanged_payload",
                "lead_id": self._lead_id,
                "user_id": self._lead_user_id,
            }
        if require_signal and not (payload.get("service_interest") or payload.get("visit_date") or payload.get("party_size")):
            return {"status": "skipped", "reason": "insufficient_qualification"}


        logger.info(
            "[CI_LEAD_INIT] reason=%s mid=%s phone=%s source=%s has_existing_user=%s score=%s",
            reason,
            self._merchant_id,
            self._customer_phone,
            payload["source"],
            bool(self._lead_user_id),
            payload["lead_score"],
        )
        try:
            result = register_lead(
                merchant_id=payload["merchant_id"],
                offer_id=payload["offer_id"],
                offer_title=payload["offer_title"],
                customer_name=payload["customer_name"],
                customer_phone=payload["customer_phone"],
                visit_date=payload["visit_date"],
                party_size=payload["party_size"],
                source=payload["source"],
                service_interest=payload["service_interest"],
                lead_score=payload["lead_score"],
                notes=payload["notes"],
                context_id=payload["context_id"],
                lead_summary=payload["lead_summary"],
                user_ask=payload["user_ask"],
                qualification_data=payload["qualification_data"],
                existing_user_id=self._lead_user_id,
                existing_auth_user_token=self._lead_auth_user_token,
                existing_user_name=self._lead_user_name,
                existing_user_email=self._lead_user_email,
            )
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.error("[CI_LEAD_INIT] reason=%s failed: %s", reason, exc)
            return {"status": "error", "error": str(exc), "reason": reason}


        if result.get("status") == "success":
            self._lead_user_id = str(result.get("user_id") or self._lead_user_id or "")
            self._lead_auth_user_token = str(
                result.get("auth_user_token") or self._lead_auth_user_token or ""
            )
            self._lead_user_name = str(result.get("user_name") or self._lead_user_name or "")
            self._lead_user_email = str(result.get("user_email") or self._lead_user_email or "")
            profile = result.get("user_profile")
            if isinstance(profile, dict) and profile:
                self._lead_user_profile = profile
            if not self._qualification_data.get("customer_name") and self._lead_user_name:
                self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = self._lead_user_name
                self._qualification_data.pop("name_asked_count", None)
            self._lead_id = str(result.get("lead_id") or self._lead_id or "")
            self._lead_last_synced_fingerprint = fingerprint
            logger.info(
                "[CI_LEAD_INIT] reason=%s success user_id=%s lead_id=%s source=%s",
                reason,
                self._lead_user_id,
                self._lead_id,
                payload["source"],
            )
        else:
            logger.warning(
                "[CI_LEAD_INIT] reason=%s non-success status=%s error=%s",
                reason,
                result.get("status"),
                result.get("error"),
            )
        return result


    async def _handle_register_lead(self, tool_args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Register lead via API and notify merchant."""
        logger.info(
            "[CI_LEAD] register_qualified_lead called: mid=%s name=%s interest=%s date=%s party=%s phone=%s",
            self._merchant_id, tool_args.get("customer_name"), tool_args.get("service_interest"),
            tool_args.get("visit_date"), tool_args.get("party_size"), getattr(self, "_customer_phone", ""),
        )
        customer_name = tool_args.get("customer_name", "")
        service_interest = tool_args.get("service_interest", "")
        visit_date = tool_args.get("visit_date", "")
        party_size = tool_args.get("party_size", "")
        notes = tool_args.get("notes", "")


        # Merge into qualification data — never overwrite accumulated service_interest
        if customer_name:
            self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = customer_name
        if service_interest:
            existing_interest = (self._qualification_data.get("service_interest") or "").strip()
            if existing_interest and service_interest.lower() not in existing_interest.lower():
                self._qualification_data["service_interest"] = f"{existing_interest}, {service_interest}"
            elif not existing_interest:
                self._qualification_data["service_interest"] = service_interest
            # else: LLM-passed value is subset of what's already accumulated — keep accumulated
        if visit_date:
            self._qualification_data["visit_date"] = visit_date
        if party_size:
            self._qualification_data["party_size"] = party_size
        if notes:
            existing_notes = (self._qualification_data.get("notes") or "").strip()
            self._qualification_data["notes"] = self._merge_notes(existing_notes, notes)


        try:
            result = self._sync_lead_init(
                reason="register_qualified_lead",
                require_signal=False,
            )
            logger.info("[CI_] Lead registered: %s", json.dumps(result))
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "register_qualified_lead", result.get("status", "error"))


            if result.get("status") in ("success", "skipped"):
                # Use fully accumulated qualification data for merchant notification.
                customer_name = self._qualification_data.get("customer_name", customer_name)
                service_interest = self._qualification_data.get("service_interest", service_interest)
                visit_date = self._qualification_data.get("visit_date", visit_date)
                party_size = self._qualification_data.get("party_size", party_size)
                notes = self._qualification_data.get("notes", notes)
                # Notify merchant via WhatsApp (behind flag — disabled by default)
                if result.get("status") == "success" and ENABLE_MERCHANT_WA_NOTIFICATION and self._merchant_phone:
                    try:
                        send_lead_notification_to_merchant(
                            merchant_phone=self._merchant_phone,
                            customer_name=customer_name,
                            customer_phone=getattr(self, "_customer_phone", ""),
                            service_interest=service_interest,
                            visit_date=visit_date,
                            party_size=party_size,
                            notes=notes,
                        )
                        logger.info("[CI_LEAD] merchant_notification sent to %s", self._merchant_phone)
                    except Exception as notify_exc:
                        logger.error("[CI_LEAD] merchant_notification failed phone=%s error=%s", self._merchant_phone, notify_exc)
                else:
                    logger.info("[CI_LEAD] merchant_notification skipped (flag=%s phone=%s)", ENABLE_MERCHANT_WA_NOTIFICATION, self._merchant_phone)


                # Advance stage + persist
                self._lead_handed_off = True
                self._qualification_data["lead_score"] = self._calculate_lead_score()
                self._advance_stage(lead_registered=True)
                self._save_state(self.current_session_id)


                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    self.current_session_id,
                    "register_qualified_lead",
                    {
                        "status": "success",
                        "message": (
                            f"Lead registered for {customer_name}. Merchant has been notified."
                            if result.get("status") == "success"
                            else f"Lead already up to date for {customer_name}."
                        ),
                        "user_id": result.get("user_id", ""),
                        "lead_id": result.get("lead_id", ""),
                    },
                )
            else:
                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    self.current_session_id,
                    "register_qualified_lead",
                    {"status": "error", "error": result.get("error", "Unknown error")},
                )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("[CI_] register_qualified_lead failed: %s", e)
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "register_qualified_lead", "error")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id,
                "register_qualified_lead",
                {"status": "error", "error": str(e)},
            )


    async def _upsert_lead_intermediate(self, session_id: str) -> None:
        """Non-blocking: progressively sync lead via register_lead/leads-init only.


        Called after every real customer turn so lead state evolves from cool→warm→hot
        without waiting for the LLM to call register_qualified_lead.
        """
        if not self._merchant_id or not self._customer_phone:
            return


        init_result = self._sync_lead_init(
            reason="turn_progress",
            require_signal=False,
        )
        if init_result.get("status") == "success":
            payload = self._lead_sync_snapshot if isinstance(self._lead_sync_snapshot, dict) else {}
            logger.info(
                "[CI_UPSERT] session=%s score=%s service=%s visit=%s lead_id=%s user_id=%s context_id=%s",
                session_id,
                payload.get("lead_score", self._calculate_lead_score()),
                payload.get("service_interest", "?"),
                payload.get("visit_date", "?"),
                self._lead_id,
                self._lead_user_id,
                payload.get("context_id", ""),
            )
        elif init_result.get("status") == "skipped":
            logger.info("[CI_UPSERT] skipped: session=%s reason=%s", session_id, init_result.get("reason"))
        else:
            logger.warning("[CI_UPSERT] leads/init sync failed (non-blocking): %s", init_result.get("error"))


    async def _handle_fetch_merchant_data(self, tool_args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        merchant_id = tool_args.get("merchant_id", self._merchant_id)
        if not merchant_id:
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id,
                "fetch_merchant_data",
                {"status": "error", "error": "No merchant_id provided"},
            )


        await self._load_merchant_data(merchant_id)


        if not self._merchant_data:
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id,
                "fetch_merchant_data",
                {"status": "error", "error": "Could not load merchant data"},
            )


        # Advance to greet/assist_qualify now that data is loaded
        self._advance_stage(merchant_id_known=True)
        self._advance_stage()  # greet → assist_qualify if data loaded
        self._save_state(self.current_session_id)


        biz = self._merchant_data.get("business_info", {})
        summary = {
            "status": "success",
            "merchant_name": self._merchant_name,
            "category": self._category,
            "address": biz.get("formatted_address", ""),
            "phone": self._merchant_phone,
            "rating": biz.get("rating"),
            "total_reviews": biz.get("total_reviews"),
            "offers_count": len(self._offers),
        }
        return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
            self.current_session_id,
            "fetch_merchant_data",
            summary,
        )


    async def _handle_mcp_tool(self, tool_name: str, tool_args: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            result = await self._vera_mcp_client.call_tool(tool_name, tool_args)
            parsed = self._parse_mcp_result(result)
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, tool_name, "success")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id,
                tool_name,
                parsed if isinstance(parsed, dict) else {"data": parsed},
            )
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.error("[CI_] MCP tool %s failed: %s", tool_name, exc)
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, tool_name, "error")
            return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                self.current_session_id,
                tool_name,
                {"status": "error", "error": str(exc)},
            )


    def _calculate_lead_score(self) -> str:
        """Calculate lead temperature: hot / warm / cool."""
        q = self._qualification_data
        visit = (q.get("visit_date") or "").lower()
        has_party = bool(q.get("party_size"))
        has_service = bool(q.get("service_interest"))
        # exclude internal trackers from qual_count
        qual_count = sum(1 for k, v in q.items() if v and k != "name_asked_count")


        if visit in ("today", "tonight", "tomorrow") or has_party:
            return "hot"
        # warm: any visit intent OR has service interest + name (clear qualified lead)
        if visit or (has_service and qual_count >= 2) or qual_count >= 3:
            return "warm"
        return "cool"


    def _build_lead_summary(self) -> str:
        """Build a concise lead summary for merchant-backend lead insights."""
        qual = self._qualification_data
        interest = (qual.get("service_interest") or "").strip()
        visit_date = (qual.get("visit_date") or "").strip()
        party_size = (qual.get("party_size") or "").strip()
        customer_name = (qual.get("customer_name") or "").strip()
        if not self._is_plausible_customer_name(customer_name):
            customer_name = ""


        if interest:
            summary = f"Customer is interested in {interest}"
        else:
            summary = "Customer reached out with an enquiry"


        details = []
        if visit_date:
            details.append(f"visit {visit_date}")
        if party_size:
            details.append(f"party size {party_size}")
        if customer_name:
            details.append(f"name {customer_name}")


        if details:
            summary = f"{summary}; " + ", ".join(details)
        return summary


    def _build_user_ask(self) -> str:
        """Return the normalized user ask for lead insights."""
        service_interest = (self._qualification_data.get("service_interest") or "").strip()
        if service_interest:
            return service_interest
        service_mode = (self._qualification_data.get("service_mode") or "").strip()
        if service_mode:
            return f"{service_mode} enquiry"
        return "general enquiry"


    def is_followup_eligible(self, bot_response_message=None) -> bool:
        """Check if followup should be scheduled."""
        if self._stage in ("closed", "identify"):
            return False
        if getattr(self, "is_proactive_followup", False):
            return False
        return True


    async def handle_batch_input(self, batch_input: Dict) -> List[Dict]:
        """Override batch handler to route each message through handle_input.


        The Kafka consumer calls handle_batch_input (not handle_input).
        BaseAgent.handle_batch_input bypasses handle_input entirely, skipping
        our mid extraction, prefix stripping, stage management, and MCP loading.
        This override routes each batch message through our handle_input.
        """
        messages = batch_input.get("messages", [])
        shared_metadata = batch_input.get("metadata", {})
        session_id = batch_input.get("session_id", "")
        source_session_id = batch_input.get("source_session_id", "")


        logger.info("[CI_TRACE] handle_batch_input: session=%s messages=%d", session_id, len(messages))


        responses = []
        for msg_data in messages:
            message_text = msg_data.get("message", "")
            msg_metadata = msg_data.get("metadata", {})
            # Merge shared metadata with per-message metadata
            merged_metadata = {**shared_metadata, **msg_metadata}


            agent_input = {
                "type": "agent_input",
                "session_id": session_id,
                "source_session_id": source_session_id,
                "message": message_text,
                "metadata": merged_metadata,
            }
            if isinstance(msg_data.get("image_urls"), list) and msg_data.get("image_urls"):
                agent_input["image_urls"] = msg_data["image_urls"]
            response = await self.handle_input(agent_input)
            responses.append(response)


        return responses


    async def handle_input(self, agent_input: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Handle incoming customer message."""
        session_id = agent_input.get("session_id", "")
        metadata = agent_input.get("metadata", {})
        context_data = metadata.get("context_data") or {}
        message = agent_input.get("message", "")
        logger.info("[CI_DEBUG] session=%s raw_message repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:300]))


        # Strip message-server prefixes ("Merchant: ", "Customer: ", "Template: ...\nMerchant: ")
        # Also handles prod Kafka format: "Merchant ID: <id>\n\nQuery: <user text>"
        raw_message = message
        if message:
            # Prod format: "Merchant ID: 7207965\n\nQuery: Customer: VERA_OFFER_INQUIRY | ..."
            _query_match = re.search(r"(?is)\bquery\s*:\s*(.+)$", message)
            if _query_match:
                message = _query_match.group(1).strip()
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s query_extracted repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
            elif "\nMerchant: " in message:
                message = message.split("\nMerchant: ", 1)[-1]
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s stripped=newline_merchant repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
            elif "\nCustomer: " in message:
                message = message.split("\nCustomer: ", 1)[-1]
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s stripped=newline_customer repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
            elif message.startswith("Merchant: "):
                message = message[len("Merchant: "):]
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s stripped=merchant_prefix repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
            elif message.startswith("Customer: "):
                message = message[len("Customer: "):]
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s stripped=customer_prefix repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
            else:
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s no_strip_match repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
            # Second pass: query extraction may leave "Customer: " or "Merchant: " prefix
            if message.startswith("Customer: "):
                message = message[len("Customer: "):]
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s second_pass stripped=customer repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
            elif message.startswith("Merchant: "):
                message = message[len("Merchant: "):]
                logger.info("[CI_STRIP] session=%s second_pass stripped=merchant repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))


        # ── Parse VERA_OFFER_INQUIRY deep-link prefix ────────────────────────
        # Format: "VERA_OFFER_INQUIRY | MID:<mid> | OID:<oid> | OFFER:<title>"
        # Sent when a consumer taps a vera offer deep-link (wa.me pre-fill).
        # Sets offer context, extracts merchant_id, clears message so LLM introduces
        # the offer proactively. Fully backwards-compatible — only triggers on exact prefix.
        logger.info("[CI_OFFER_PARSE] session=%s after_strip repr=%s", session_id, repr(message[:200]))
        if message and message.startswith("VERA_OFFER_INQUIRY"):
            _parsed_mid = ""
            _parsed_oid = ""
            _parsed_offer_title = ""
            for _part in message.split("|"):
                _part = _part.strip()
                if _part.startswith("MID:"):
                    _parsed_mid = _part[4:].strip()
                elif _part.startswith("OID:"):
                    _parsed_oid = _part[4:].strip()
                elif _part.startswith("OFFER:"):
                    _parsed_offer_title = _part[6:].strip()
            if _parsed_mid:
                context_data["merchant_id"] = _parsed_mid
                agent_input.setdefault("metadata", {}).setdefault("context_data", {})["merchant_id"] = _parsed_mid
            self._offer_inquiry_mode = True
            self._offer_context = {"offer_id": _parsed_oid, "offer_title": _parsed_offer_title}
            # Clear stale response_id thread — VERA_OFFER_INQUIRY is always the first customer
            # message of a new conversation. Stale IDs cause the LLM to continue an old thread
            # (wrong stage/context) instead of starting fresh with the new system prompt.
            try:
                self._unset_response_id(session_id)
                logger.info("[CI_OFFER] cleared previous_response_id for fresh offer inquiry thread")
            except Exception as _e:
                logger.warning("[CI_OFFER] failed to clear previous_response_id: %s", _e)
            # Use "Hi" instead of empty string — empty message triggers Azure OpenAI safety refusal.
            # System prompt's OFFER INQUIRY block handles the opening; this is just a trigger.
            message = "Hi"
            agent_input["message"] = message
            logger.info(
                "[CI_OFFER] offer inquiry: mid=%s oid=%s title=%s",
                _parsed_mid, _parsed_oid, _parsed_offer_title,
            )


        # ── Parse merchant_id from deeplink pre-filled text ──────────────
        # wa.me links encode merchant context in the first message:
        #   Format: "MID:<merchant_id>|<merchant_name>|<customer_message>"
        #   Example: "MID:2532|Pizza 65|Hi I want to know more"
        # Also handle: just a bare merchant_id as first word (e.g., "2532 Hi tell me")
        _deeplink_mid = ""
        _deeplink_name = ""
        if message and not context_data.get("merchant_id"):
            if message.startswith("MID:"):
                parts = message.split("|", 2)
                _deeplink_mid = parts[0][4:].strip()
                # Guard: if no pipe separator, _deeplink_mid may contain extra tokens
                # e.g. "MID: 7207965 OID: abc" → take only the first whitespace-delimited token
                _deeplink_mid = _deeplink_mid.split()[0] if _deeplink_mid else ""
                if len(parts) >= 2:
                    _deeplink_name = parts[1].strip()
                if len(parts) >= 3:
                    message = parts[2].strip()  # Clean customer message
                else:
                    message = ""  # No customer message, just merchant context
                logger.info("[CI_TRACE] deeplink parsed mid=%s name=%s msg=%s", _deeplink_mid, _deeplink_name, message[:60])
            else:
                # Try to find merchant_id ANYWHERE in the message (4-8 digit number)
                # Handles: "2532 Hi tell me", "tell me about 52940", just "2532"
                mid_match = re.search(r'\b(\d{4,8})\b', message)
                if mid_match:
                    _deeplink_mid = mid_match.group(1)
                    # Remove the mid from message so LLM doesn't see it
                    message = message[:mid_match.start()].strip() + " " + message[mid_match.end():].strip()
                    message = message.strip()
                    logger.info("[CI_TRACE] mid extracted=%s from message, cleaned=%s", _deeplink_mid, message[:60])


        if _deeplink_mid:
            context_data["merchant_id"] = _deeplink_mid
            if _deeplink_name:
                context_data["merchant_name"] = _deeplink_name
            agent_input.setdefault("metadata", {}).setdefault("context_data", {})["merchant_id"] = _deeplink_mid


        agent_input["message"] = message  # Update so BaseAgent sees clean message


        logger.info(
            "[CI_TRACE] handle_input START session=%s mid=%s msg=%s source=%s deeplink_mid=%s",
            session_id, context_data.get("merchant_id", "?"), (message or "")[:80],
            metadata.get("source", "?"), _deeplink_mid or "none",
        )


        # Store session context on instance for BaseAgent (must set ALL attributes it expects)
        self.current_session_id = session_id
        self.current_source_session_id = agent_input.get("source_session_id", session_id)
        self.current_metadata = metadata
        self.current_context = context_data
        self.current_intent = metadata.get("subjected_intent", "customer_incoming")
        self.current_chat_history = metadata.get("chat_history", [])
        self.current_message = message
        self.current_received_via_app_chat = metadata.get("received_via_app_chat", False)
        self.current_app_meta_data = metadata.get("app_meta_data", {})
        self._current_response_text = ""
        self._last_communicated_message = ""
        self._sync_messages_sent = []
        self.is_proactive_followup = metadata.get("source") == "proactive_followup"


        # Extract customer phone from metadata (try multiple fields)
        self._customer_phone = (
            metadata.get("phone_number", "")
            or context_data.get("customer_phone", "")
            or metadata.get("phone", "")
            or context_data.get("phone_number", "")
        )
        logger.info("[CI_TRACE] phone=%s proactive=%s", self._customer_phone, self.is_proactive_followup)


        # Cancel pending followups on real customer message
        if not self.is_proactive_followup and session_id:
            try:
                cancel_follow_up(int(session_id))
            except Exception:
                pass  # Non-critical — session_id may not be numeric


        # Load persisted conversation state
        self._load_state(session_id)
        logger.info(
            "[CI_TRACE] state_loaded stage=%s mid=%s merchant=%s qual_count=%d",
            self._stage, self._merchant_id, self._merchant_name,
            sum(1 for v in self._qualification_data.values() if v),
        )


        # ── Extract outbound campaign metadata ────────────────────────────────
        # Outbound flow: merchant sends template message; metadata carries campaign config.
        # These fields are set once and persisted. Values from metadata always win (idempotent).
        #
        # Kafka path stores fields under context_data.whatsapp_metadata (confirmed from logs).
        # HTTP/local path may have them flat at top level or under meta_data.
        # Resolution order: top-level → meta_data nested → whatsapp_metadata nested.
        _wa_meta = context_data.get("whatsapp_metadata") if isinstance(context_data, dict) else None
        _wa_meta = _wa_meta if isinstance(_wa_meta, dict) else {}
        _nested_meta = metadata.get("meta_data") if isinstance(metadata, dict) else None
        _nested_meta = _nested_meta if isinstance(_nested_meta, dict) else {}


        def _resolve(*keys_or_dicts):
            """Return first non-empty string found across dicts in order."""
            for src in keys_or_dicts:
                v = (src or "").strip() if isinstance(src, str) else ""
                if v:
                    return v
            return ""


        # merchant_id may live at top-level in outbound metadata (not inside context_data)
        _meta_merchant_id = str(metadata.get("merchant_id", "")).strip()
        if _meta_merchant_id and not context_data.get("merchant_id"):
            context_data["merchant_id"] = _meta_merchant_id


        # Language — explicit value from metadata takes priority over "mirror customer" default
        _ISO_LANG = {"en": "english", "hi": "hindi", "mr": "marathi", "ta": "tamil", "te": "telugu", "kn": "kannada"}
        _meta_lang = _resolve(
            metadata.get("language"), metadata.get("template_language"),
            _nested_meta.get("language"), _wa_meta.get("language"),
        ).lower()
        _meta_lang = _ISO_LANG.get(_meta_lang, _meta_lang)
        if _meta_lang:
            self._language = _meta_lang


        # Agent tone — PROFESSIONAL / FRIENDLY / CASUAL
        _meta_tone = _resolve(
            metadata.get("agent_tone"), _nested_meta.get("agent_tone"), _wa_meta.get("agent_tone"),
        ).upper()
        if _meta_tone:
            self._agent_tone = _meta_tone


        # Free-form context the merchant provided for this campaign
        _meta_context_dump = _resolve(
            metadata.get("context_dump"), _nested_meta.get("context_dump"), _wa_meta.get("context_dump"),
        )
        if _meta_context_dump:
            self._context_dump = _meta_context_dump


        # Social / listing links — used to call vera_get_merchant_by_links for rich JD/Google data
        _meta_jd = _resolve(metadata.get("justdial_link"), _nested_meta.get("justdial_link"), _wa_meta.get("justdial_link"))
        _meta_ig = _resolve(metadata.get("instagram_link"), _nested_meta.get("instagram_link"), _wa_meta.get("instagram_link"))
        _meta_gg = _resolve(metadata.get("google_link"), _nested_meta.get("google_link"), _wa_meta.get("google_link"))
        if _meta_jd or _meta_ig or _meta_gg:
            self._social_links = {k: v for k, v in [("justdial", _meta_jd), ("instagram", _meta_ig), ("google", _meta_gg)] if v}


        # Campaign / template name — presence of either flags outbound mode
        _meta_campaign = _resolve(
            metadata.get("campaign"), _nested_meta.get("campaign"), _wa_meta.get("campaign"),
        )
        if _meta_campaign:
            self._campaign = _meta_campaign
            self._outbound_mode = True
        _meta_template = _resolve(
            metadata.get("template_name"), _nested_meta.get("template_name"), _wa_meta.get("template_name"),
        )
        if _meta_template:
            self._template_name = _meta_template
            self._outbound_mode = True


        if self._outbound_mode:
            logger.info(
                "[CI_TRACE] outbound_mode=True campaign=%s template=%s lang=%s tone=%s",
                self._campaign, self._template_name, self._language, self._agent_tone,
            )


        # Extract merchant_id from context (set by message-server routing)
        merchant_id = str(context_data.get("merchant_id", ""))
        if merchant_id and not self._merchant_id:
            self._merchant_id = merchant_id


        # Language: LLM mirrors customer's language automatically via prompt instruction
        # No detection needed — prompt says "Mirror the customer's language exactly"


        # Fetch merchant context from JD/Google links early (before stage logic)
        # so JD data counts as merchant-known even when merchant_id is absent
        if self._outbound_mode and self._social_links:
            await self._load_merchant_by_links()
            if not self._merchant_name and self._links_merchant_data:
                _jd_entry = self._links_merchant_data.get("justdial") or {}
                self._merchant_name = _jd_entry.get("jdJSON", {}).get("name", "")


        # Stage advancement: if we have merchant_id but haven't loaded data yet
        has_msg = bool(message and not self.is_proactive_followup)
        _merchant_known = bool(self._merchant_id or self._links_merchant_data)
        if self._merchant_id:
            self._advance_stage(merchant_id_known=True, has_customer_message=has_msg)


            # Auto-load merchant data if not yet loaded (or re-fetch if only summary cached)
            if not self._merchant_data or "business_info" not in (self._merchant_data or {}):
                logger.info("[CI_TRACE] loading merchant data mid=%s", self._merchant_id)
                await self._load_merchant_data(self._merchant_id)
                logger.info("[CI_TRACE] merchant_data loaded=%s name=%s", bool(self._merchant_data), self._merchant_name)
            if self._merchant_data:
                self._advance_stage(has_customer_message=has_msg)  # greet → assist_qualify
        elif _merchant_known:
            # No merchant_id but have JD/Google listing data — treat as merchant known
            self._advance_stage(merchant_id_known=True, has_customer_message=has_msg)
            self._advance_stage(has_customer_message=has_msg)  # greet → assist_qualify (links data = merchant data)
