        # Load customer CRM profile for personalisation (non-blocking, cached per session)
        if self._merchant_id and self._customer_phone:
            await self._load_customer_profile(self._merchant_id, self._customer_phone)


        # Ensure allowlisted MCP tool schemas are ready before get_tools() is called.
        await self._prefetch_mcp_tools()


        # Bootstrap identity from noOtp once per chat so name/user token are available early.
        if self._customer_phone and not self.is_proactive_followup:
            self._bootstrap_customer_identity()


        # Fetch rich offer details if in offer inquiry mode and OID is real
        logger.info("[CI_OFFER_MODE] session=%s offer_inquiry_mode=%s offer_context=%s",
                    session_id, self._offer_inquiry_mode, self._offer_context)
        if self._offer_inquiry_mode:
            _oid = self._offer_context.get("offer_id", "")
            logger.info("[CI_OFFER_MODE] session=%s loading offer details oid=%s", session_id, _oid)
            if _oid and _oid.lower() != "tempid":
                await self._load_offer_details(_oid)
                logger.info("[CI_OFFER_MODE] session=%s offer_details_loaded=%s",
                            session_id, bool(self._offer_context.get("offer_details")))


        # Save state before processing (captures stage + merchant data)
        self._save_state(session_id)


        # Increment turn count for anti-repetition tracking
        if message and not self.is_proactive_followup:
            self._turn_count += 1


        # Infer qualification data from the message
        self._infer_qualification_from_message(message)


        qual_count = sum(1 for v in self._qualification_data.values() if v)
        logger.info(
            "[CI_TRACE] processing session=%s stage=%s mid=%s merchant=%s lang=%s "
            "qual_count=%d lead_score=%s phone=%s history_len=%d",
            session_id, self._stage, self._merchant_id, self._merchant_name,
            self._language, qual_count, self._calculate_lead_score(),
            self._customer_phone, len(self.current_chat_history),
        )


        # Add multimodal image context for LLM turn (if present in metadata).
        augmented_message, context_image_urls = self._prepare_multimodal_context(
            agent_input.get("message", ""),
            context_data,
        )
        incoming_image_urls = agent_input.get("image_urls", [])
        merged_image_urls: List[str] = []
        seen_urls = set()
        for url in [*(incoming_image_urls if isinstance(incoming_image_urls, list) else []), *context_image_urls]:
            normalized = str(url or "").strip()
            if normalized and normalized not in seen_urls:
                seen_urls.add(normalized)
                merged_image_urls.append(normalized)


        agent_input["message"] = augmented_message
        self.current_message = augmented_message
        has_media_turn = bool(merged_image_urls) or bool(
            isinstance(context_data.get("direct_media"), dict) and context_data.get("direct_media", {}).get("url")
        )
        if merged_image_urls:
            agent_input["image_urls"] = merged_image_urls
            logger.info("[CI_MEDIA] multimodal attached=%d", len(merged_image_urls))
        else:
            agent_input.pop("image_urls", None)


        # Delegate to BaseAgent's LLM processing
        try:
            last_response_id = self._get_response_id(session_id)
            response = await self._process_agent_input(
                agent_input, self.current_chat_history, last_response_id
            )
            await self._pull_qualification_state_from_mcp(session_id)
            # Track how many times agent has asked for customer name
            if not self._qualification_data.get("customer_name"):
                last_msg = (self._last_communicated_message or "").lower()
                _name_ask_phrases = ("your name", "may i know", "aapka naam", "naam bata", "naam kya",
                                     "what should i call", "kya naam", "name please", "your good name",
                                     "can i get your name", "who am i speaking", "what's your name",
                                     "whats your name", "tell me your name")
                if any(p in last_msg for p in _name_ask_phrases):
                    count = int(self._qualification_data.get("name_asked_count", 0))
                    self._qualification_data["name_asked_count"] = count + 1
            # Save state after processing (captures any stage changes from tool calls)
            self._save_state(session_id)


            # Progressive lead sync should run only on real inbound customer turns.
            if (message or has_media_turn) and not self.is_proactive_followup:
                await self._upsert_lead_intermediate(session_id)


            # Schedule followup if eligible
            if self.is_followup_eligible():
                try:
                    fu_config = get_agent_followup_config(self.agent_type)
                    fu_interval = fu_config.get("intervals", {}).get(1, fu_config.get("interval_hours", 4.0))
                    fu_max = fu_config.get("max_attempts", 3)
                    schedule_follow_up(
                        ticket_id=int(session_id),
                        agent_type=self.agent_type,
                        interval_hours=fu_interval,
                        max_attempts=fu_max,
                    )
                except Exception as exc:
                    logger.warning("[CI_] Followup scheduling failed: %s", exc)


            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "message_processed", "success")
            return response
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("[CI_] Error: %s", e, exc_info=True)
            increment_tool_call(self.agent_type, "message_processing", "error")
            return MessageProtocol.create_agent_response(
                session_id,
                "Sorry, something went wrong. Please try again.",
                {"error": str(e)},
            )
        finally:
            # Always save state — even on error, preserve qual data + stage for next turn
            try:
                self._save_state(session_id)
            except Exception:
                pass


    def _infer_qualification_from_message(self, message: str) -> None:
        """Extract qualification data from customer message using simple patterns."""
        if not message:
            return
        lowered = message.lower()


        # Name detection — skip if already collected
        if not self._qualification_data.get("customer_name"):
            name_triggers = ["my name is ", "i'm ", "i am ", "mera naam ", "naam "]
            _name_captured = False
            for trigger in name_triggers:
                if trigger in lowered:
                    after = message[lowered.index(trigger) + len(trigger):]
                    name = after.split(",")[0].split(".")[0].split("\n")[0].strip()
                    if self._is_plausible_customer_name(name):
                        self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = name
                        self._qualification_data.pop("name_asked_count", None)  # Clean up tracker
                        _name_captured = True
                        break


            # Heuristic: if agent already asked for name and customer replies with a short
            # word-only message (no digits), treat it as a standalone name response
            if not _name_captured and int(self._qualification_data.get("name_asked_count", 0)) >= 1:
                _words = message.strip().split()
                _NON_NAME = {"yes", "no", "ok", "okay", "sure", "hi", "hello", "haan", "nahi",
                             "han", "nah", "thanks", "thank", "great", "good", "nice", "hmm"}
                if (
                    1 <= len(_words) <= 3
                    and not re.search(r"\d", message)
                    and all(re.match(r"^[a-zA-Z\u0900-\u097F]+$", w) for w in _words)
                    and _words[0].lower() not in _NON_NAME
                    and self._is_plausible_customer_name(message.strip())
                ):
                    self._qualification_data["customer_name"] = message.strip().title()
                    self._qualification_data.pop("name_asked_count", None)


        # Visit date inference
        if not self._qualification_data.get("visit_date"):
            visit = self._infer_visit_date(lowered)
            if visit:
                self._qualification_data["visit_date"] = visit


        # Preferred time inference — safety net (LLM also saves via update_qualification_data)
        if not self._qualification_data.get("preferred_time"):
            preferred_time = self._infer_preferred_time(lowered)
            if preferred_time:
                self._qualification_data["preferred_time"] = preferred_time


        # Service interest is now identified by the LLM via update_qualification_data tool — not inferred here


        # Party size
        if not self._qualification_data.get("party_size"):
            party_patterns = [
                r"(\d+)\s*(?:people|persons|logo|log|jan|jne)",
                r"(?:party of|group of|table for|for)\s*(\d+)",
                r"(?:hum|ham)\s*(\d+)\s*(?:log|jan|hain)",
            ]
            for pat in party_patterns:
                m = re.search(pat, lowered)
                if m:
                    self._qualification_data["party_size"] = m.group(1)
                    break


        # Dietary preference inference
        if not self._qualification_data.get("dietary_preference"):
            if any(w in lowered for w in ("non-veg", "non veg", "nonveg", "chicken", "mutton", "fish")):
                self._qualification_data["dietary_preference"] = "non-veg"
            elif any(w in lowered for w in ("veg", "vegetarian", "pure veg", "vegan")):
                self._qualification_data["dietary_preference"] = "veg"


        # Service mode inference
        if not self._qualification_data.get("service_mode"):
            if any(w in lowered for w in ("delivery", "deliver", "home delivery")):
                self._qualification_data["service_mode"] = "delivery"
            elif any(w in lowered for w in ("dine in", "dine-in", "table", "reservation", "book")):
                self._qualification_data["service_mode"] = "dine-in"
            elif any(w in lowered for w in ("takeout", "takeaway", "take away", "parcel")):
                self._qualification_data["service_mode"] = "takeout"


    @staticmethod
    def _infer_visit_date(lowered: str) -> str:
        """Extract visit date/timing from customer message including Hinglish patterns."""
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("today", "tonight", "aaj", "abhi", "right now")):
            return "today"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("tomorrow", "kal", "kal tak")):
            return "tomorrow"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("this weekend", "is weekend", "weekend pe", "weekend mein")):
            return "this weekend"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("next week", "agle hafte", "agle week")):
            return "next week"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("this week", "is hafte", "is week")):
            return "this week"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("next month", "agle mahine")):
            return "next month"
        # "coming soon / will visit" intent — Hinglish
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("aa jata", "aa jaaunga", "aaunga", "aane wala", "aajata",
                                       "aa raha", "aa rahi", "aata hoon", "aati hoon",
                                       "will come", "will visit", "planning to visit", "plan to come")):
            return "soon"
        for day in ("monday", "tuesday", "wednesday", "thursday", "friday", "saturday", "sunday"):
            if f"this {day}" in lowered or f"is {day}" in lowered or day in lowered:
                return f"this {day}"
        # Date patterns: "5th april", "april 5", "5 april", "5/4", "may mein"
        m = re.search(r"(\d{1,2})(?:st|nd|rd|th)?\s+(jan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|oct|nov|dec)\w*", lowered)
        if m:
            return f"{m.group(1)} {m.group(2)}"
        m = re.search(r"(jan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|oct|nov|dec)\w*\s+(\d{1,2})", lowered)
        if m:
            return f"{m.group(2)} {m.group(1)}"
        m = re.search(r"(jan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|oct|nov|dec)\w*\s+mein", lowered)
        if m:
            return m.group(1)
        return ""


    @staticmethod
    def _prepare_multimodal_context(message: str, context_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> tuple[str, List[str]]:
        """Convert direct/history media metadata into message hints + image_urls."""
        if not isinstance(message, str):
            message = str(message or "")
        if not isinstance(context_data, dict):
            return message, []


        augmented_message = message
        image_urls: List[str] = []


        direct_media = context_data.get("direct_media")
        if isinstance(direct_media, dict) and direct_media.get("url"):
            dm_type = str(direct_media.get("type", "image") or "image")
            dm_url = str(direct_media.get("url") or "").strip()
            dm_mime = str(direct_media.get("mime_type", "") or "").strip()
            if dm_url:
                if dm_type == "image":
                    image_urls.append(dm_url)
                else:
                    lines = [
                        f"\n\n[DIRECT_{dm_type.upper()}_FROM_CUSTOMER]",
                        f"URL: {dm_url}",
                    ]
                    if dm_mime:
                        lines.append(f"MIME: {dm_mime}")
                    augmented_message += "\n".join(lines)


        pending_media_list = context_data.get("pending_media_from_history")
        if isinstance(pending_media_list, list):
            uploadable = [
                item for item in pending_media_list
                if isinstance(item, dict) and item.get("url") and item.get("type") in ("image", "video")
            ]
            if uploadable:
                item = uploadable[0]
                lines = [
                    f"\n\n[LAST_{item.get('type', 'image').upper()}_FROM_CUSTOMER — found in conversation history]",
                ]
                if item.get("caption"):
                    lines.append(f"Caption when sent: \"{item['caption']}\"")
                lines.append(f"URL: {item['url']}  Type: {item['type']}")
                if item.get("type") == "image" and not (
                    isinstance(direct_media, dict)
                    and direct_media.get("url")
                    and str(direct_media.get("type", "image") or "image") == "image"
                ):
                    image_urls.append(str(item["url"]))
                    lines.append("The customer may be referring to this previously shared image in the current message.")
                else:
                    lines.append("The customer may be referring to this previously shared media in the current message.")
                augmented_message += "\n".join(lines)


        return augmented_message, image_urls


    @staticmethod
    def _infer_preferred_time(lowered: str) -> str:
        """Extract preferred time slot from customer message."""
        # Specific clock time: "10am", "10:30am", "around 10", "at 10"
        m = re.search(r"(?:around|at|by)?\s*(\d{1,2})(?::(\d{2}))?\s*(am|pm)", lowered)
        if m:
            hour, minute, period = m.group(1), m.group(2) or "00", m.group(3)
            return f"{hour}:{minute} {period}"
        m = re.search(r"(?:around|at|by)\s+(\d{1,2})(?::(\d{2}))?(?!\s*(?:jan|feb|mar|apr|may|jun|jul|aug|sep|oct|nov|dec|\d))", lowered)
        if m:
            return f"{m.group(1)}:00"
        # Named slots — specific before generic
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("late evening", "late night")):
            return "late evening"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("early morning", "subah subah")):
            return "early morning"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("morning", "subah", "suba")):
            return "morning"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("noon", "dopahar", "dopehar", "lunch time")):
            return "noon"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("afternoon", "dopahar baad")):
            return "afternoon"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("evening", "shaam", "after 6", "after 7", "after 5")):
            return "evening"
        if any(w in lowered for w in ("night", "raat")):
            return "night"
        return ""


- [agents/vera/customer_incoming_prompts.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/agents/vera/customer_incoming_prompts.py)


"""
Customer Incoming Agent — Prompt Templates


Stage-specific prompts for the customer-facing concierge agent.
Answers customer questions about a merchant and qualifies leads.


Qualification questions are dynamically generated from the merchant's actual data,
not generic category templates.
"""


import json
from urllib.parse import quote_plus
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional




def _render_json(data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]], max_len: int = 4000) -> str:
    """Safely render JSON for embedding in prompts."""
    if not data:
        return "{}"
    try:
        s = json.dumps(data, indent=2, default=str)
        return s[:max_len] if len(s) > max_len else s
    except Exception:
        return str(data)[:max_len]




def _extract_merchant_highlights(merchant_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """Extract key highlights from merchant data for the greeting."""
    highlights = []
    biz = merchant_data.get("business_info", {})


    if biz.get("editorial_summary"):
        highlights.append(biz["editorial_summary"])
    if biz.get("rating") and biz.get("total_reviews"):
        highlights.append(f"Rated {biz['rating']}/5 ({biz['total_reviews']} reviews)")
    if biz.get("price_level"):
        levels = {1: "Budget-friendly", 2: "Moderate", 3: "Upscale", 4: "Premium"}
        highlights.append(levels.get(biz["price_level"], ""))


    return " | ".join(h for h in highlights if h)




def _build_service_capabilities(merchant_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """Build a list of what the merchant offers from actual data."""
    biz = merchant_data.get("business_info", {})
    caps = []


    if biz.get("dine_in"):
        caps.append("Dine-in")
    if biz.get("delivery"):
        caps.append("Delivery")
    if biz.get("takeout"):
        caps.append("Takeout")
    if biz.get("reservable"):
        caps.append("Reservations")
    if biz.get("serves_vegetarian_food"):
        caps.append("Vegetarian options")
    if biz.get("serves_beer") or biz.get("serves_wine"):
        caps.append("Alcohol served")


    # Meal services
    meals = []
    for meal in ["breakfast", "brunch", "lunch", "dinner"]:
        if biz.get(f"serves_{meal}"):
            meals.append(meal.capitalize())
    if meals:
        caps.append(f"Serves: {', '.join(meals)}")


    return ", ".join(caps) if caps else "Services information not available"




def _classify_category_bucket(category: str) -> str:
    """Map any category string to an intent bucket for qualification logic."""
    cat = (category or "").lower()


    _FOOD = {
        "restaurant", "cafe", "bakery", "bar", "food", "coffee shop", "sweet shop",
        "icecream shop", "ice cream", "tiffin service", "food delivery", "buffet",
        "lounge", "pub", "night club", "dairy products",
    }
    _BEAUTY = {
        "salon", "spa", "beauty parlour", "parlour", "nail studio", "tattoo studio",
        "makeup artist", "mehendi artist",
    }
    _HEALTH = {
        "doctor", "clinic", "hospital", "dental", "dentist", "dermatologist",
        "gynaecologist", "physician", "paediatrician", "ortho doctor", "ent doctor",
        "ophthalmologist", "homeopathy doc", "ayurved doc", "health clinic",
        "eye hospital", "skin clinic", "physiotherapist", "pathology", "pharmacy",
        "patient care", "home nursing", "veterinary doc",
    }
    _FITNESS = {
        "gym", "fitness", "yoga", "dance class", "drawing class", "coaching centre",
        "computer training", "driving school", "home tutor",
    }
    _ACCOMMODATION = {
        "hotel", "lodge", "inn", "resort", "homestay", "oyo", "lodging",
        "hostel", "dormitory", "paying guest", "bungalow rental", "farmhouse rental",
        "co-working", "laptop rental",
    }
    _EVENT = {
        "event organiser", "caterer", "wedding planner", "photographer",
        "banquet hall", "tent house", "mandap decor", "balloon decor",
        "flower decor", "party decor", "disc jockey", "bands",
        "sound system rental", "projector rental", "pandit",
    }
    _HOME_SERVICE = {
        "ac repair", "appliance repair", "bike repair", "car repair",
        "cleaning service", "electrician", "electronics repair", "fridge repair",
        "mobile repair", "pest control", "plumber", "sofa repair",
        "washing machine repair", "water purifier repair", "carpenter",
        "painter", "waterproofing", "false ceiling", "pop contractor",
        "civil contractor", "borewell contractor", "fabricator", "gardener",
        "housekeeping", "laundry", "dry cleaner",
    }
    _RENTAL = {
        "car rental", "bike rental", "ac on rent", "tempo rentals",
        "bus service", "taxi service",
    }
    _PROFESSIONAL = {
        "ca", "lawyer", "insurance agent", "finance consult", "loan service",
        "property consult", "real estate agent", "architect", "interior designer",
        "website developer", "ad agency", "astrologer", "aadhar agent",
        "marriage certification", "rent agreements", "travel agent",
    }
    _SHOPPING = {
        "clothing shop", "electronics shop", "furniture shop", "gift shop",
        "jeweller", "mobile phones", "footwear", "garment shop", "book shop",
        "stationery shop", "home decor", "supermarket", "pet supplies",
        "plant nursery", "opticians", "spare parts", "textile shop",
        "wallpaper dealer", "water purifier dealer", "wedding card dealer",
        "flex printing", "printing service",
    }


    for bucket, keywords in [
        ("food", _FOOD),
        ("beauty", _BEAUTY),
        ("health", _HEALTH),
        ("fitness", _FITNESS),
        ("accommodation", _ACCOMMODATION),
        ("event", _EVENT),
        ("home_service", _HOME_SERVICE),
        ("rental", _RENTAL),
        ("professional", _PROFESSIONAL),
        ("shopping", _SHOPPING),
    ]:
        if cat in keywords or any(k in cat for k in keywords):
            return bucket


    return "generic"




def _build_qualification_questions(
    merchant_data: Dict[str, Any],
    category: str,
    qualification_data: Dict[str, Any],
    max_questions: int = 3,
) -> str:
    """Generate qualification questions annotated as bundleable groups vs standalone.


    Bundleable = logically related, natural to ask in one sentence (e.g. when + how many).
    Standalone = different dimensions; asking together feels like an interrogation (e.g. name, dietary pref).


    Returns a prompt block the LLM uses to decide pacing.
    """
    biz = merchant_data.get("business_info", {})
    already_collected = set(k for k, v in qualification_data.items() if v)
    bucket = _classify_category_bucket(category)


    # Each entry: (field_key, question_text, group_id)
    # Questions sharing the same group_id can be asked together.
    # group_id=None means standalone — ask alone.
    candidates: list[tuple[str, str, object]] = []


    # Name is always standalone and highest priority
    if "customer_name" not in already_collected:
        candidates.append(("customer_name", "May I know your name?", None))


    if bucket == "food":
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When are you planning to order/visit?", "timing"))
        if "party_size" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("party_size", "How many people is this for?", "timing"))
        if biz.get("dine_in") and biz.get("delivery") and "service_mode" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_mode", "Would you prefer dine-in or delivery?", None))
        if biz.get("serves_vegetarian_food") and "dietary_preference" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("dietary_preference", "Any dietary preferences? (veg/non-veg)", None))


    elif bucket == "beauty":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What service are you looking for?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When would you like to come in?", "timing"))
        if "preferred_time" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("preferred_time", "Any preferred time slot?", "timing"))


    elif bucket == "health":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What type of consultation are you looking for?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When would you like to schedule?", "timing"))
        if "urgency" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("urgency", "Is this urgent or a routine appointment?", "timing"))


    elif bucket == "fitness":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What are you looking for — trial, membership, or specific classes?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When are you thinking of starting?", "timing"))
        if "preferred_time" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("preferred_time", "Do you prefer morning or evening sessions?", "timing"))


    elif bucket == "accommodation":
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When are you checking in?", "timing"))
        if "party_size" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("party_size", "How many guests?", "timing"))
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "How many nights are you thinking?", None))


    elif bucket == "event":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What kind of event are you planning?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When is the event?", "timing"))
        if "party_size" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("party_size", "Roughly how many people?", "timing"))


    elif bucket == "home_service":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What exactly needs to be fixed/done?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When do you need this done?", "timing"))
        if "urgency" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("urgency", "Is it urgent, or flexible on timing?", "timing"))


    elif bucket == "rental":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What do you need and for how long?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When do you need it from?", "timing"))
        if "party_size" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("party_size", "How many people will be using it?", None))


    elif bucket == "professional":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What specifically do you need help with?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When would you like to connect?", "timing"))
        if "urgency" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("urgency", "Is this time-sensitive?", "timing"))


    elif bucket == "shopping":
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What exactly are you looking for?", None))
        if "urgency" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("urgency", "Is this for immediate need or you're exploring?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When are you planning to visit?", None))


    else:
        if "service_interest" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("service_interest", "What specifically are you looking for?", None))
        if "visit_date" not in already_collected:
            candidates.append(("visit_date", "When are you planning to visit?", None))


    candidates = candidates[:max_questions]
    if not candidates:
        return "(all key details collected)"


    # Group into bundleable clusters and standalone entries for the prompt
    seen_groups: set = set()
    bundleable_lines: list[str] = []
    standalone_lines: list[str] = []


    for _field, question, group_id in candidates:
        if group_id is not None:
            if group_id not in seen_groups:
                seen_groups.add(group_id)
                grouped = [q for _, q, g in candidates if g == group_id]
                if len(grouped) > 1:
                    bundleable_lines.append(" + ".join(f'"{q}"' for q in grouped))
                else:
                    standalone_lines.append(question)
        else:
            standalone_lines.append(question)


    out = []
    if bundleable_lines:
        out.append("CAN ASK TOGETHER (same topic — natural in one sentence):")
        out.extend(f"  • {b}" for b in bundleable_lines)
    if standalone_lines:
        out.append("ASK ALONE (different topics — one per message):")
        out.extend(f"  • {s}" for s in standalone_lines)
    return "\n".join(out)




def _build_hours_text(merchant_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """Format opening hours from merchant data."""
    biz = merchant_data.get("business_info", {})
    hours = biz.get("opening_hours") or {}
    if not hours:
        return "Hours not available"
    # Places API returns opening_hours as a dict with weekday_text, or as a list of periods
    if isinstance(hours, list):
        # It's a list of period strings like ["Monday: 9:00 AM – 10:00 PM", ...]
        return "\n".join(str(h) for h in hours) if hours else "Hours not available"
    if isinstance(hours, dict):
        periods = hours.get("weekday_text", [])
        if periods:
            return "\n".join(str(p) for p in periods)
        # Try periods format
        raw_periods = hours.get("periods", [])
        if raw_periods:
            lines = []
            for p in raw_periods:
                if isinstance(p, dict):
                    day = p.get("open", {}).get("day", "")
                    open_t = p.get("open", {}).get("time", "")
                    close_t = p.get("close", {}).get("time", "")
                    if day:
                        lines.append(f"{day}: {open_t} - {close_t}")
            return "\n".join(lines) if lines else "Hours not available"
    return "Hours not available"




def _build_reviews_summary(merchant_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """Build a short summary of recent reviews."""
    reviews = merchant_data.get("reviews", [])
    if not reviews:
        return "No recent reviews available"


    _star_map = {"ONE": 1, "TWO": 2, "THREE": 3, "FOUR": 4, "FIVE": 5}
    lines = []
    for r in reviews[:3]:
        raw_rating = r.get("rating", 0)
        if isinstance(raw_rating, str):
            raw_rating = _star_map.get(raw_rating.upper(), 0)
        try:
            stars = "★" * int(raw_rating)
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            stars = ""
        author = r.get("author_name") or r.get("author", "Customer")
        text = (r.get("text") or r.get("comment") or "")[:120]
        if text:
            lines.append(f'{stars} {author}: "{text}"')
    return "\n".join(lines) if lines else "No recent reviews available"




def _build_offers_text(offers: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Format active offers for the prompt."""
    if not offers:
        return "No active offers currently"
    lines = []
    for o in offers[:5]:
        title = o.get("title", "Special Offer")
        desc = o.get("description", "")
        value = o.get("value", "")
        lines.append(f"- {title}" + (f": {desc}" if desc else "") + (f" ({value})" if value else ""))
    return "\n".join(lines)




def _classify_category(cat: str) -> str:
    """Map a category string to a broad group for hint selection."""
    c = cat.lower()
    if any(k in c for k in ("hotel", "lodge", "inn", "resort", "homestay", "oyo", "lodging", "hostel", "dormitory", "paying guest", "pg", "bungalow rental", "farmhouse")):
        return "accommodation"
    if any(k in c for k in ("restaurant", "cafe", "bakery", "dhaba", "food", "eatery", "coffee shop", "icecream", "sweet shop", "tiffin", "dairy", "buffet")):
        return "food"
    if any(k in c for k in ("bar", "lounge", "night club", "pub")):
        return "nightlife"
    if any(k in c for k in ("salon", "spa", "beauty parlour", "beauty", "parlour", "nail studio", "tattoo")):
        return "beauty"
    if any(k in c for k in ("gym", "fitness", "yoga", "crossfit", "dance class", "drawing class")):
        return "fitness"
    if any(k in c for k in ("doctor", "dentist", "dermatologist", "gynaecologist", "ent doctor", "ophthalmologist", "optician", "ortho", "paediatrician", "physiotherapist", "physician", "ayurved", "homeopathy", "clinic", "hospital", "pathology", "eye hospital", "skin clinic", "home nursing", "patient care", "veterinary")):
        return "medical"
    if any(k in c for k in ("ac repair", "appliance repair", "carpenter", "cleaning service", "electrician", "electronics repair", "fridge repair", "gardener", "housekeeping", "painter", "pest control", "plumber", "sofa repair", "washing machine repair", "waterproofing", "false ceiling", "pop contractor", "borewell", "water purifier")):
        return "home_service"
    if any(k in c for k in ("event", "caterer", "decor", "balloon", "bands", "banquet", "disc jockey", "dj", "flower decor", "makeup artist", "mandap", "mehendi", "pandit", "party decor", "tent house", "wedding", "photographer")):
        return "events_wedding"
    if any(k in c for k in ("bike dealer", "bike rental", "bike repair", "car dealer", "car rental", "car repair", "spare parts", "driving school", "taxi", "tempo", "bus service", "transporter")):
        return "automotive_transport"
    if any(k in c for k in ("school", "college", "coaching", "home tutor", "computer training")):
        return "education"
    if any(k in c for k in ("ca", "chartered", "finance consult", "insurance agent", "lawyer", "property consult", "real estate", "architect", "interior designer", "website developer", "ad agency", "rent agreement", "astrologer", "marriage certif")):
        return "professional"
    if any(k in c for k in ("shop", "store", "jeweller", "mobile phone", "pharmacy", "supermarket", "footwear", "furniture", "clothing", "garment", "textile", "book shop", "gift shop", "stationery", "home decor", "wallpaper", "pet supplies", "electronics shop")):
        return "retail"
    if any(k in c for k in ("packers", "courier", "laundry", "dry cleaner", "security service", "printing service", "flex printing", "sound system", "projector rental", "laptop rental", "ac on rent", "travel agent", "water supplier")):
        return "services"
    if any(k in c for k in ("co-working", "coworking")):
        return "coworking"
    return "generic"

        "reservation availability, wait times, special combos or deals",
    ],

        "entry policies, cover charges, or reservation perks",
    ],
    "beauty": [

        "proximity and convenience of location",
        "packages or combo deals relevant to their interest",

    "fitness": [

        "batch timings that suit mornings or evenings",

        "trainer qualifications and certifications",
        "crowd density at their preferred slot — spacious vs packed",
    ],
    "medical": [

        "multi-specialty under one roof, lab/pharmacy on premises",
    ],
    "home_service": [

        "same-day or emergency service availability",
    ],
    "events_wedding": [

        "customisation — how flexible to their vision and theme",
        "pricing transparency — packages vs à la carte",

    "automotive_transport": [

        "custom orders, bulk pricing, or delivery service",
    ],
    "services": [
        "service area coverage and response time",

    "generic": [

}




def _build_category_location_angles(category: str, address: str, jd_info: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Generate category + location aware selling angle hints for the LLM."""
    lines = []


    # Extract locality from address
    if address and address != "Not available":
        parts = [p.strip() for p in address.split(",")]
        locality = ", ".join(parts[-2:]) if len(parts) >= 2 else address
        lines.append(f"Location: {locality}")


    group = _classify_category(category)
    hints = _CATEGORY_HINTS.get(group, _CATEGORY_HINTS["generic"])


    # Add JD specialisations if available
    if jd_info:
        sub = jd_info.get("subcategory", [])
        if sub:
            lines.append(f"Specialisations: {', '.join(sub[:4])}")
        services = jd_info.get("services_offered", [])
        if services:
            lines.append(f"Key services: {', '.join(services[:5])}")


    # Add locality-specific advantages from address keywords (universal across categories)
    if address and address != "Not available":
        addr_lower = address.lower()
        _locality_advantages = []
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("airport", "igi", "terminal", "aerocity")):
            _locality_advantages.append("Near airport — great for travellers, transit stays, early flights, late arrivals")
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("station", "railway", "junction")):
            _locality_advantages.append("Near railway station — easy access for train travellers")
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("metro",)):
            _locality_advantages.append("Near metro — well connected by public transport")
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("mall", "market", "bazaar")):
            _locality_advantages.append("In a commercial area — shopping, dining, and services nearby")
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("highway", "nh-", "nh ", "national highway")):
            _locality_advantages.append("On highway — easy to reach by road, convenient for road trips")
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("temple", "mandir", "gurudwara", "church", "mosque", "dargah")):
            _locality_advantages.append("Near place of worship — convenient for pilgrimage visits")
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("hospital", "aiims", "medical college")):
            _locality_advantages.append("Near hospital — convenient for patient attendants and medical visits")
        if any(k in addr_lower for k in ("university", "college", "campus", "iit", "iim")):
            _locality_advantages.append("Near educational institution — good for students and visitors")
        if _locality_advantages:
            lines.append("Locality advantages to weave in naturally:")
            for adv in _locality_advantages:
                lines.append(f"  -> {adv}")


    lines.append("Selling angles to vary across messages (pick a DIFFERENT one each time — never reuse):")
    for h in hints:
        lines.append(f"  • {h}")


    return "\n".join(lines)




def _build_jd_info_section(jd_info: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Format JD crawled data into a compact prompt section."""
    if not jd_info:
        return ""
    lines = []
    if jd_info.get("about"):
        lines.append(f"About: {jd_info['about']}")
    if jd_info.get("services_offered"):
        lines.append(f"Services: {', '.join(jd_info['services_offered'])}")
    if jd_info.get("subcategory"):
        lines.append(f"Specialisations: {', '.join(jd_info['subcategory'])}")
    if jd_info.get("timings"):
        t = jd_info["timings"]
        sample = next(iter(t.values()), None)
        if sample:
            lines.append(f"Timings (sample): {sample[0] if isinstance(sample, list) else sample}")
    if jd_info.get("rating") and jd_info.get("total_reviews"):
        lines.append(f"JD Rating: {jd_info['rating']}/5 ({jd_info['total_reviews']} reviews)")
    return "\n".join(lines) if lines else ""




def _build_language_instruction(language: str, outbound_mode: bool) -> str:
    """Build language instruction — explicit in outbound, mirror-based in inbound."""
    _LANG_DISPLAY = {
        "english": "English",
        "hindi": "Hindi (Devanagari script)",
        "hinglish": "Hinglish",
        "marathi": "Marathi",
        "tamil": "Tamil",
        "telugu": "Telugu",
        "kannada": "Kannada",
    }
    _LANG_SCRIPT_NOTE = {
        "hinglish": (
            "Hinglish = Hindi words written in ROMAN (Latin) script mixed with English. "
            "Example: 'Koi baat nahi, booking confirm ho gayi!' "
            "NEVER use Devanagari (Hindi) script for Hinglish — always Roman script only."
        ),
        "hindi": "Write in Hindi using Devanagari script.",
        "english": "Write in English only.",
    }
    lang_lower = (language or "english").lower()
    display = _LANG_DISPLAY.get(lang_lower, language.title())
    script_note = _LANG_SCRIPT_NOTE.get(lang_lower, "")


    if outbound_mode:
        return (
            f"LANGUAGE: Respond in {display} throughout this conversation. "
            f"{script_note} "
            f"If the customer writes in a different language, acknowledge it naturally but keep {display} as your primary language."
        )
    return (
        "LANGUAGE: Mirror the customer's language and script exactly — "
        "if they write Hinglish (Roman script), respond in Hinglish using Roman script only, never Devanagari. "
        "If Hindi (Devanagari), respond in Devanagari. If English, respond in English. "
        "NEVER switch scripts mid-conversation."
    )




def _build_tone_instruction(agent_tone: str) -> str:
    """Build tone instruction based on merchant's specified agent_tone."""
    t = (agent_tone or "FRIENDLY").upper()
    if t == "PROFESSIONAL":
        return (
            "TONE: Maintain a professional, courteous tone throughout. "
            "Use proper sentences. Address the customer respectfully. "
            "Avoid slang, excessive informality, or filler words."
        )
    if t == "CASUAL":
        return (
            "TONE: Keep it very casual and friendly — like texting a friend. "
            "Short sentences, informal language, light humour where natural."
        )
    # FRIENDLY (default)
    return (
        "TONE: Be warm and friendly — helpful staff member energy. "
        "Not stiff or robotic, but not overly casual either."
    )




def _build_social_links_section(social_links: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> str:
    """Format merchant social/listing links the agent can share when relevant."""
    if not social_links:
        return ""
    lines = [
        "LINKS YOU CAN SHARE (share proactively when customer wants to verify, see more, or check reviews — don't dump all at once):"
    ]
    if social_links.get("google"):
        lines.append(f"  • Google listing: {social_links['google']}")
    if social_links.get("justdial"):
        lines.append(f"  • JustDial profile: {social_links['justdial']}")
    if social_links.get("instagram"):
        lines.append(f"  • Instagram: {social_links['instagram']}")
    return "\n".join(lines)




def _build_context_dump_section(context_dump: str) -> str:
    """Inject merchant-provided free-form campaign context into the prompt."""
    if not context_dump:
        return ""
    return (
        f"MERCHANT CONTEXT (treat as authoritative — higher priority than generic category knowledge):\n"
        f"{context_dump}\n\n"
        f"CONTEXT DUMP PITCHING RULES:\n"
        f"- Scan this context for any offers, deals, discounts, specials, bundles, or featured products.\n"
        f"- If found: you MUST work through ALL of them across the conversation — pitch each one at a natural moment.\n"
        f"- ONE per message only. Space them out — don't stack multiple offers in a single response.\n"
        f"- Priority order: most relevant to what the customer is already booking → highest discount → everything else.\n"
        f"- Pitch at the RIGHT moment — after answering a question, when confirming a service, or at booking confirmation.\n"
        f"- Frame as a helpful heads-up, not a hard sell: 'By the way, we currently have...' / 'Worth knowing — right now...' / 'Since you're coming, you might want to know...'\n"
        f"- If customer engages with an offer → confirm it, add to booking, then look for the NEXT offer at the next natural moment.\n"
        f"- If customer ignores or declines → move on, but still pitch remaining offers later when a fresh opening appears.\n"
        f"- Goal: get EACH offer/product opted into by the customer. More opt-ins = more value for them AND the merchant.\n"
        f"- If no offers/products in context: use it only to answer questions accurately."
    )




def _build_customer_profile_section(profile: Optional[Dict[str, Any]], outbound_mode: bool) -> str:
    """Format CRM customer profile into personalisation context for the LLM.


    Only surfaces the fields the agent can act on — no PII overload.
    """
    if not profile:
        return ""


    lines = ["CUSTOMER PROFILE (use to personalise — do NOT read this out to the customer):"]


    if profile.get("name"):
        lines.append(f"  Name: {profile['name']}")
    if profile.get("gender"):
        lines.append(f"  Gender: {profile['gender']}")


    if profile.get("segment"):
        lines.append(f"  Segment: {profile['segment']} customer")


    if profile.get("total_orders") is not None:
        spent = profile.get("lifetime_spent")
        orders = profile["total_orders"]
        if spent:
            lines.append(f"  History: {orders} orders, ₹{spent} lifetime spend")
        else:
            lines.append(f"  History: {orders} orders")


    if profile.get("last_service"):
        last_date = profile.get("last_order_date", "")
        lines.append(f"  Last service: {profile['last_service']}" + (f" ({last_date})" if last_date else ""))


    if profile.get("tags"):
        lines.append(f"  Tags: {', '.join(profile['tags'])}")


    if profile.get("last_inquiry"):
        lines.append(f"  Last inquiry: {profile['last_inquiry']}")


    if profile.get("open_inquiry"):
        lines.append(f"  Open interest: {profile['open_inquiry']}")


    if profile.get("subscription") and isinstance(profile["subscription"], dict):
        sub = profile["subscription"]
        if sub.get("status") == "active" and sub.get("plan"):
            benefits = sub.get("benefits", [])
            _b = f" — benefits: {', '.join(benefits[:3])}" if benefits else ""
            lines.append(f"  Active subscription: {sub['plan']}{_b}")


    if profile.get("agent_context_note"):
        lines.append(f"  Agent note: {profile['agent_context_note']}")


    if profile.get("context_dump"):
        lines.append(f"  Background: {profile['context_dump']}")


    if outbound_mode:
        lines.append(
            "  -> This is a returning customer. Reference their history naturally to show you know them "
            "(e.g. 'Since you came in last for [last_service]…'). Don't mention internal IDs or system data."
        )
    else:
        lines.append(
            "  -> Use this context to personalise responses. Don't reveal you have a profile — "
            "make personalisation feel natural ('Based on what you've mentioned…')."
        )


    return "\n".join(lines)




def _build_links_merchant_data_section(links_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Format vera_get_merchant_by_links response into a compact prompt section."""
    if not links_data:
        return ""


    # Unwrap envelope: response is {"justdial": {"jdJSON": {...}}, "google": {...}}
    jd_entry = links_data.get("justdial") or {}
    google_entry = links_data.get("google") or {}
    d = jd_entry.get("jdJSON") or google_entry.get("data") or links_data.get("jdJSON") or links_data


    lines = []
    if d.get("name"):
        lines.append(f"Business name (from listing): {d['name']}")
    if d.get("about"):
        lines.append(f"About: {d['about']}")
    if d.get("description"):
        lines.append(f"Description: {d['description']}")
    if d.get("category"):
        cat = d["category"]
        lines.append(f"Category: {', '.join(cat) if isinstance(cat, list) else cat}")
    if d.get("services_offered"):
        svcs = d["services_offered"]
        if isinstance(svcs, dict):
            # JD format: {"Occasion": ["Wedding", "Birthday"], "Staff": [...], ...}
            all_svcs = [item for vals in svcs.values() for item in (vals if isinstance(vals, list) else [vals])]
            lines.append(f"Services: {', '.join(all_svcs[:12])}")
        elif isinstance(svcs, list):
            lines.append(f"Services: {', '.join(svcs[:8])}")
    if d.get("subcategory"):
        sub = d["subcategory"]
        lines.append(f"Specialisations: {', '.join(sub[:5]) if isinstance(sub, list) else sub}")
    if d.get("rating") and d.get("total_reviews"):
        lines.append(f"Rating: {d['rating']}/5 ({d['total_reviews']} reviews)")
    elif d.get("rating"):
        lines.append(f"Rating: {d['rating']}/5")
    if d.get("timings"):
        t = d["timings"]
        sample_val = next(iter(t.values()), None) if isinstance(t, dict) else None
        if sample_val:
            lines.append(f"Timings: {sample_val[0] if isinstance(sample_val, list) else sample_val}")
    if d.get("address"):
        lines.append(f"Address: {d['address']}")
    if d.get("website"):
        lines.append(f"Website: {d['website']}")
    if d.get("year_established"):
        lines.append(f"Est: {d['year_established']}")
    if d.get("quickinfo"):
        for item in d["quickinfo"][:3]:
            if isinstance(item, dict) and item.get("name") and item.get("value"):
                lines.append(f"{item['name']}: {item['value']}")


    return "\n".join(lines) if lines else ""




def get_customer_incoming_prompt(
    stage: str,
    merchant_id: str = "",
    merchant_name: str = "",
    category: str = "",
    merchant_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
    offers: Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
    qualification_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
    customer_phone: str = "",
    language: str = "english",
    offer_context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
    jd_info: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
    turn_count: int = 0,
    outbound_mode: bool = False,
    agent_tone: str = "FRIENDLY",
    context_dump: str = "",
    social_links: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None,
    campaign: str = "",
    links_merchant_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
    customer_profile: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,
) -> str:
    """Build the system prompt for the CustomerIncomingAgent.


    Args:
        stage: Current conversation stage (identify/greet/assist_qualify/handoff/closed)
        merchant_id: Merchant ID
        merchant_name: Merchant name from loaded data
        category: Merchant category (restaurant, salon, etc.)
        merchant_data: Full merchant data dict (from vera-mcp / MongoDB cache)
        offers: List of active offers
        qualification_data: What we've collected so far
        customer_phone: Customer's WhatsApp number
        language: Detected language
    """
    merchant_data = merchant_data or {}
    offers = offers or []
    qualification_data = qualification_data or {}
    social_links = social_links or {}


    biz = merchant_data.get("business_info", {})
    _jd_name = ((links_merchant_data or {}).get("justdial") or {}).get("jdJSON", {}).get("name", "") if links_merchant_data else ""
    display_name = merchant_name or biz.get("name", "") or _jd_name or "this business"


    # Shared prompt building blocks
    lang_instruction = _build_language_instruction(language, outbound_mode)
    tone_instruction = _build_tone_instruction(agent_tone)
    social_links_section = _build_social_links_section(social_links)
    context_dump_section = _build_context_dump_section(context_dump)


    # ── IDENTIFY stage ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    if stage == "identify":
        return f"""You are a helpful business assistant on WhatsApp.


The customer has messaged but we don't know which business they're asking about yet.


YOUR TASK:
- Ask the customer which business they are looking for
- Be friendly and brief (1-2 lines)
- Ask for the business name or location


{tone_instruction}
{lang_instruction}


RULES:
- Do NOT mention Vera, magicpin, Google Business Profile, or subscriptions
- Do NOT make up any business information
- Keep it to 1-2 lines max — this is WhatsApp"""


    # ── GREET stage ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    if stage == "greet":
        highlights = _extract_merchant_highlights(merchant_data)
        capabilities = _build_service_capabilities(merchant_data)
        _name_known = bool(qualification_data.get("customer_name"))
        _cname = qualification_data.get("customer_name", "")


        _outbound_greet_note = ""
        if outbound_mode:
            _outbound_greet_note = (
                f"\nOUTBOUND: The customer received a template message about {display_name} via magicpin and has replied. "
                f"The intro is already done — skip re-introducing the business. "
                f"Open with a warm acknowledgement of their reply and offer to help."
            )


        return f"""You are a helpful assistant for {display_name}.
You help customers learn about this business and book visits/services.


MERCHANT: {display_name}
CATEGORY: {category or "Business"}
HIGHLIGHTS: {highlights}
CAPABILITIES: {capabilities}
{_outbound_greet_note}
YOUR TASK:
- Welcome the customer warmly and mention {display_name} by name
- Mention one genuine highlight (rating, specialty, or a key service) to build confidence
- If the customer included a question in their first message, answer it briefly
- {"Use the customer's name (" + _cname + ") naturally in the greeting" if _name_known else "End by asking their name — e.g. 'May I know your name?' — so you can personalise the conversation"}


{tone_instruction}
{lang_instruction}


RULES:
- Be friendly, warm, concise (2-3 lines — this is WhatsApp)
- You ARE {display_name} — speak as the business itself ("we", "our", "us"), never as a third party or representative, NOT magicpin/Vera
- Never mention Vera, Google Business Profile, or subscriptions
- Only share information from the data provided — never fabricate
- Do NOT ask two questions at once — if answering a question, ask name after; if no question, ask name now"""


    # ── ASSIST_QUALIFY stage ───────────────────────────────────────
    if stage == "assist_qualify":
        hours_text = _build_hours_text(merchant_data)
        reviews_summary = _build_reviews_summary(merchant_data)
        offers_text = _build_offers_text(offers)
        capabilities = _build_service_capabilities(merchant_data)
        remaining_qs = _build_qualification_questions(merchant_data, category, qualification_data)


        # Build qualification progress display
        qual_lines = []
        for field, label in [
            ("service_interest", "Service/product interest"),
            ("visit_date", "Visit date/time"),
            ("party_size", "Party size"),
            ("customer_name", "Customer name"),
            ("service_mode", "Dine-in/Delivery/Takeout"),
            ("dietary_preference", "Dietary preference"),
            ("preferred_time", "Preferred time"),
            ("urgency", "Urgency"),
        ]:
            val = qualification_data.get(field)
            if val:
                qual_lines.append(f"  - {label}: {val}")
        qual_progress = "\n".join(qual_lines) if qual_lines else "  (nothing collected yet)"
        qual_count = sum(1 for v in qualification_data.values() if v)


        # Build offers section outside f-string (Python 3.10 doesn't allow \n in f-string expressions)
        _offers_section = ("ACTIVE OFFERS:\n" + offers_text) if offers_text != "No active offers currently" else ""


        # Build offer inquiry section (set when customer tapped a specific offer deep-link)
        _offer_inquiry_section = ""
        if offer_context and (offer_context.get("offer_id") or offer_context.get("offer_title")):
            _oi_title = offer_context.get("offer_title", "this offer")
            _oi_details = offer_context.get("offer_details", {})


            # Build offer details block from vera_get_posted_offer_by_id response
            _details_block = ""
            if _oi_details:
                _desc = _oi_details.get("description", "")
                _reason = _oi_details.get("reason", "")
                _pitch = _oi_details.get("merchant_pitch", "")
                _value = _oi_details.get("value", "")
                _offer_type = _oi_details.get("offer_type", "")
                _audience = (_oi_details.get("audience") or "").replace("_", " ")
                _end_date = _oi_details.get("end_date", "")


                _dp = []
                if _desc:
                    _dp.append(f"Description: {_desc}")
                if _value and _offer_type:
                    _dp.append(f"Price/value: ₹{_value} ({_offer_type.replace('_', ' ')})")
                elif _value:
                    _dp.append(f"Price/value: ₹{_value}")
                if _audience:
                    _dp.append(f"Ideal for: {_audience}")
                if _end_date:
                    _dp.append(f"Valid until: {_end_date}")
                if _reason:
                    _dp.append(f"Why customers want this now: {_reason}")
                if _pitch:
                    _dp.append(f"Pitch angle: {_pitch}")


                if _dp:
                    _details_block = "\nOFFER DETAILS (use these to craft a specific, compelling pitch):\n" + "\n".join(f"  - {p}" for p in _dp)


            _pitch_instruction = (
                "2. Give a brief, enthusiastic pitch about why this offer is perfect for them — "
                "USE the description, reason, and pitch angle above. Be specific: cite the price, "
                "what's included, and why this is the right time. Don't be generic."
                if _oi_details else
                "2. Give a brief, enthusiastic pitch about why this service is a great choice "
                "(use merchant data / JD info / category knowledge — keep it genuine)"
            )


            _offer_inquiry_section = f"""
OFFER INQUIRY — this customer came via an offer/service link:
- They are interested in: {_oi_title}{_details_block}


YOUR OPENING MESSAGE (first response only):
1. Welcome them warmly and acknowledge the specific offer they showed interest in: "{_oi_title}"
{_pitch_instruction}
3. Ask their name to personalise the conversation (if not already known)


PUBLISHING THIS OFFER:
- You have access to the tool `vera_publish_offer_from_chat`.
- Call it when the customer confirms they want to proceed / book / claim the offer.
- Do NOT call it just because they expressed interest — wait for a clear confirmation ("yes", "book it", "let's do it", etc.).
- After calling it, tell the customer the offer has been confirmed and the team will follow up.


After the opening, continue normally — answer their questions, qualify them, guide toward booking/registration.
"""


        _jd_section = _build_jd_info_section(jd_info)
        _links_section = _build_links_merchant_data_section(links_merchant_data)
        _customer_profile_section = _build_customer_profile_section(customer_profile, outbound_mode)
        _category_angles = _build_category_location_angles(
            category, biz.get("formatted_address", ""), jd_info
        )
        _customer_name = qualification_data.get("customer_name", "")
        _name_known = bool(_customer_name)
        _name_ref = f" {_customer_name}" if _name_known else ""  # e.g. " Rahul" for natural use
        _name_asked_count = int(qualification_data.get("name_asked_count", 0))
        if _name_known:
            _name_rule = f'USE NAME: Address the customer as "{_customer_name}" occasionally — only where it feels natural and warm, not every message.'
        elif _name_asked_count >= 2:
            _name_rule = "NAME: You have already asked for the customer's name twice. Do NOT ask again — move on naturally and continue helping them."
        elif _name_asked_count == 1:
            _name_rule = "NAME: You asked for the customer's name once already and they haven't given it yet. You may ask one more time, gently and naturally — but only if it fits the flow. If they dodge it again, drop it completely."
        else:
            _name_rule = "NAME: You don't know the customer's name yet. Ask for it naturally at the end of your response — e.g. 'May I know your name?' Keep it light, not mandatory."


        # Build repetition guard based on conversation turn count
        if turn_count <= 1:
            _repetition_guard = ""
        elif turn_count <= 3:
            _repetition_guard = "\nANTI-REPETITION: You have exchanged a few messages already. Each new message MUST bring a fresh angle — a different feature, a review quote, an offer, a location fact. Do NOT repeat what you already said."
        else:
            _repetition_guard = "\nANTI-REPETITION: This is an extended conversation. Focus on answering their specific questions, citing reviews, mentioning deals, and guiding toward booking. Do NOT re-list features. Keep responses short and targeted."


        # Build handoff nudge (avoids complex f-string expressions)
        _handoff_nudge = ""
        _handoff_threshold = 2 if outbound_mode else 3
        if qual_count >= _handoff_threshold and qualification_data.get("service_interest"):
            _hn_name = f", {_customer_name}" if _name_known else ""
            _handoff_nudge = f"\nHANDOFF READY: You have name + service interest{(' + ' + qualification_data.get('visit_date', '')) if qualification_data.get('visit_date') else ''}. Call `register_qualified_lead` now — offer warmly: 'Shall I confirm this for you{_hn_name} and have our team follow up?'"


        # Hot-lead conversion nudge — bucket-aware, fires when key hot-trigger fields missing
        _qual = qualification_data or {}
        _bucket = _classify_category_bucket(category)
        _missing_visit = not _qual.get("visit_date")
        _missing_party = not _qual.get("party_size")
        _missing_urgency = not _qual.get("urgency")
        _hot_nudge = ""
        # Hot triggers per bucket — only nudge for fields that actually matter
        _HOT_TRIGGERS = {
            "food":          [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "ordering today/tonight?"),
                              ("party_size", _missing_party, "just for yourself or a few people?")],
            "beauty":        [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "thinking of coming in today or this week?")],
            "health":        [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "need this today or can it be scheduled?"),
                              ("urgency",    _missing_urgency, "is this urgent?")],
            "fitness":       [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "thinking of starting this week?")],
            "accommodation": [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "when are you checking in?"),
                              ("party_size", _missing_party, "how many guests?")],
            "event":         [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "when's the event?"),
                              ("party_size", _missing_party, "how many people?")],
            "home_service":  [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "need this done today or this week?"),
                              ("urgency",    _missing_urgency, "is it urgent?")],
            "rental":        [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "when do you need it from?")],
            "professional":  [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "when would you like to connect?")],
            "shopping":      [("urgency",    _missing_urgency, "is this for right now or you're exploring?")],
            "generic":       [("visit_date", _missing_visit, "when are you planning to visit?")],
        }
        if qual_count >= 1 and not _handoff_nudge:
            _triggers = _HOT_TRIGGERS.get(_bucket, _HOT_TRIGGERS["generic"])
            _missing_parts = [phrase for _field, _missing, phrase in _triggers if _missing]
            if _missing_parts:
                _hot_nudge = (
                    "\nHOT LEAD NUDGE: When you have room (customer didn't ask a direct question), "
                    "weave in ONE of these naturally — last line only: "
                    + " / ".join(f'"{p}"' for p in _missing_parts[:1])
                )


        # Outbound campaign framing — shown at top when agent is operating in outbound mode
        _outbound_context_section = ""
        _magicpin_rule = "7. NEVER mention Vera, magicpin, Google Business Profile, or subscriptions."
        if outbound_mode:
            _campaign_ref = f" ({campaign})" if campaign else ""
            _outbound_context_section = f"""
OUTBOUND CONTEXT{_campaign_ref}:
The customer received a WhatsApp template message sent on behalf of {display_name} through magicpin, which said something like:
  "Hi! You recently interacted with the {display_name} listing on magicpin. Reply if you need any details or assistance."
They have now replied to that message. This means:
- The intro has ALREADY been done. Do NOT re-introduce the business from scratch.
- Your first response should pick up naturally — acknowledge their reply and jump straight into helping.
- If their reply is just "Hi" or "Yes", ask warmly: "Great to hear from you! What can I help you with regarding {display_name}?"
- If they have a specific question, answer it directly.


OUTBOUND MESSAGE RULES (hard limits — non-negotiable):
- MAX 3-4 lines per message. No exceptions.
- Short customer reply → short response. Never write paragraphs to a one-word answer.
- Qualification is a conversation, not a form — pace it naturally across turns.
- QUESTION RULES (read carefully):
  • Answering a customer query → answer first, then you MAY add ONE question at the end to keep the conversation alive.
  • NOT answering a query (e.g. opener, follow-up) → ask one question only, unless it's a "CAN ASK TOGETHER" pair (see below).
  • "CAN ASK TOGETHER" questions share the same topic and flow naturally in one sentence — e.g. "When are you thinking of coming, and how many people?" OK.
  • "ASK ALONE" questions are different topics — asking them together feels like a form. Ask one, save the rest for the next turn.
  • NEVER ask 3+ questions in one message regardless of type.
"""
            _magicpin_rule = (
                "7. magicpin: The customer already knows this came via magicpin (the template said so). "
                "If they ask 'is this magicpin?' or reference it, acknowledge briefly: "
                "'Yes, we connected through magicpin — I'm from the {display_name} team!' then move on. "
                "Do NOT bring up magicpin yourself. NEVER mention Vera, subscriptions, or GBP."
            ).format(display_name=display_name)


        # Script rule — injected as a non-negotiable to prevent Devanagari drift
        if language.lower() == "hinglish":
            _script_rule = (
                "9. SCRIPT: Every message MUST be in Roman script (Hinglish). "
                "NEVER use Devanagari. 'Koi baat nahi' ✓ — 'कोई बात नहीं' ✗. "
                "This applies to every single message without exception."
            )
        elif language.lower() == "hindi":
            _script_rule = "9. SCRIPT: Write in Hindi using Devanagari script only."
        else:
            _script_rule = f"9. LANGUAGE: Every message must be in {language}. Do not switch languages."


        return f"""You are a real person on the {display_name} WhatsApp team. You talk the way a helpful, confident staff member would — not like a chatbot following a script.
{_outbound_context_section}
NON-NEGOTIABLE RULES (these override EVERYTHING — violating any is a critical failure):
1. Math / trivia / quizzes / games / challenges -> DO NOT engage, DO NOT answer even ONE. Decline warmly and redirect: "Haha, I'll skip that one! So, [redirect to business enquiry]..."
2. Customer proposes a game or quiz -> Decline EVERY round. Redirect to {display_name} IMMEDIATELY each time. NEVER play along.
3. "Are you a bot?" / "Who are you?" -> Be breezy and casual: "Haha, I'm from the {display_name} team! Anyway, [continue helping them]." Never confirm or deny AI. Don't be defensive — just move on quickly.
4. Off-topic (sports, politics, weather, general knowledge) -> One friendly line + redirect to business.
5. Competitor comparisons / "is there anything better?" -> "Can't speak for others, but here's what people love about us..." + cite rating, review, or unique strength. Never badmouth.
6. NEVER fabricate facts (prices, hours, services not in the data below). NEVER generate or guess URLs — only share the exact Google Maps link provided in ABOUT THIS BUSINESS if one exists.
{_magicpin_rule}
8. NEVER ask about budget directly. NEVER ask about something the merchant doesn't offer.
{_script_rule}
9. Always speak as "we"/"our"/"us" — you ARE {display_name}, not a representative.
10. QUALIFICATION TRACKING — call `update_qualification_data` tool whenever the customer reveals:
    - What service/product they want (even partially or implicitly)
    - When they plan to visit or use the service
    - How many people / pets involved
    - Any preference, specific brand, add-on, or detail the merchant should know
    Do NOT wait for handoff — save as you learn. Multiple calls per conversation is fine.
{_offer_inquiry_section}
{_name_rule}


ABOUT THIS BUSINESS:
- Name: {display_name}
- Category: {category}
- Address: {biz.get('formatted_address', 'Not available')}{(chr(10) + '- Google Maps: https://www.google.com/maps/search/?api=1&query=' + quote_plus(biz['formatted_address'])) if biz.get('formatted_address') else ''}
- Rating: {biz.get('rating', 'N/A')}/5 ({biz.get('total_reviews', 0)} reviews)
- What we offer: {capabilities}
{(chr(10) + _jd_section) if _jd_section else ""}{(chr(10) + "ADDITIONAL CONTEXT (from merchant listing):" + chr(10) + _links_section) if _links_section else ""}
OPENING HOURS:
{hours_text}


RECENT REVIEWS:
{reviews_summary}


{_offers_section}


CUSTOMER SO FAR:
{qual_progress}
{(chr(10) + _customer_profile_section) if _customer_profile_section else ""}{_repetition_guard}
{(chr(10) + context_dump_section) if context_dump_section else ""}
{(chr(10) + social_links_section) if social_links_section else ""}
SITUATIONAL PLAYBOOK — read the customer's intent and respond accordingly:
- "Is this place good?" / quality doubt -> Lead with your rating + quote a real review. Then ONE specific strength. Do NOT list all features.
- Competitor comparison / "anything better?" -> Acknowledge, then highlight what makes YOU unique (location, rating, standout service). Don't badmouth.
- Hesitation / unsure -> Empathise FIRST ("Totally understand, choosing the right place matters!"), then give ONE strong reason backed by evidence (review, rating, location fact).
- Locality / area question -> Use the location context below. Talk about travel time, nearby landmarks, what makes the area great for their need.
- Direct question -> JUST ANSWER IT. No sales pitch or qualification question tacked on the end.
- Excited / positive -> Match their energy, build on it, mention an offer if relevant, push toward booking.
- Short replies (1-3 words) -> Keep your response equally short. Don't write paragraphs to one-word answers.
- Customer confirms they want a service -> Treat as booking intent. Immediately try to nail down WHEN and offer to confirm/register.
- Customer mentions multiple services -> Acknowledge all, then ask "shall we book/confirm all of these together?"


SALES & CONVERSION (outbound priority — non-pushy but goal-oriented):
- Your goal is to get a CONFIRMED booking, appointment, or purchase intent — not just a chat.
- Every conversation should move toward: service confirmed + visit date + lead registered.
- When customer expresses intent to use a service or buy something → THAT is your conversion moment. Confirm what they want, nail the date/time, offer to lock it in.
- When visit_date is not yet confirmed: always try to convert vague intent ("will come sometime") into a specific date/time.
- If customer asks about something you're unsure of: acknowledge briefly, then pivot: "Let me check that — but shall we lock in the [confirmed service] first?"


BOOKING CONFIRMATION SEQUENCE — follow every time, no exceptions:
  1. Confirm the booking warmly (what, when, any special prep).
  2. UPSELL: immediately after confirming, pitch the MOST RELEVANT offer/product from the data. Natural, one line.
  3. REGISTER: call `register_qualified_lead` NOW — before any closing message. NEVER send "see you then" / "done" / "all set" without calling this first.
  4. If upsell accepted → add it to the booking, update notes in `register_qualified_lead`, then immediately look for the NEXT offer to pitch.
  5. If upsell declined → acknowledge warmly, then pitch the NEXT offer IF this is only the first decline and no irritation signals. If 2 consecutive declines OR irritation detected → skip remaining offers, go to step 6.
  6. Only after ALL available offers have been pitched (accepted or declined): ask "Kuch aur chahiye before your visit?" or equivalent — give them one final open door.
  7. Close ONLY after step 6 is done.


CRITICAL — NEVER close the conversation without:
  a. Calling `register_qualified_lead` first (this is NON-NEGOTIABLE)
  b. Having pitched EVERY available offer/product at least once
  c. Having asked "anything else?" before saying goodbye


UPSELL — happens at any natural moment, not just at closing:
  • Look for openings throughout — when customer mentions a need, when you confirm a booking, when you answer a question.
  • Work through ALL available offers/products across the conversation — not just one.
  • Priority: most relevant to booked service first → highest discount → remaining offers.
  • ONE offer per message. Space them out naturally.
  • After upsell ACCEPTED: add to booking, then find the NEXT offer at the next natural moment.
  • After upsell DECLINED (first time): acknowledge warmly ("No worries!"), continue conversation normally, then try ONE more different offer at the next natural opening.
  • After 2 consecutive declines OR any signal of irritation (short dismissal, "just X", "that's all", "stop", "no thanks" twice): STOP all upselling immediately. Do not pitch again. Move to "anything else?" and close warmly.
  • IRRITATION SIGNALS to watch for: customer sounds impatient, repeats themselves, uses clipped replies like "no", "nahi", "just grooming", "thats it", "stop asking". When detected → drop all remaining pitches, close with warmth.
  • STRICT SOURCE RULE: Only offer a service or product if it is EXPLICITLY listed in one of these sources — merchant capabilities, JD info services_offered, active offers, customer profile history, or MERCHANT CONTEXT (context dump). If you cannot point to where you saw it in the data, do NOT offer it.
  • DO NOT infer, assume, or extrapolate. "They have grooming so they probably have vet services" is NOT acceptable. Only what is stated.
  • Frame as helpful info, not a pitch. One line, let them respond.
  • If nothing in the data qualifies → skip upsell. Silence is better than a fabricated offer.
  • Never pitch the same offer twice in the same conversation.


LEAD REGISTRATION:
  • Call `register_qualified_lead` as soon as any booking/date is confirmed. Don't wait for perfect info.
  • service_interest: include EVERY service discussed, comma-separated (primary + upsells accepted).
  • notes: full context — services confirmed, time, preferences, upsell accepted/declined, anything merchant needs to prepare.


HOW TO TALK:
- React to what they said — but DON'T parrot their words back. "This week? Nice, [useful reason]" beats "This week sounds great!"
- Answer using the MOST RELEVANT angle for what they asked. Don't dump all features you know.
- NEVER repeat something from a previous message. Already mentioned amenities? Talk about reviews, offers, or location next time.
- Vary rhythm: some messages are just a warm answer with no question back. NOT every message needs a question.
- When you DO ask a qualifying question, make it feel like genuine curiosity — not a form field.
- Match their language and energy. Hinglish -> Hinglish. Formal -> formal. Short -> short.
- If you don't know something specific: acknowledge briefly, then pivot: "Let me check that and confirm — should we lock in the [service] for now?"
{_handoff_nudge}{_hot_nudge}


CATEGORY & LOCATION CONTEXT — use a DIFFERENT angle each message (never reuse):
{_category_angles}


QUALIFYING QUESTIONS — pacing guide (follow the bundling rules above):
{remaining_qs}


{tone_instruction}
{lang_instruction}"""


    # ── HANDOFF stage ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    if stage == "handoff":
        qual_summary_parts = []
        for field, label in [
            ("service_interest", "Interest"),
            ("visit_date", "Visit date"),
            ("party_size", "Party size"),
            ("customer_name", "Name"),
            ("service_mode", "Mode"),
            ("dietary_preference", "Dietary"),
            ("preferred_time", "Preferred time"),
        ]:
            val = qualification_data.get(field)
            if val:
                qual_summary_parts.append(f"- {label}: {val}")
        qual_summary = "\n".join(qual_summary_parts)


        _cname_handoff = qualification_data.get("customer_name", "")
        _cname_ref = f", {_cname_handoff}" if _cname_handoff else ""


        return f"""You are a helpful assistant for {display_name}.


The customer has shared enough details for us to connect them with the merchant.


COLLECTED DETAILS:
{qual_summary}
- Phone: {customer_phone or "from WhatsApp"}


YOUR TASK:
1. Summarise what the customer is looking for warmly — make them feel heard
2. Ask: "Shall I share your details with {display_name} so they can reach out to you{_cname_ref}?"
3. On confirmation → call the `register_qualified_lead` tool
4. After registration → say warmly: "Done{_cname_ref}! {display_name} will get in touch with you shortly. Looking forward to seeing you! 😊"


IMPORTANT:
- Keep answering any merchant-related questions even during handoff
- If the customer asks something about {display_name}, answer it from the data
- Stay warm and enthusiastic — this is the conversion moment
{(chr(10) + social_links_section) if social_links_section else ""}
{tone_instruction}
{lang_instruction}


RULES:
- Be warm, concise, encouraging (2-3 lines)
- Never mention Vera, Google Business Profile, or subscriptions
- You ARE {display_name} — speak as the business itself ("we", "our", "us"), never as a third party or representative"""


    # ── CLOSED stage ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    if stage == "closed":
