        return f"""You are a helpful assistant for {display_name}.


The customer's lead has been registered and {display_name} has been notified.


YOUR TASK:
- Continue answering any questions the customer has about {display_name}
- If they share new information (different service, different date), note it
- Be helpful and friendly — the conversation doesn't end at handoff


MERCHANT DATA IS STILL AVAILABLE — use it to answer questions.
{(chr(10) + social_links_section) if social_links_section else ""}
{tone_instruction}
{lang_instruction}


RULES:
- Stay helpful and answer merchant-related questions
- Keep messages to 2-3 lines
- Never mention Vera, Google Business Profile, or subscriptions
- You ARE {display_name} — speak as the business itself ("we", "our", "us"), never as a third party or representative
- If they want to change their booking details, let them know the merchant will confirm directly"""


    # Fallback
    return f"You are a helpful assistant for {display_name}. Answer customer questions about this business. {lang_instruction}"








**Challenge-useful conversation/state patterns**
- [agents/vera/followup_state.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/agents/vera/followup_state.py)
- """
Follow-up lifecycle state resolver for NewVeraSalesAgent.


Reference implementation of FollowupStateResolver for Vera WhatsApp sales.
Self-registers at import time — just import this module in run_followup_poller.py.


Lifecycle states (priority order)
-----------------------------------
OPTED_OUT           hard stop signals → terminal, cancel chain
SUBSCRIBED          Redis state=associated-paying → terminal, suppress silently
PAYMENT_LINK_SENT   pending payment link in Redis or chat
FREE_WRITE_USED     GBP write done, not yet activated
GBP_CONNECTED       connected, no write done yet
LINK_SENT           connect URL sent, merchant not replied since
ACTIVE_CONVERSATION merchant has replied, stalled
NOT_REPLIED         no merchant reply at all since outreach


Data sources (decreasing reliability)
---------------------------------------
Redis  vera:sales:v2:{mid}         → association state, decline_count
       vera:sales:v2:writes:{mid}  → write count
       vera:sales:v2:payment:{mid} → payment link + status
DB     MultiAgentChatHistory       → URL signals, hard-stop / soft-decline patterns
"""


import json
import logging
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import Optional, List


from utility.followup_state_base import FollowupState, FollowupStateResolver, register_resolver


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ── Redis key prefixes (must mirror NewVeraSalesAgent constants) ───────────────
_STATE_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:"
_WRITE_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:writes:"
_PAYMENT_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:payment:"


_VERA_STATE_NOT_PAYING = "associated-not-paying"
_VERA_STATE_PAYING = "associated-paying"


# ── Hard-stop patterns — true opt-out ─────────────────────────────────────────
_HARD_STOP_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(stop\s+messaging|don'?t\s+(?:contact|message)\s+me|do\s+not\s+contact|"
    r"remove\s+(?:me|number)|unsubscribe|block|hataao|band\s+karo|nahi\s+chahiye\s+kuch)\b",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)


# ── Soft-decline patterns — objection, not opt-out ────────────────────────────
_SOFT_DECLINE_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(nahi\b|no\b|not\s+interested|need\s+nahi|nahi\s+chahiye|"
    r"baad\s+mein|later|maybe\s+later|abhi\s+nahi|not\s+now|no\s+thanks|no\s+thank\s+you)\b",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)


# ── URL patterns ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
_VERA_URL_RE = re.compile(r"https?://vera\.magicpin\.com[^\s<>\"']*", re.IGNORECASE)
_PAYMENT_URL_RE = re.compile(
    r"https?://[^\s<>\"']*(?:pay\.magicpin|razorpay|cashfree|checkout)[^\s<>\"']*",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)


# ── Objection angles mapped to soft_decline_count ────────────────────────────
_OBJECTION_ANGLES = [
    "",   # 0 declines — no extra directive
    "NEXT ANGLE: Lead with urgency — unanswered reviews are hurting their ranking right now.",
    "NEXT ANGLE: Visibility gap — profile incomplete, competitors rank above them for the same searches.",
    "NEXT ANGLE: Zero-effort — Vera runs daily on autopilot, they do nothing. Frame as set-and-forget.",
    "NEXT ANGLE: Low-risk close — Rs 499/month to activate, cancel anytime, no contract. Ask if worth trying once.",
]


# ── Internal helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────


def _extract_gbp_signals(state_data: Optional[dict]) -> str:
    """
    Pull the most salient GBP signal from cached Redis state_data so follow-up
    triggers can cite it inline — no tool call needed from the agent.


    Returns a single human-readable line, or "" if no signal is available.
    """
    if not state_data:
        return ""
    sd = state_data
    # Priority: unanswered reviews > rating < 4 > low review count
    unanswered = sd.get("unanswered_review_count") or sd.get("pending_reviews")
    if unanswered and int(unanswered) > 0:
        return f"You have {unanswered} unanswered review(s) on Google — hurting your ranking right now."
    rating = sd.get("rating") or sd.get("google_rating")
    try:
        rating = float(rating)
        if rating < 4.0:
            return f"Your Google rating is {rating:.1f} — below the 4.0 threshold most customers filter by."
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        pass
    review_count = sd.get("review_count") or sd.get("total_reviews")
    try:
        review_count = int(review_count)
        if review_count < 10:
            return f"Your profile has only {review_count} Google reviews — competitors in your area have far more."
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        pass
    return ""


def _hours_since(ts: Optional[datetime]) -> float:
    if not ts:
        return 0.0
    if ts.tzinfo is None:
        ts = ts.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    return max(0.0, (datetime.now(timezone.utc) - ts).total_seconds() / 3600)


def _redis_json(client, key: str) -> Optional[dict]:
    try:
        raw = client.get(key)
        if not raw:
            return None
        return json.loads(raw.decode("utf-8") if isinstance(raw, bytes) else raw)
    except Exception as exc:
        logger.debug("Redis get %s failed: %s", key, exc)
        return None


def _redis_int(client, key: str) -> int:
    try:
        raw = client.get(key)
        return int(raw) if raw else 0
    except Exception:
        return 0


def _build_state_journey(messages: list, anchor: Optional[datetime]) -> str:
    """
    Build a compact state-transition timeline from chat history.


    Sequences three event types into chronological order:
      - Agent follow-up nudges  (source=proactive_followup in metadata, or [PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] prefix)
      - Merchant replies
      - Key URL events          (connect URL / payment link sent by agent)


    Times are expressed as hours relative to the first message (anchor).
    Returns a single-line string, e.g.:


      T+0h outreach →  T+2h nudge(NOT_REPLIED) → T+5h merchant-replied →
      T+8h connect-url-sent → T+32h nudge(LINK_SENT,charged) → T+33h merchant-replied
    """
    if not messages or not anchor:
        return ""
    if anchor.tzinfo is None:
        anchor = anchor.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)


    def _rel(ts: Optional[datetime]) -> str:
        if not ts:
            return "T+?h"
        if ts.tzinfo is None:
            ts = ts.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
        h = max(0.0, (ts - anchor).total_seconds() / 3600)
        return f"T+{h:.0f}h"


    events: List[tuple] = []  # (datetime, label)


    for m in messages:
        ts = m.created_at
        text = m.message or ""
        sender = m.sender or ""


        if sender == "whatsapp":
            # Merchant reply — record first word so we know if it's a yes/no/question
            preview = text.strip()[:30].replace("\n", " ")
            events.append((ts, f"merchant-replied({preview!r})"))


        elif sender in ("system", "agent", "NewVeraSalesAgent"):
            # Agent-side: detect follow-up nudges vs URL events
            is_followup = (
                text.startswith("[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP]")
                or text.startswith("[CHARGED_FOLLOWUP]")
            )
            if is_followup:
                # Extract lifecycle tag from the trigger text if present
                lifecycle_tag = ""
                lc_match = re.search(r"LIFECYCLE:\s*(\w+)", text)
                if lc_match:
                    lifecycle_tag = lc_match.group(1)
                charged = text.startswith("[CHARGED_FOLLOWUP]")
                label = f"nudge({lifecycle_tag}{',' if lifecycle_tag else ''}{'charged' if charged else 'free'})"
                events.append((ts, label))
            else:
                # Check for URL signals
                if _VERA_URL_RE.search(text):
                    events.append((ts, "connect-url-sent"))
                if _PAYMENT_URL_RE.search(text):
                    events.append((ts, "payment-link-sent"))


    if not events:
        return ""


    events.sort(key=lambda x: (x[0] or datetime.min.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)))
    parts = [f"{_rel(ts)} {label}" for ts, label in events]
    return " → ".join(parts)


# ── Resolver ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────


class NewVeraSalesAgentResolver(FollowupStateResolver):
    """Vera WhatsApp sales follow-up lifecycle resolver."""


    agent_type = "NewVeraSalesAgent"


    def resolve(
        self,
        session,
        ticket_id: int,
        context_data: dict,
        redis_client=None,
        max_soft_declines: int = 0,
    ) -> FollowupState:
        try:
            return self._resolve_inner(session, ticket_id, context_data, redis_client, max_soft_declines)
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.error("NewVeraSalesAgentResolver.resolve failed ticket=%s: %s", ticket_id, exc)
            return FollowupState(
                lifecycle="UNKNOWN",
                is_terminal=False,
                last_event_label="state resolution failed",
            )


    def _resolve_inner(
        self,
        session,
        ticket_id: int,
        context_data: dict,
        redis_client,
        max_soft_declines: int = 0,
    ) -> FollowupState:
        from utility.db_models import MultiAgentChatHistory


        merchant_id = str((context_data or {}).get("merchant_id", "") or "")
        phone = str((context_data or {}).get("phone_number", "") or "")


        # ── Chat history ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        messages: List[MultiAgentChatHistory] = (
            session.query(MultiAgentChatHistory)
            .filter(MultiAgentChatHistory.ticket_id == ticket_id)
            .order_by(MultiAgentChatHistory.created_at.asc())
            .all()
        )
        merchant_msgs = [m for m in messages if m.sender == "whatsapp"]
        agent_msgs = [m for m in messages if m.sender not in ("whatsapp", "system")]
        first_msg = messages[0] if messages else None
        last_merchant_msg = merchant_msgs[-1] if merchant_msgs else None
        has_replied = bool(merchant_msgs)


        # ── Sentiment signals from communicate_to_user tool args ──────────────
        # Primary source: model-classified merchant_sentiment stored in
        # agent_metadata when the agent calls communicate_to_user.
        # The model has full conversational context; this is more reliable than
        # regex on raw merchant text.
        # Fallback: regex on raw text for messages before this feature was deployed.
        agent_sentiments = [
            (m.agent_metadata or {}).get("merchant_sentiment")
            for m in agent_msgs
            if (m.agent_metadata or {}).get("merchant_sentiment")
        ]
        is_opted_out_from_sentiment = any(s == "hard_stop" for s in agent_sentiments)
        soft_decline_from_sentiment = sum(1 for s in agent_sentiments if s == "soft_decline")


        # Hard-stop: model classification first; regex fallback for legacy messages
        if is_opted_out_from_sentiment:
            is_opted_out = True
        else:
            recent_text = " ".join(m.message or "" for m in merchant_msgs[-5:])
            is_opted_out = bool(_HARD_STOP_RE.search(recent_text))


        # Soft-decline count: Redis (primary) > model sentiment (secondary) > regex (legacy)
        redis_state_data: Optional[dict] = None
        if redis_client and merchant_id:
            redis_state_data = _redis_json(redis_client, f"{_STATE_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            soft_decline_count = int((redis_state_data or {}).get("decline_count", 0))
        elif soft_decline_from_sentiment > 0:
            soft_decline_count = soft_decline_from_sentiment
        else:
            soft_decline_count = sum(
                1 for m in merchant_msgs if _SOFT_DECLINE_RE.search(m.message or "")
            )


        # ── Scan agent messages for lifecycle URL signals ─────────────────────
        connect_url: Optional[str] = None
        connect_sent_at: Optional[datetime] = None
        payment_link: Optional[str] = None
        payment_sent_at: Optional[datetime] = None


        for m in agent_msgs:
            text = m.message or ""
            if connect_url is None:
                hit = _VERA_URL_RE.search(text)
                if hit:
                    connect_url = hit.group(0)
                    connect_sent_at = m.created_at
            if payment_link is None:
                hit = _PAYMENT_URL_RE.search(text)
                if hit:
                    payment_link = hit.group(0)
                    payment_sent_at = m.created_at


        # ── Redis enrichment ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
        gbp_state = ""
        write_count = 0
        redis_payment_status = None


        if redis_client and merchant_id:
            if redis_state_data is None:
                redis_state_data = _redis_json(redis_client, f"{_STATE_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            gbp_state = (redis_state_data or {}).get("state", "")
            write_count = _redis_int(redis_client, f"{_WRITE_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            redis_payment = _redis_json(redis_client, f"{_PAYMENT_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            if redis_payment and redis_payment.get("payment_link"):
                payment_link = redis_payment["payment_link"]
                redis_payment_status = redis_payment.get("status")


        # ── GBP signals from cached state_data (avoids agent tool calls on follow-up) ──
        gbp_signals = _extract_gbp_signals(redis_state_data)


        # ── State transition journey (used by generic fallback trigger) ────────
        state_journey = _build_state_journey(
            messages, anchor=first_msg.created_at if first_msg else None
        )


        # ── WhatsApp 24h session window ────────────────────────────────────────
        # WhatsApp only allows free-form (session) messages within 24h of the
        # merchant's last inbound message.  Outside that window every message
        # sent by us must be a paid pre-approved template.
        # We track this so build_trigger() can suppress free-form follow-ups
        # rather than silently burning template budget or getting Kaleyra rejections.
        hours_since_last_merchant_msg = (
            _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at) if last_merchant_msg else float("inf")
        )
        wa_window_open = has_replied and hours_since_last_merchant_msg < 24.0


        # ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        def _state(lifecycle, hours, label, is_terminal=False, terminal_reason=""):
            return FollowupState(
                lifecycle=lifecycle,
                is_terminal=is_terminal,
                terminal_reason=terminal_reason,
                soft_decline_count=soft_decline_count,
                hours_since_last_event=hours,
                last_event_label=label,
                has_replied=has_replied,
                merchant_id=merchant_id,
                phone=phone,
                extra={
                    "connect_url": connect_url,
                    "payment_link": payment_link,
                    "gbp_signals": gbp_signals,
                    "wa_window_open": wa_window_open,
                    "hours_since_last_merchant_msg": hours_since_last_merchant_msg,
                    "state_journey": state_journey,
                },
            )


        # ── State classification (priority order) ──────────────────────────────


        if is_opted_out:
            return _state(
                "OPTED_OUT",
                _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None),
                "merchant sent hard stop signal",
                is_terminal=True,
                terminal_reason="opted out",
            )


        # ── Soft-decline limit — prevent persisting past genuine disinterest ───
        # Checked before any other non-terminal state so it takes priority.
        # max_soft_declines=0 means no limit (legacy / non-sales agents).
        if max_soft_declines > 0 and soft_decline_count >= max_soft_declines:
            return _state(
                "SOFT_DECLINE_LIMIT",
                _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None),
                f"merchant declined {soft_decline_count}x — objection angles exhausted",
                is_terminal=True,
                terminal_reason=f"soft decline limit reached ({soft_decline_count}/{max_soft_declines})",
            )


        if gbp_state == _VERA_STATE_PAYING:
            return _state(
                "SUBSCRIBED",
                _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None),
                "merchant is already subscribed",
                is_terminal=True,
                terminal_reason="subscribed — no follow-up needed",
            )


        is_payment_pending = bool(payment_link and redis_payment_status != "completed")
        if is_payment_pending:
            hours = _hours_since(payment_sent_at)
            return _state("PAYMENT_LINK_SENT", hours, f"payment link sent {hours:.0f}h ago")


        if gbp_state == _VERA_STATE_NOT_PAYING and write_count > 0:
            hours = _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None)
            return _state("FREE_WRITE_USED", hours, f"free GBP action done, last reply {hours:.0f}h ago")


        if gbp_state == _VERA_STATE_NOT_PAYING:
            hours = _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None)
            return _state("GBP_CONNECTED", hours, f"GBP connected, last reply {hours:.0f}h ago")


        if connect_url and connect_sent_at:
            merchant_replied_after_link = any(
                (m.created_at or datetime.min.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)) > connect_sent_at
                for m in merchant_msgs
            )
            if not merchant_replied_after_link:
                hours = _hours_since(connect_sent_at)
                return _state("LINK_SENT", hours, f"connect URL sent {hours:.0f}h ago, no reply yet")


        if has_replied:
            hours = _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at)
            return _state("ACTIVE_CONVERSATION", hours, f"merchant last replied {hours:.0f}h ago")


        hours = _hours_since(first_msg.created_at if first_msg else None)
        return _state("NOT_REPLIED", hours, f"outreach sent {hours:.0f}h ago, no reply yet")


    def build_trigger(
        self,
        state: FollowupState,
        attempt: int,
        max_attempts: int,
        max_charged_followups: int = 0,
    ) -> Optional[str]:
        if state.is_terminal:
            return None  # caller cancels the chain


        is_final = attempt >= max_attempts
        attempt_label = f"Attempt {attempt}/{max_attempts}" + (" — FINAL" if is_final else "")
        angle_idx = min(max(state.soft_decline_count, 0), len(_OBJECTION_ANGLES) - 1)
        angle = _OBJECTION_ANGLES[angle_idx]
        angle_line = f" {angle}" if angle else ""


        connect_url = (state.extra or {}).get("connect_url")
        payment_link = (state.extra or {}).get("payment_link")
        gbp_signals = (state.extra or {}).get("gbp_signals", "")
        wa_window_open: bool = (state.extra or {}).get("wa_window_open", False)
        hours_since_merchant = (state.extra or {}).get("hours_since_last_merchant_msg", -1)


        # ── WhatsApp 24h window gate ───────────────────────────────────────────
        # wa_window_open = merchant has replied AND their last message was < 24h ago.
        # When the window is closed, outbound messages must use a paid Meta template.
        #
        # Decision:
        #   window open                          → free session message, always proceed
        #   window closed, attempt <= threshold  → charged follow-up ([CHARGED_FOLLOWUP])
        #   window closed, attempt > threshold   → suppress (return None)
        #
        # max_charged_followups comes from AGENT_FOLLOWUP_CONFIG and defaults to 0
        # (suppress all out-of-window follow-ups unless explicitly budgeted).
        if not wa_window_open:
            if attempt <= max_charged_followups:
                logger.info(
                    "followup charged: wa_window_closed attempt=%d/%d lifecycle=%s "
                    "merchant_id=%s phone=%s hours_since_merchant_msg=%.0f",
                    attempt, max_charged_followups,
                    state.lifecycle, state.merchant_id, state.phone, hours_since_merchant,
                )
                # Caller detects [CHARGED_FOLLOWUP] prefix and routes via template API.
                _charged_prefix = "[CHARGED_FOLLOWUP] "
            else:
                logger.info(
                    "followup suppressed: wa_window_closed, charged budget exhausted "
                    "attempt=%d max_charged=%d lifecycle=%s merchant_id=%s phone=%s",
                    attempt, max_charged_followups,
                    state.lifecycle, state.merchant_id, state.phone,
                )
                return None
        else:
            _charged_prefix = ""


        # Inline cached signal so the agent sends without calling any GBP tool.
        signal_hint = (
            f" GBP SIGNAL (cite this, do NOT call any tool to fetch it): {gbp_signals}"
            if gbp_signals else
            " Mention one plausible Google profile gap (unanswered reviews, low rating, or incomplete profile)."
        )


        if state.lifecycle == "NOT_REPLIED":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: NOT_REPLIED — no reply in {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h since outreach. "
                f"Send ONE warm nudge. Do NOT call any tool — just send the message."
                f"{signal_hint}"
                f" Do NOT re-introduce yourself. Max 3 lines."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "LINK_SENT":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: LINK_SENT — connect URL sent {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h ago, "
                f"no reply since. "
                f"CONNECT URL (resend as-is): {connect_url} "
                f"Re-share this exact URL. Do NOT call any tool — just send the message."
                f"{signal_hint}"
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "GBP_CONNECTED":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: GBP_CONNECTED — merchant connected GBP {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h ago "
                f"but has not activated Vera yet. "
                f"Offer to do ONE free action right now (reply to a review or create a post) as proof of value."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "FREE_WRITE_USED":
            payment_hint = (
                f" PAYMENT LINK (resend if relevant): {payment_link}."
                if payment_link else ""
            )
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: FREE_WRITE_USED — free GBP action done, "
                f"merchant has not activated ({state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h since last activity)."
                f"{payment_hint} "
                f"Nudge toward activation. Reference the work you already did."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "PAYMENT_LINK_SENT":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: PAYMENT_LINK_SENT — payment link sent {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h ago, "
                f"merchant has not paid. "
                f"PAYMENT LINK (resend as-is): {payment_link} "
                f"Re-share this exact link. One gentle nudge line, nothing more."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        # ── Generic informed fallback (ACTIVE_CONVERSATION or any unhandled lifecycle) ──
        # Build a rich context block — current state snapshot + full state-transition
        # journey — so the agent can act intelligently in any edge-case lifecycle.
        state_journey = (state.extra or {}).get("state_journey", "")


        _state_lines = [f"lifecycle={state.lifecycle}", f"last_event={state.last_event_label}"]
        if state.soft_decline_count:
            _state_lines.append(f"soft_declines={state.soft_decline_count}")
        if not state.has_replied:
            _state_lines.append("merchant_has_not_replied=True")
        if connect_url:
            _state_lines.append(f"connect_url={connect_url}")
        if payment_link:
            _state_lines.append(f"payment_link={payment_link}")
        if gbp_signals:
            _state_lines.append(f"gbp_signal={gbp_signals}")
        _state_snapshot = " | ".join(_state_lines)


        journey_block = (
            f" JOURNEY: {state_journey}."
            if state_journey else ""
        )


        return (
            f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
            f"STATE: {_state_snapshot}."
            f"{journey_block} "
            f"Pick up with a fresh, concrete angle — do NOT repeat your last message. "
            f"Do NOT call any data-fetching tool. Use the state and journey above to inform your message."
            f"{angle_line} "
            f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
        )


# ── Self-register ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
register_resolver(NewVeraSalesAgentResolver())


 




[agents/vera/merchant_followup_state.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/agents/vera/merchant_followup_state.py)


"""
Follow-up lifecycle state resolver for VeraMerchantAgent.


Self-registers at import time — just import this module in run_followup_poller.py.


VeraMerchantAgent covers the full merchant lifecycle:
  ACQUIRE → ACTIVATE → DELIVER → GROW → RETAIN


Redis keys (inherited from VeraSalesAgent / NewVeraSalesAgent — same prefix):
  vera:sales:v2:{mid}          → association state (associated-not-paying / associated-paying)
                                 + decline_count
  vera:sales:v2:writes:{mid}   → GBP write count (free demo actions)
  vera:sales:v2:payment:{mid}  → pending payment link + status


Lifecycle states (priority order)
-----------------------------------
OPTED_OUT           hard stop signal → terminal
SUBSCRIBED          Redis state=associated-paying → terminal
PAYMENT_LINK_SENT   pending payment link (not yet paid)
FREE_WRITE_USED     free GBP action done, not activated
GBP_CONNECTED       connected GBP, no write done yet
LINK_SENT           OAuth connect URL sent, not replied
ACTIVE_CONVERSATION merchant has replied, stalled
NOT_REPLIED         no merchant reply at all


Sentiment classification (primary source: communicate_to_user.merchant_sentiment)
-----------------------------------
The VeraMerchantAgent adds merchant_sentiment to communicate_to_user tool args.
This is more reliable than regex on merchant text because:
  - The model has full conversational context when classifying
  - Avoids false positives from partial word matches in Hindi/Hinglish
Regex runs as a fallback for messages sent before this feature was deployed.
"""


import json
import logging
import re
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import List, Optional


from utility.followup_state_base import FollowupState, FollowupStateResolver, register_resolver


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ── Redis key prefixes (mirror VeraSalesAgent constants) ─────────────────────
_STATE_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:"
_WRITE_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:writes:"
_PAYMENT_PREFIX = "vera:sales:v2:payment:"


_VERA_STATE_NOT_PAYING = "associated-not-paying"
_VERA_STATE_PAYING = "associated-paying"


# ── Hard-stop patterns — true opt-out ────────────────────────────────────────
_HARD_STOP_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(stop\s+messaging|don'?t\s+(?:contact|message)\s+me|do\s+not\s+contact|"
    r"remove\s+(?:me|number)|unsubscribe|block|hataao|band\s+karo|nahi\s+chahiye\s+kuch)\b",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)


# ── Soft-decline patterns — objection, not opt-out ───────────────────────────
_SOFT_DECLINE_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(nahi\b|no\b|not\s+interested|need\s+nahi|nahi\s+chahiye|"
    r"baad\s+mein|later|maybe\s+later|abhi\s+nahi|not\s+now|no\s+thanks|no\s+thank\s+you)\b",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)


# ── URL patterns ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
_VERA_URL_RE = re.compile(r"https?://vera\.magicpin\.com[^\s<>\"']*", re.IGNORECASE)
_PAYMENT_URL_RE = re.compile(
    r"https?://[^\s<>\"']*(?:pay\.magicpin|razorpay|cashfree|checkout)[^\s<>\"']*",
    re.IGNORECASE,
)


# ── Objection angles (indexed by soft_decline_count) ─────────────────────────
_OBJECTION_ANGLES = [
    "",   # 0 declines — no extra directive
    "NEXT ANGLE: Lead with urgency — unanswered reviews are hurting their ranking right now.",
    "NEXT ANGLE: Visibility gap — profile incomplete, competitors rank above them for the same searches.",
    "NEXT ANGLE: Zero-effort — Vera runs daily on autopilot, they do nothing. Frame as set-and-forget.",
    "NEXT ANGLE: Low-risk close — ₹499/month to activate, cancel anytime, no contract. Ask if worth trying once.",
]


# ── Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────


def _hours_since(ts: Optional[datetime]) -> float:
    if not ts:
        return 0.0
    if ts.tzinfo is None:
        ts = ts.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    return max(0.0, (datetime.now(timezone.utc) - ts).total_seconds() / 3600)


def _redis_json(client, key: str) -> Optional[dict]:
    try:
        raw = client.get(key)
        if not raw:
            return None
        return json.loads(raw.decode("utf-8") if isinstance(raw, bytes) else raw)
    except Exception as exc:
        logger.debug("Redis get %s failed: %s", key, exc)
        return None


def _redis_int(client, key: str) -> int:
    try:
        raw = client.get(key)
        return int(raw) if raw else 0
    except Exception:
        return 0


def _extract_gbp_signals(state_data: Optional[dict]) -> str:
    """Pull the most salient GBP signal from cached Redis state_data."""
    if not state_data:
        return ""
    unanswered = state_data.get("unanswered_review_count") or state_data.get("pending_reviews")
    if unanswered and int(unanswered) > 0:
        return f"You have {unanswered} unanswered review(s) on Google — hurting your ranking right now."
    try:
        rating = float(state_data.get("rating") or state_data.get("google_rating") or 0)
        if 0 < rating < 4.0:
            return f"Your Google rating is {rating:.1f} — below the 4.0 threshold most customers filter by."
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        pass
    try:
        review_count = int(state_data.get("review_count") or state_data.get("total_reviews") or 0)
        if 0 < review_count < 10:
            return f"Your profile has only {review_count} Google review(s) — competitors in your area have far more."
    except (TypeError, ValueError):
        pass
    return ""


# ── Resolver ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────


class VeraMerchantAgentResolver(FollowupStateResolver):
    """Follow-up lifecycle resolver for VeraMerchantAgent."""


    agent_type = "VeraMerchantAgent"


    def resolve(
        self,
        session,
        ticket_id: int,
        context_data: dict,
        redis_client=None,
        max_soft_declines: int = 0,
    ) -> FollowupState:
        try:
            return self._resolve_inner(session, ticket_id, context_data, redis_client, max_soft_declines)
        except Exception as exc:
            logger.error("VeraMerchantAgentResolver.resolve failed ticket=%s: %s", ticket_id, exc)
            return FollowupState(
                lifecycle="UNKNOWN",
                is_terminal=False,
                last_event_label="state resolution failed",
            )


    def _resolve_inner(
        self,
        session,
        ticket_id: int,
        context_data: dict,
        redis_client,
        max_soft_declines: int = 0,
    ) -> FollowupState:
        from utility.db_models import MultiAgentChatHistory


        merchant_id = str((context_data or {}).get("merchant_id", "") or "")
        phone = str((context_data or {}).get("phone_number", "") or "")


        # ── Chat history ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        messages: List[MultiAgentChatHistory] = (
            session.query(MultiAgentChatHistory)
            .filter(MultiAgentChatHistory.ticket_id == ticket_id)
            .order_by(MultiAgentChatHistory.created_at.asc())
            .all()
        )
        merchant_msgs = [m for m in messages if m.sender == "whatsapp"]
        agent_msgs = [m for m in messages if m.sender not in ("whatsapp", "system")]
        first_msg = messages[0] if messages else None
        last_merchant_msg = merchant_msgs[-1] if merchant_msgs else None
        has_replied = bool(merchant_msgs)


        # ── Sentiment signals from communicate_to_user tool args ──────────────
        # Primary: model-classified merchant_sentiment stored in agent_metadata.
        # Fallback: regex on raw merchant text (legacy messages).
        agent_sentiments = [
            (m.agent_metadata or {}).get("merchant_sentiment")
            for m in agent_msgs
            if (m.agent_metadata or {}).get("merchant_sentiment")
        ]
        is_opted_out_from_sentiment = any(s == "hard_stop" for s in agent_sentiments)
        soft_decline_from_sentiment = sum(1 for s in agent_sentiments if s == "soft_decline")


        if is_opted_out_from_sentiment:
            is_opted_out = True
        else:
            recent_text = " ".join(m.message or "" for m in merchant_msgs[-5:])
            is_opted_out = bool(_HARD_STOP_RE.search(recent_text))


        # Soft-decline: Redis (primary) > model sentiment > regex (legacy fallback)
        redis_state_data: Optional[dict] = None
        if redis_client and merchant_id:
            redis_state_data = _redis_json(redis_client, f"{_STATE_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            soft_decline_count = int((redis_state_data or {}).get("decline_count", 0))
        elif soft_decline_from_sentiment > 0:
            soft_decline_count = soft_decline_from_sentiment
        else:
            soft_decline_count = sum(
                1 for m in merchant_msgs if _SOFT_DECLINE_RE.search(m.message or "")
            )


        # ── URL signals from agent messages ───────────────────────────────────
        connect_url: Optional[str] = None
        connect_sent_at: Optional[datetime] = None
        payment_link: Optional[str] = None
        payment_sent_at: Optional[datetime] = None


        for m in agent_msgs:
            text = m.message or ""
            if connect_url is None:
                hit = _VERA_URL_RE.search(text)
                if hit:
                    connect_url = hit.group(0)
                    connect_sent_at = m.created_at
            if payment_link is None:
                hit = _PAYMENT_URL_RE.search(text)
                if hit:
                    payment_link = hit.group(0)
                    payment_sent_at = m.created_at


        # ── Redis enrichment ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        gbp_state = ""
        write_count = 0
        redis_payment_status = None


        if redis_client and merchant_id:
            if redis_state_data is None:
                redis_state_data = _redis_json(redis_client, f"{_STATE_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            gbp_state = (redis_state_data or {}).get("state", "")
            write_count = _redis_int(redis_client, f"{_WRITE_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            redis_payment = _redis_json(redis_client, f"{_PAYMENT_PREFIX}{merchant_id}")
            if redis_payment and redis_payment.get("payment_link"):
                payment_link = redis_payment["payment_link"]
                redis_payment_status = redis_payment.get("status")


        gbp_signals = _extract_gbp_signals(redis_state_data)


        # ── WhatsApp 24h session window ───────────────────────────────────────
        hours_since_last_merchant_msg = (
            _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at) if last_merchant_msg else float("inf")
        )
        wa_window_open = has_replied and hours_since_last_merchant_msg < 24.0


        # ── Helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        def _state(lifecycle, hours, label, is_terminal=False, terminal_reason=""):
            return FollowupState(
                lifecycle=lifecycle,
                is_terminal=is_terminal,
                terminal_reason=terminal_reason,
                soft_decline_count=soft_decline_count,
                hours_since_last_event=hours,
                last_event_label=label,
                has_replied=has_replied,
                merchant_id=merchant_id,
                phone=phone,
                extra={
                    "connect_url": connect_url,
                    "payment_link": payment_link,
                    "gbp_signals": gbp_signals,
                    "wa_window_open": wa_window_open,
                    "hours_since_last_merchant_msg": hours_since_last_merchant_msg,
                },
            )


        # ── State classification (priority order) ─────────────────────────────


        if is_opted_out:
            return _state(
                "OPTED_OUT",
                _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None),
                "merchant sent hard stop signal",
                is_terminal=True,
                terminal_reason="opted out",
            )


        if max_soft_declines > 0 and soft_decline_count >= max_soft_declines:
            return _state(
                "SOFT_DECLINE_LIMIT",
                _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None),
                f"merchant declined {soft_decline_count}x — objection angles exhausted",
                is_terminal=True,
                terminal_reason=f"soft decline limit reached ({soft_decline_count}/{max_soft_declines})",
            )


        if gbp_state == _VERA_STATE_PAYING:
            return _state(
                "SUBSCRIBED",
                _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None),
                "merchant is subscribed",
                is_terminal=True,
                terminal_reason="subscribed — no follow-up needed",
            )


        is_payment_pending = bool(payment_link and redis_payment_status != "completed")
        if is_payment_pending:
            hours = _hours_since(payment_sent_at)
            return _state("PAYMENT_LINK_SENT", hours, f"payment link sent {hours:.0f}h ago")


        if gbp_state == _VERA_STATE_NOT_PAYING and write_count > 0:
            hours = _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None)
            return _state("FREE_WRITE_USED", hours, f"free GBP action done, last reply {hours:.0f}h ago")


        if gbp_state == _VERA_STATE_NOT_PAYING:
            hours = _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at if last_merchant_msg else None)
            return _state("GBP_CONNECTED", hours, f"GBP connected, last reply {hours:.0f}h ago")


        if connect_url and connect_sent_at:
            merchant_replied_after_link = any(
                (m.created_at or datetime.min.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)) > connect_sent_at
                for m in merchant_msgs
            )
            if not merchant_replied_after_link:
                hours = _hours_since(connect_sent_at)
                return _state("LINK_SENT", hours, f"connect URL sent {hours:.0f}h ago, no reply yet")


        if has_replied:
            hours = _hours_since(last_merchant_msg.created_at)
            return _state("ACTIVE_CONVERSATION", hours, f"merchant last replied {hours:.0f}h ago")


        hours = _hours_since(first_msg.created_at if first_msg else None)
        return _state("NOT_REPLIED", hours, f"outreach sent {hours:.0f}h ago, no reply yet")


    def build_trigger(
        self,
        state: FollowupState,
        attempt: int,
        max_attempts: int,
        max_charged_followups: int = 0,
    ) -> Optional[str]:
        if state.is_terminal:
            return None


        is_final = attempt >= max_attempts
        attempt_label = f"Attempt {attempt}/{max_attempts}" + (" — FINAL" if is_final else "")
        angle_idx = min(max(state.soft_decline_count, 0), len(_OBJECTION_ANGLES) - 1)
        angle = _OBJECTION_ANGLES[angle_idx]
        angle_line = f" {angle}" if angle else ""


        connect_url = (state.extra or {}).get("connect_url")
        payment_link = (state.extra or {}).get("payment_link")
        gbp_signals = (state.extra or {}).get("gbp_signals", "")
        wa_window_open: bool = (state.extra or {}).get("wa_window_open", False)
        hours_since_merchant = (state.extra or {}).get("hours_since_last_merchant_msg", -1)


        # ── WhatsApp 24h window gate ──────────────────────────────────────────
        if not wa_window_open:
            if attempt <= max_charged_followups:
                logger.info(
                    "followup charged: wa_window_closed attempt=%d/%d lifecycle=%s "
                    "merchant_id=%s phone=%s hours_since_merchant_msg=%.0f",
                    attempt, max_charged_followups,
                    state.lifecycle, state.merchant_id, state.phone, hours_since_merchant,
                )
                _charged_prefix = "[CHARGED_FOLLOWUP] "
            else:
                logger.info(
                    "followup suppressed: wa_window_closed, charged budget exhausted "
                    "attempt=%d max_charged=%d lifecycle=%s merchant_id=%s phone=%s",
                    attempt, max_charged_followups,
                    state.lifecycle, state.merchant_id, state.phone,
                )
                return None
        else:
            _charged_prefix = ""


        signal_hint = (
            f" GBP SIGNAL (cite this, do NOT call any tool): {gbp_signals}"
            if gbp_signals else
            " Mention one plausible Google profile gap (unanswered reviews, low rating, or incomplete profile)."
        )


        if state.lifecycle == "NOT_REPLIED":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: NOT_REPLIED — no reply in {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h since outreach. "
                f"Send ONE warm nudge. Do NOT call any tool — just send the message."
                f"{signal_hint}"
                f" Do NOT re-introduce yourself. Max 3 lines."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "LINK_SENT":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: LINK_SENT — connect URL sent {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h ago, "
                f"no reply since. "
                f"CONNECT URL (resend as-is): {connect_url} "
                f"Re-share this exact URL. Do NOT call any tool — just send the message."
                f"{signal_hint}"
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "GBP_CONNECTED":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: GBP_CONNECTED — merchant connected GBP {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h ago "
                f"but has not activated Vera yet. "
                f"Offer to do ONE free action right now (reply to a review or create a post) as proof of value."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "FREE_WRITE_USED":
            payment_hint = (
                f" PAYMENT LINK (resend if relevant): {payment_link}."
                if payment_link else ""
            )
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: FREE_WRITE_USED — free GBP action done, "
                f"merchant has not activated ({state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h since last activity)."
                f"{payment_hint} "
                f"Nudge toward activation. Reference the work you already did."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        if state.lifecycle == "PAYMENT_LINK_SENT":
            return (
                f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
                f"LIFECYCLE: PAYMENT_LINK_SENT — payment link sent {state.hours_since_last_event:.0f}h ago, "
                f"merchant has not paid. "
                f"PAYMENT LINK (resend as-is): {payment_link} "
                f"Re-share this exact link. One gentle nudge, nothing more."
                f"{angle_line} "
                f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
            )


        # ── Generic fallback (ACTIVE_CONVERSATION or any unhandled lifecycle) ─
        _state_lines = [f"lifecycle={state.lifecycle}", f"last_event={state.last_event_label}"]
        if state.soft_decline_count:
            _state_lines.append(f"soft_declines={state.soft_decline_count}")
        if not state.has_replied:
            _state_lines.append("merchant_has_not_replied=True")
        if connect_url:
            _state_lines.append(f"connect_url={connect_url}")
        if payment_link:
            _state_lines.append(f"payment_link={payment_link}")
        if gbp_signals:
            _state_lines.append(f"gbp_signal={gbp_signals}")
        _state_snapshot = " | ".join(_state_lines)


        return (
            f"{_charged_prefix}[PROACTIVE_FOLLOWUP] {attempt_label}. "
            f"STATE: {_state_snapshot}. "
            f"Pick up with a fresh, concrete angle — do NOT repeat your last message. "
            f"Do NOT call any data-fetching tool."
            f"{angle_line} "
            f"Max 2 lines. Send exactly ONE message, then stop."
        )


# ── Self-register ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
register_resolver(VeraMerchantAgentResolver())


# NOTE: GatewayVeraAgent does NOT have a resolver yet — it uses the legacy
# prompt-based followup path. Add GatewayVeraAgentResolver here when ready.

# Default provider for agents not in the config - DeepSeek
DEFAULT_PROVIDER = LLMProvider.DEEPSEEK


def get_agent_provider(agent_name: str, agent_class=None) -> LLMProvider:
    """
    Get the configured provider for an agent.


    Supports inheritance: if agent_name is not in config but inherits from
    a configured parent (e.g., EmployeeAgent), uses parent's provider.


    Args:
        agent_name: The agent_type to look up
        agent_class: Optional agent class for inheritance checking


    Returns:
        LLMProvider for this agent
    """
    logger.info(f"[LLM CONFIG] Getting provider for agent_name='{agent_name}', agent_class={agent_class.__name__ if agent_class else None}")
    logger.info(f"[LLM CONFIG] AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG keys: {list(AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG.keys())}")
    
    # Direct match in config
    if agent_name in AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG:
        provider = AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG[agent_name]
        logger.info(f"[LLM CONFIG] Agent '{agent_name}' found in AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG -> provider={provider.value}")
        return provider
    
    logger.info(f"[LLM CONFIG] Agent '{agent_name}' NOT found in AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG, checking inheritance...")


    # Check inheritance-based defaults.
    # All EmployeeAgent subclasses use DeepSeek.
    # Keep AnalystAgent check explicit for clarity (it inherits from EmployeeAgent).
    if agent_class:
        try:
            from employee_agents.analysts.base import AnalystAgent
            if issubclass(agent_class, AnalystAgent):
                logger.info(f"[LLM CONFIG] {agent_name} inherits from AnalystAgent, using DeepSeek")
                return LLMProvider.DEEPSEEK


            from employee_agents.base.employee_agent import EmployeeAgent
            if issubclass(agent_class, EmployeeAgent):
                logger.info(f"[LLM CONFIG] {agent_name} inherits from EmployeeAgent, using DeepSeek")
                return LLMProvider.DEEPSEEK
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"[LLM CONFIG] Could not check inheritance for {agent_name}: {e}")


    # Fall back to default
    logger.info(f"[LLM CONFIG] Agent '{agent_name}' using DEFAULT_PROVIDER={DEFAULT_PROVIDER.value}")
    return DEFAULT_PROVIDER



def list_agent_providers() -> Dict[str, str]:
    """List all agents and their configured providers"""
    from .base import LLMProvider


    # Known agents in the system
    all_agents = [
        "CustomerAgent",
        "MerchantAgent",
        "RiderAgent",
        "VoucherAgent",
        "MagicOrderAgent",
        "MagicPayAgent",
        "MagicProAgent",
        "CMSAgent",
        "MerchantOpsSupportAgent",
        "EmployeeAgent",
        "MerchantMasterV2",
    ]


    result = {}
    for agent in all_agents:
        provider = AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG.get(agent, DEFAULT_PROVIDER)
        result[agent] = provider.value


    return result








- [services/llm/factory.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/services/llm/factory.py)


"""
LLM Provider Factory.


This module provides factory functions to get the appropriate LLM client
based on agent configuration.
"""


import os
import logging
from typing import Optional
from .base import BaseLLMClient, LLMProvider
from .config import AGENT_PROVIDER_CONFIG, DEFAULT_PROVIDER, get_agent_provider


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


def get_llm_provider(
    agent_name: str,
    provider_type: Optional[LLMProvider] = None,
    agent_class=None
) -> BaseLLMClient:
    """
    Get the configured LLM provider for an agent.


    Args:
        agent_name: Name of the agent (e.g., "CustomerAgent")
        provider_type: Override to force a specific provider
        agent_class: Optional agent class for inheritance-based lookup


    Returns:
        Configured LLM client instance


    Example:
        # Get default provider for an agent
        provider = get_llm_provider("CustomerAgent")


        # Force Gemini for testing
        provider = get_llm_provider("CustomerAgent", LLMProvider.GEMINI)
    """
    from utility.constants import (
        OPENAI_API_KEY, GPT_41_API_URL,
        EMPLOYEE_AGENT_API_KEY, EMPLOYEE_AGENT_API_URL
    )


    # Determine which provider to use
    if provider_type:
        selected_provider = provider_type
    else:
        selected_provider = get_agent_provider(agent_name, agent_class)


    logger.debug(f"Getting LLM provider for {agent_name}: {selected_provider.value}")


    if selected_provider == LLMProvider.AZURE_OPENAI:
        from .azure_openai import AzureOpenAIClient


        # Use employee-specific credentials for EmployeeAgent and V2 agents
        if agent_name == "EmployeeAgent" or agent_name.endswith("V2"):
            return AzureOpenAIClient(
                api_key=EMPLOYEE_AGENT_API_KEY,
                api_version="2025-04-01-preview",
                azure_endpoint=EMPLOYEE_AGENT_API_URL
            )
        else:
            return AzureOpenAIClient(
                api_key=OPENAI_API_KEY,
                api_version="2025-04-01-preview",
                azure_endpoint=GPT_41_API_URL
            )


    elif selected_provider == LLMProvider.GEMINI:
        from .gemini import GeminiClient


        # Check which Gemini API to use
        use_vertexai = os.environ.get("GEMINI_USE_VERTEXAI", "false").lower() in ("true", "1", "yes")


        if use_vertexai:
            # Vertex AI mode
            # If GEMINI_API_KEY is set and no VERTEX_AI_PROJECT → express mode (API key routes via Vertex endpoints)
            # If VERTEX_AI_PROJECT is set → full project mode with service account / ADC
            project_id = os.environ.get("VERTEX_AI_PROJECT")
            api_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY")  # Used for express mode


            if not project_id and not api_key:
                raise ValueError(
                    "Vertex AI mode requires either VERTEX_AI_PROJECT (service account/ADC) "
                    "or GEMINI_API_KEY (express mode). "
                    "Set GEMINI_USE_VERTEXAI=false to use Developer API instead."
                )


            location = os.environ.get("VERTEX_AI_LOCATION", "global")
            credentials_path = os.environ.get("GEMINI_CREDENTIALS_PATH")
            use_dedicated = os.environ.get("VERTEX_AI_USE_DEDICATED", "false").lower() in ("true", "1", "yes")


            if project_id:
                logger.info(f"Using Vertex AI Gemini API: project={project_id}, location={location}, dedicated={use_dedicated}")
            else:
                logger.info(f"Using Vertex AI Express Mode (API key, no project): location={location}, dedicated={use_dedicated}")


            return GeminiClient(
                api_key=api_key,
                project_id=project_id,
                location=location,
                credentials_path=credentials_path,
                use_dedicated=use_dedicated,
                use_vertexai=True
            )
        else:
            # Developer API mode: requires api_key, location is ignored
            gemini_api_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
            if not gemini_api_key:
                raise ValueError(
                    "GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable not set. "
                    "Please set it to your Google AI API key."
                )
            logger.info("Using Google AI Developer API (location not applicable)")
            return GeminiClient(
                api_key=gemini_api_key,
                use_vertexai=False
            )


    elif selected_provider == LLMProvider.DEEPSEEK:
        from .internal_deepseek import InternalDeepSeekClient


        logger.info("Using Internal DeepSeek API endpoint")
        return InternalDeepSeekClient()


    elif selected_provider == LLMProvider.AGENT_GATEWAY:
        from .agent_gateway import AgentGatewayClient


        logger.info(f"Using Agent Gateway for {agent_name}")
        return AgentGatewayClient()


    else:
        raise ValueError(f"Unknown provider type: {selected_provider}")


def get_azure_openai_client(
    api_key: Optional[str] = None,
    api_version: str = "2025-04-01-preview",
    azure_endpoint: Optional[str] = None
) -> BaseLLMClient:
    """
    Get an Azure OpenAI client with custom configuration.


    Args:
        api_key: API key (defaults to OPENAI_API_KEY env var)
        api_version: API version
        azure_endpoint: Azure endpoint URL (defaults to GPT_41_API_URL)


    Returns:
        AzureOpenAIClient instance
    """
    from utility.constants import OPENAI_API_KEY, GPT_41_API_URL
    from .azure_openai import AzureOpenAIClient


    return AzureOpenAIClient(
        api_key=api_key or OPENAI_API_KEY,
        api_version=api_version,
        azure_endpoint=azure_endpoint or GPT_41_API_URL
    )


def get_gemini_client(
    api_key: Optional[str] = None,
    project_id: Optional[str] = None,
    location: str = "global",
    use_vertexai: bool = False,
    credentials_path: Optional[str] = None,
    use_dedicated: bool = False
) -> BaseLLMClient:
    """
    Get a Gemini client with custom configuration.


    Args:
        api_key: Google API key (required for Developer API, optional for Vertex AI)
        project_id: GCP project ID (required for Vertex AI)
        location: GCP region (only applies to Vertex AI)
        use_vertexai: If True, uses Vertex AI API. If False, uses Developer API.
        credentials_path: Path to service account JSON (for Vertex AI)
        use_dedicated: If True, adds dedicated subscription header


    Returns:
        GeminiClient instance
    """
    from .gemini import GeminiClient


    if use_vertexai:
        if not project_id:
            project_id = os.environ.get("VERTEX_AI_PROJECT")
            if not project_id:
                raise ValueError("project_id required for Vertex AI")
        return GeminiClient(
            api_key=api_key or os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY"),
            project_id=project_id,
            location=location,
            credentials_path=credentials_path or os.environ.get("GEMINI_CREDENTIALS_PATH"),
            use_dedicated=use_dedicated,
            use_vertexai=True
        )
    else:
        api_key = api_key or os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        if not api_key:
            raise ValueError("GEMINI_API_KEY not provided")
        return GeminiClient(
            api_key=api_key,
            use_vertexai=False
        )












- [services/llm/azure_openai.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/services/llm/azure_openai.py)
- """
Azure OpenAI LLM client implementation.
"""


import json
import copy
import logging
import time
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from openai import RateLimitError
from .base import BaseLLMClient, LLMResponse


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class AzureOpenAIClient(BaseLLMClient):
    """Azure OpenAI client wrapper"""


    def __init__(self, api_key: str, api_version: str, azure_endpoint: str):
        from openai import AzureOpenAI
        self.client = AzureOpenAI(
            api_key=api_key,
            api_version=api_version,
            azure_endpoint=azure_endpoint
        )
        self.api_version = api_version
        self.azure_endpoint = azure_endpoint


    def _ensure_resp_prefix(self, response_id: Optional[str]) -> Optional[str]:
        """
        Ensure the response_id has the 'resp_' prefix required by the Azure OpenAI API.
        
        The API expects response IDs to begin with 'resp_', but IDs are stored as UUIDs
        in the database. This method adds the prefix if missing.
        
        Args:
            response_id: The response ID from the database (UUID format)
            
        Returns:
            Response ID with 'resp_' prefix, or None if input is None
        """
        if not response_id:
            return None
        
        # If already has prefix, return as-is
        if response_id.startswith('resp_'):
            logger.debug(f"[RESPONSE_ID] Already has 'resp_' prefix: {response_id}")
            return response_id
        
        # Add prefix to UUID
        prefixed_id = f"resp_{response_id}"
        logger.info(f"[RESPONSE_ID] Added 'resp_' prefix: {response_id} -> {prefixed_id}")
        return prefixed_id


    def _make_schema_strict(
        self, schema: Dict[str, Any], nullable: bool = False
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Recursively transform a JSON schema to be Azure strict-mode compatible.


        Rules applied:
        - Every object gets ``additionalProperties: false``
        - Every property is added to ``required``; properties that were optional
          become nullable (their type gains "null")
        - Array ``items`` are processed recursively
        - Nested objects are wrapped in ``anyOf`` when nullable so they remain
          valid alongside ``{"type": "null"}``
        """
        schema = dict(schema)


        # OpenAI rejects schemas where $ref has sibling keywords
        # (e.g. {"$ref": "...", "description": "..."}). Keep only $ref.
        if "$ref" in schema:
            ref_schema: Dict[str, Any] = {"$ref": schema["$ref"]}
            if nullable:
                return {"anyOf": [ref_schema, {"type": "null"}]}
            return ref_schema


        # Strictify reusable definitions that are often referenced by $ref.
        for defs_key in ("$defs", "definitions"):
            if isinstance(schema.get(defs_key), dict):
                schema[defs_key] = {
                    name: self._make_schema_strict(def_schema)
                    if isinstance(def_schema, dict)
                    else def_schema
                    for name, def_schema in schema[defs_key].items()
                }


        # Recurse through schema combinators so nested object branches become strict.
        for combiner in ("anyOf", "oneOf", "allOf"):
            if isinstance(schema.get(combiner), list):
                schema[combiner] = [
                    self._make_schema_strict(branch)
                    if isinstance(branch, dict)
                    else branch
                    for branch in schema[combiner]
                ]


        is_object = schema.get("type") == "object" or "properties" in schema


        if is_object:
            schema["additionalProperties"] = False
            properties = schema.get("properties", {})
            existing_required: set = set(schema.get("required", []))


            new_props: Dict[str, Any] = {}
            for prop_name, prop_schema in properties.items():
                is_req = prop_name in existing_required
                new_props[prop_name] = self._make_schema_strict(
                    prop_schema, nullable=not is_req
                )


            schema["properties"] = new_props
            # All properties are now required (optional ones are nullable)
            schema["required"] = list(properties.keys())


            if nullable:
                # Wrap in anyOf so object + null is unambiguous
                return {"anyOf": [schema, {"type": "null"}]}
            return schema


        # Array: recurse into items
        if schema.get("type") == "array" and "items" in schema:
            schema["items"] = self._make_schema_strict(schema["items"])


        # Make scalar/array nullable
        if nullable:
            current_type = schema.get("type")
            if current_type and current_type != "null":
                if isinstance(current_type, list):
                    if "null" not in current_type:
                        schema["type"] = current_type + ["null"]
                else:
                    schema["type"] = [current_type, "null"]


        return schema


    def _make_tools_strict(
        self, tools: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        Inject ``strict: true`` into every function tool and transform its
        parameter schema to comply with Azure strict-mode requirements.


        Handles two tool formats:
        - Azure OpenAI format: {"type": "function", "function": {"name": ..., "parameters": ...}}
        - Base agent format: {"type": "function", "name": ..., "parameters": ...}


        Non-function tools are passed through unchanged.
        """
        strict_tools = []
        for tool in tools:
            if tool.get("type") != "function":
                strict_tools.append(tool)
                continue


            tool = dict(tool)  # shallow copy — don't mutate caller's list


            # Handle Azure OpenAI format (nested "function" key)
            if "function" in tool:
                tool["function"] = dict(tool["function"])  # shallow copy
                tool["function"]["strict"] = True
                if "parameters" in tool["function"]:
                    tool["function"]["parameters"] = self._make_schema_strict(
                        tool["function"]["parameters"]
                    )
            else:
                # Handle base agent format (flat structure)
                tool["strict"] = True
                if "parameters" in tool:
                    tool["parameters"] = self._make_schema_strict(tool["parameters"])


            strict_tools.append(tool)
        return strict_tools


    def create_response(
        self,
        model: str,
        messages: List[Dict[str, Any]],
        tools: Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
        previous_response_id: Optional[str] = None,
        agent_type: Optional[str] = None,
        session_id: Optional[str] = None,
        **kwargs
    ) -> LLMResponse:
        """
        Create response using Azure OpenAI Responses API.
        
        Azure OpenAI is stateful - it uses previous_response_id to maintain conversation state.
        When previous_response_id is provided, only the new input (last message) is sent.
        When previous_response_id is None, the full messages history is sent.
        
        Handles metrics tracking internally when agent_type and session_id are provided.
        """


        # Build request parameters
        # Azure OpenAI stateful logic: if we have a previous_response_id,
        # extract only the new input from the end of messages array.
        # New input could be:
        # - User message (role="user" or role="developer")  
        # - Tool results (type="function_call_output", no "role" key)
        if previous_response_id:
            # Stateful continuation: send only new input
            if messages:
                # Find the new input by iterating from the end
                # Collect messages until we hit something from chat_history
                # (LLM response objects have "output" key with list value and no "role" key)
                new_input = []
                for msg in reversed(messages):
                    # Skip system messages (these are at the start, not new input)
                    if msg.get("role") == "system":
                        break
                    
                    # Check if this is an LLM response object from chat_history
                    # These have "output" as a list and no "role" key
                    if "output" in msg and isinstance(msg.get("output"), list) and "role" not in msg:
                        # Hit a previous response in history, stop collecting
                        break
                    
                    # This is new input (user message or tool result)
                    new_input.insert(0, msg)
                    
                    # If we hit a user/developer message, we've collected the new user input
                    # (tool results don't have role, so this won't trigger for them)
                    if msg.get("role") in ["user", "developer"]:
                        break
                
                input_data = new_input if new_input else messages[-1:]
            else:
                input_data = messages
        else:
            # Initial call: send full message history
            input_data = messages


        params = {
            "model": model,
            "input": input_data,
        }


        if tools:
            params["tools"] = self._make_tools_strict(tools)


        # Ensure previous_response_id has 'resp_' prefix before passing to API
        if previous_response_id:
            prefixed_response_id = self._ensure_resp_prefix(previous_response_id)
            if prefixed_response_id:
                params["previous_response_id"] = prefixed_response_id


        # Add reasoning and text verbosity settings if provided and non-empty
        if kwargs.get("reasoning"):
            params["reasoning"] = kwargs["reasoning"]
        if kwargs.get("text"):
            params["text"] = kwargs["text"]


        # Retry logic for rate limit errors (HL-1664)
        max_retries = 5
        last_error = None
        
        for attempt in range(max_retries + 1):  # +1 to include initial attempt
            try:
                response = self.client.responses.create(**params)
                response_dict = response.model_dump()
                
                # Log model response details
                logger.info(f"[MODEL RESPONSE] ========== Received response for session {session_id or 'unknown'} ==========")
                logger.info(f"[MODEL RESPONSE] Provider: {self.get_provider_name()}, Model: {model}")
                if 'tools' in response_dict and response_dict['tools']:
                    tool_names = [tool.get('name', 'unknown') for tool in response_dict['tools']]
                    logger.info(f"[MODEL RESPONSE] Available tools: {', '.join(tool_names)}")
                response_json_without_tools = copy.deepcopy(response_dict)
                response_json_without_tools.pop('tools', None)
                logger.info(f"[MODEL RESPONSE] Full response JSON: {json.dumps(response_json_without_tools, indent=2)}")
                
                # Extract and log the actual message text
                if "output" in response_dict and response_dict["output"]:
                    for output in response_dict["output"]:
                        if output.get("type") == "message":
                            content = output.get("content", [])
                            for c in content:
                                if c.get("type") == "output_text":
                                    actual_message = c.get("text", "")
                                    logger.info(f"[MODEL RESPONSE] *** AGENT MESSAGE: {actual_message}")
                        elif output.get("type") == "function_call":
                            call_name = output.get("name", "unknown")
                            logger.info(f"[MODEL RESPONSE] *** FUNCTION CALL: {call_name}")
                
                # Track metrics if agent_type provided
                if agent_type:
                    from utility.metrics import increment_openai_response, increment_openai_token_usage
                    increment_openai_response(agent_type, model, 200)
                    increment_openai_token_usage(agent_type, model, response_dict, session_id or -1)


                # Track token usage in Redis if session_id provided, but never let Redis/DB sync block delivery.
                if session_id and 'usage' in response_dict:
                    try:
                        from utility.redis_config import incr_tokens
                        from utility.db_models import sync_token_usage_from_redis
                        incr_tokens(session_id, response_dict['usage'])
                        sync_token_usage_from_redis(session_id)
                    except Exception as sync_err:
                        logger.warning(
                            "[TOKEN_SYNC] Non-blocking token sync failed for session %s: %s",
                            session_id,
                            sync_err,
                        )
                
                # Save external call to database for usage tracking
                try:
                    from utility.db_models import save_external_call
                    save_external_call(
                        response_id=response.id,
                        response=response_dict,
                        usage=response_dict.get("usage", {}),
                        request_data=params,
                        usecase=agent_type or "azure_openai"
                    )
                except Exception as db_err:
                    logger.warning(f"[AZURE_OPENAI] Failed to save external call: {db_err}")
                
                return LLMResponse(
                    id=response.id,
                    model=model,
                    output=response_dict.get("output", []),
                    usage=response_dict.get("usage", {}),
                    raw_response=response_dict
                )
            except RateLimitError as e:
                last_error = e
                if attempt < max_retries:
                    delay = 2 ** attempt  # 1s, 2s, 4s, 8s, 16s
                    logger.warning(
                        f"[AZURE_OPENAI_RETRY] Attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries + 1}, retrying in {delay}s (RateLimitError: {e})"
                    )
                    time.sleep(delay)
                else:
                    logger.error(
                        f"[AZURE_OPENAI_RETRY] Max retries ({max_retries}) exceeded, giving up (RateLimitError: {e})"
                    )
            except Exception as e:
                # Non-rate-limit errors: raise immediately
                raise
        
        # If we exhausted all retries, raise the last error
        # Track error metrics before raising
        if agent_type and last_error:
            from utility.metrics import increment_openai_response
            increment_openai_response(agent_type, model, 500)
        raise last_error


    def get_provider_name(self) -> str:
        return "azure_openai"
    
    def is_recoverable_error(self, error: Exception) -> bool:
        """
        Check if error is a recoverable Azure OpenAI error.


        Detects errors like:
        - "No tool output found for function call"
        - "Previous response with id ... not found"
        - "DeploymentNotFound" (404) - deployment unavailable, clear thread and retry with current provider
        - Rate limit errors (HTTP 429, error code 429, or "too many requests")


        Returns:
            True if error should be retried (either with conversation reset or retry logic)
        """
        error_message = str(getattr(error, "message", error) or "").lower()
        print(error_message)
        is_response_state_error = (
            "no tool output found for function call" in error_message
            or "previous response with id" in error_message
        )
        is_deployment_not_found = (
            "deploymentnotfound" in error_message
            or "deployment for this resource does not exist" in error_message
            or (hasattr(error, "status_code") and error.status_code == 404)
        )
        is_rate_limit_error = (
            isinstance(error, RateLimitError)
            or "429" in str(getattr(error, "status_code", ""))
            or "rate limit" in error_message
            or "too many requests" in error_message
        )
        return is_response_state_error or is_deployment_not_found or is_rate_limit_error
    
    def handle_recoverable_error(self, session_id: str, unset_response_id_callback):
        """
        Handle Azure OpenAI recoverable error by resetting conversation state.
        
        Args:
            session_id: The session identifier
            unset_response_id_callback: Callback to reset response_id in Redis
        """
        unset_response_id_callback(session_id)


 


[services/llm/internal_deepseek.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/services/llm/internal_deepseek.py)


"""
Internal DeepSeek Client - Calls DeepSeek core logic directly.


This client calls the shared deepseek_core logic directly instead of making 
HTTP calls to an endpoint. Provides stateful conversation management and consistent API integration.
"""


import json
import logging
import os
import time
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional


from .base import BaseLLMClient, LLMResponse
from .deepseek_core import call_deepseek_chat
from utility.constants import INTERNAL_API_BASE_URL
from utility.agent_types import ToolNames
from utility.redis_config import get_redis_client


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


SALESMONET_DEEPSEEK_WHITELIST_KEY = "salesmonet:deepseek_whitelist"
SALESMONET_DEEPSEEK_ROUTE_URL_KEY = "salesmonet:deepseek_route_url"
SYNTHETIC_TOOL_RESPONSE_AGENT_TYPES = {"testsalesagentv2"}


def normalize_tools(tools: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    Normalize tools from base agent format to OpenAI format with proper schema validation.


    Handles:
    1. Converting base agent format to OpenAI format (adds 'function' wrapper)
    2. Ensures all tools have proper parameters schema with "type": "object"
    3. Adds empty parameters if missing
    4. Validates the schema for DeepSeek compatibility


    Args:
        tools: List of tool definitions in various formats


    Returns:
        List of normalized tools in OpenAI format with valid schemas
    """
    if not tools:
        return tools


    normalized_tools = []


    for i, tool in enumerate(tools):
        if not isinstance(tool, dict) or tool.get('type') != 'function':
            # Non-function tool, pass through as-is
            normalized_tools.append(tool)
            continue


        # Check if already in OpenAI format (has 'function' key)
        if 'function' in tool:
            # Already in OpenAI format, just validate parameters
            function_def = tool['function']
        else:
            # Convert from base agent format to OpenAI format
            function_def = {
                "name": tool.get('name'),
                "description": tool.get('description', ''),
                "parameters": tool.get('parameters')
            }


        # Ensure parameters has proper schema
        if not function_def.get('parameters'):
            # Missing parameters - add empty object schema
            function_def['parameters'] = {
                "type": "object",
                "properties": {}
            }
            logger.debug(f"[NORMALIZE TOOLS] Added empty parameters to tool: {function_def.get('name')}")
        elif not isinstance(function_def['parameters'], dict):
            # Invalid parameters - replace with empty object schema
            function_def['parameters'] = {
                "type": "object",
                "properties": {}
            }
            logger.warning(f"[NORMALIZE TOOLS] Fixed invalid parameters for tool: {function_def.get('name')}")
        elif function_def['parameters'].get('type') != 'object':
            # Parameters exists but wrong type - ensure it's object type
            if 'properties' not in function_def['parameters']:
                function_def['parameters']['properties'] = {}
            function_def['parameters']['type'] = 'object'
            logger.debug(f"[NORMALIZE TOOLS] Fixed parameters type for tool: {function_def.get('name')}")


        # Create normalized tool in OpenAI format
        normalized_tool = {
            "type": "function",
            "function": function_def
        }


        normalized_tools.append(normalized_tool)


    logger.info(f"[NORMALIZE TOOLS] Normalized {len(tools)} tools - all have valid schemas")
    return normalized_tools


class InternalDeepSeekClient(BaseLLMClient):
    """
    Internal DeepSeek client that uses our /deepseek API endpoint.


    This provides:
    - Stateful conversation management via previous_response_id
    - Consistent API format with other endpoints
    - Database conversation history storage
    - Metrics and error handling
    """
