    def __init__(self, api_base_url: Optional[str] = None):
        """
        Initialize the internal DeepSeek client.


        Args:
            api_base_url: Base URL for our internal API (defaults to INTERNAL_API_BASE_URL constant)
        """
        self.api_base_url = (api_base_url or INTERNAL_API_BASE_URL).rstrip('/')
        self.endpoint_url = f"{self.api_base_url}/botops/api/deepseek"


    def _is_salesmonet_routed_phone(self, phone: str) -> bool:
        """Check whether the phone is in the SalesMonet DeepSeek whitelist."""
        try:
            return bool(get_redis_client().sismember(SALESMONET_DEEPSEEK_WHITELIST_KEY, phone))
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Redis whitelist check failed for phone {phone}: {e}")
            return False


    def _resolve_endpoint_url(self, **kwargs) -> str:
        """Resolve endpoint URL per request without mutating client state.


        For whitelisted phones, checks Redis for a route override URL
        (key: salesmonet:deepseek_route_url). If set, requests go to that host —
        useful for local dev via ngrok. If absent/empty, falls through to the
        default INTERNAL_API_BASE_URL so production is unaffected.
        """
        request_api_base_url = (kwargs.get("api_base_url") or self.api_base_url or INTERNAL_API_BASE_URL).rstrip("/")
        phone = kwargs.get("phone_number")


        if phone and self._is_salesmonet_routed_phone(phone):
            try:
                routed_url = get_redis_client().get(SALESMONET_DEEPSEEK_ROUTE_URL_KEY)
                if routed_url:
                    request_api_base_url = routed_url.rstrip("/")
                    logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Redis route override for {phone}: {request_api_base_url}")
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Redis route URL lookup failed: {e}")


        return f"{request_api_base_url}/botops/api/deepseek"


    def _validate_tool_sequence(self, messages: List[Dict[str, Any]], is_stateful_continuation: bool = False) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        Ensure tool messages have preceding assistant messages with tool_calls.
        DeepSeek API requires tool messages to follow assistant messages that contain tool_calls.


        Simple approach: For each tool message, check if the immediate previous assistant has the matching tool_call_id.
        """
        if not messages:
            return messages


        valid_messages = []


        # In stateful continuation, be more permissive with tool messages at the start
        # They might be valid responses from previous conversation turns
        allow_orphaned_tools_at_start = is_stateful_continuation


        for i, msg in enumerate(messages):
            msg_role = msg.get("role")


            if msg_role == "tool":
                tool_call_id = msg.get("tool_call_id", "")


                # In stateful mode, be more lenient - allow tool messages that might be from previous turns
                if allow_orphaned_tools_at_start:
                    valid_messages.append(msg)
                    logger.debug(f"[TOOL SEQUENCE] Allowed tool message in stateful mode: {tool_call_id}")
                    continue


                # Look backwards for the most recent assistant message
                found_matching_tool_call = False
                for j in range(i - 1, -1, -1):
                    prev_msg = messages[j]
                    prev_role = prev_msg.get("role")


                    if prev_role == "assistant":
                        # Check if this assistant has the matching tool_call
                        tool_calls = prev_msg.get("tool_calls", [])
                        for tc in tool_calls:
                            if tc.get("id") == tool_call_id:
                                found_matching_tool_call = True
                                break
                        break  # Stop at first assistant (don't look further back)
                    elif prev_role in ["user", "system"]:
                        break  # Stop at user/system boundary


                if found_matching_tool_call:
                    valid_messages.append(msg)
                    logger.debug(f"[TOOL SEQUENCE] Kept valid tool message: {tool_call_id}")
                else:
                    logger.warning(f"[TOOL SEQUENCE] Removing orphaned tool message: {tool_call_id}")


            else:
                # Non-tool message - always keep
                valid_messages.append(msg)


                # After seeing any non-tool message, we're no longer at the start
                if msg_role in ["user", "system", "assistant"]:
                    allow_orphaned_tools_at_start = False


        if len(valid_messages) < len(messages):
            logger.warning(f"[TOOL SEQUENCE] Filtered {len(messages) - len(valid_messages)} orphaned tool messages")


        # DeepSeek-specific fix: Remove communicate_to_user tool calls that don't have corresponding tool messages
        # since these are handled asynchronously and the API doesn't expect tool responses for them
        for i, msg in enumerate(valid_messages):
            if msg.get("role") == "assistant" and msg.get("tool_calls"):
                updated_tool_calls = []
                for tool_call in msg.get("tool_calls", []):
                    tool_call_id = tool_call.get("id")
                    tool_name = tool_call.get("function", {}).get("name", "")


                    # Check if there's a corresponding tool message for this tool call
                    has_tool_response = False
                    for j in range(i + 1, len(valid_messages)):
                        if valid_messages[j].get("role") == "tool" and valid_messages[j].get("tool_call_id") == tool_call_id:
                            has_tool_response = True
                            break


                    # For communicate_to_user, KEEP it even without tool response (it's async)
                    # Only remove other tool calls that genuinely need responses
                    if tool_name == ToolNames.COMMUNICATE_TO_USER:
                        updated_tool_calls.append(tool_call)  # Always keep communicate_to_user
                        logger.debug(f"[DEEPSEEK FIX] Keeping communicate_to_user tool call (async): {tool_call_id}")
                    elif has_tool_response:
                        updated_tool_calls.append(tool_call)
                    else:
                        logger.info(f"[DEEPSEEK FIX] Removing {tool_name} tool call without response: {tool_call_id}")


                # Update the message with filtered tool calls
                if len(updated_tool_calls) != len(msg.get("tool_calls", [])):
                    valid_messages[i] = dict(msg)
                    if updated_tool_calls:
                        valid_messages[i]["tool_calls"] = updated_tool_calls
                    else:
                        # Remove tool_calls key if no tool calls remain
                        valid_messages[i].pop("tool_calls", None)


        # Ensure we have at least one message
        if not valid_messages:
            logger.warning("[TOOL SEQUENCE] No valid messages after filtering - adding fallback")
            valid_messages = [{"role": "user", "content": "Please respond to the user's previous message"}]


        return valid_messages


    def _prepare_messages(self, messages: List[Dict[str, Any]], previous_response_id: Optional[str] = None, agent_type: Optional[str] = None) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        Format messages properly for the OpenAI-compatible DeepSeek API.
        Extracts new input if continuing stateful chat, and formats tool calls into expected format.


        Args:
            include_system_prompt: When True, prepend system messages even in stateful mode.
                Useful for agents with complex specialist prompts that the proxy may not retain.
        """
        # FIRST: Clean up empty LLM response object messages from input
        # These are extracted assistant messages with no tool_calls and no content (audio, refusal, etc.)
        cleaned_messages = []
        system_msgs = []
        for msg in messages:
            # Skip empty LLM response object assistant messages
            if (msg.get("role") == "assistant" and 
                not msg.get("tool_calls") and 
                not msg.get("content") and
                ("audio" in msg or "refusal" in msg or "annotations" in msg or "function_call" in msg)):
                logger.debug(f"[PREPARE MESSAGES] Skipping empty LLM response object: {list(msg.keys())}")
                continue
            cleaned_messages.append(msg)
        
        if len(cleaned_messages) < len(messages):
            logger.info(f"[PREPARE MESSAGES] Removed {len(messages) - len(cleaned_messages)} empty LLM response messages")
        
        # Use cleaned messages for the rest of processing
        messages = cleaned_messages
        
        # If previous_response_id is provided, the API already loads history.
        # We just need to extract the current interaction's messages from the end.
        if previous_response_id:
            # Collect system/developer messages upfront so they're always included in follow-up calls.
            # Without this, DeepSeek loses all system context after the first message.
            system_msgs = []
            for msg in messages:
                role = msg.get("role")
                if role in ("system", "developer"):
                    formatted = dict(msg)
                    if formatted.get("role") == "developer":
                        formatted["role"] = "system"
                    system_msgs.append(formatted)


            new_input = []
            # Track if we've seen a user message (boundary of current turn)
            seen_user_message = False
            # Track tool_call_ids we're expecting responses for
            expected_tool_call_ids = set()


            for msg in reversed(messages):
                if msg.get("role") == "system":
                    break


                # Check for LLM response object and extract assistant message
                if "output" in msg and isinstance(msg.get("output"), list) and "role" not in msg:
                    # This is an LLM response object, extract the assistant message with tool_calls
                    tool_calls_found = []
                    for output_item in msg.get("output", []):
                        if output_item.get("type") == "function_call":
                            call_id = output_item.get("call_id", "")
                            expected_tool_call_ids.add(call_id)
                            tool_calls_found.append({
                                "id": call_id,
                                "type": "function",
                                "function": {
                                    "name": output_item.get("name", ""),
                                    "arguments": output_item.get("arguments", "{}")
                                }
                            })


                    # Add assistant message with tool_calls if any were found
                    if tool_calls_found:
                        assistant_msg = {
                            "role": "assistant",
                            "content": "",
                            "tool_calls": tool_calls_found
                        }
                        new_input.insert(0, assistant_msg)
                        logger.debug(f"[STATEFUL PREP] Extracted assistant message with {len(tool_calls_found)} tool calls and IDs: {expected_tool_call_ids}")
                    
                    # Continue collecting tool responses - don't break yet
                    # We need to include all preceding tool messages that respond to this assistant's tool_calls
                    continue


                # Format the message
                formatted_msg = dict(msg)


                # DeepSeek does not support the 'developer' role. Map it to 'system'
                if formatted_msg.get("role") == "developer":
                    formatted_msg["role"] = "system"


                # Format internal tool results to OpenAI format
                if formatted_msg.get("type") == "function_call_output" or (
                    "output" in formatted_msg and "role" not in formatted_msg and not isinstance(formatted_msg.get("output"), list)
                ):
                    tool_call_id = formatted_msg.get("call_id") or formatted_msg.get("tool_call_id", "")
                    formatted_msg = {
                        "role": "tool",
                        "tool_call_id": tool_call_id,
                        "content": str(formatted_msg.get("output", ""))
                    }
                    if "type" in formatted_msg:
                        del formatted_msg["type"]
                    
                    # Only include tool messages if they match expected tool_call_ids
                    if expected_tool_call_ids and tool_call_id in expected_tool_call_ids:
                        new_input.insert(0, formatted_msg)
                        expected_tool_call_ids.discard(tool_call_id)
                        logger.debug(f"[STATEFUL PREP] Added tool response for {tool_call_id}")
                        continue
                    elif not expected_tool_call_ids:
                        # First tool message - add it and prepare for assistant message
                        new_input.insert(0, formatted_msg)
                        continue


                new_input.insert(0, formatted_msg)


                # Stop extracting after we've seen a user message
                # This prevents pulling in orphaned tool messages from previous turns
                if msg.get("role") in ["user", "developer"]:
                    seen_user_message = True
                    break  # Stop here instead of continuing
            
            # Filter out any purely empty structural messages if necessary, but base interaction usually handles this.
            input_data = system_msgs + new_input if new_input else messages[-1:]
            logger.info(f"[STATEFUL PREP] Final input_data has {len(input_data)} messages (system: {len(system_msgs)}, new: {len(new_input)})")
        else:
            # Initial call: send full message history but ensure proper formatting
            input_data = []
            for msg in messages:
                # Check for LLM response object and extract assistant message
                if "output" in msg and isinstance(msg.get("output"), list) and "role" not in msg:
                    # This is an LLM response object, extract the assistant message with tool_calls
                    tool_calls_found = []
                    for output_item in msg.get("output", []):
                        if output_item.get("type") == "function_call":
                            tool_calls_found.append({
                                "id": output_item.get("call_id", ""),
                                "type": "function",
                                "function": {
                                    "name": output_item.get("name", ""),
                                    "arguments": output_item.get("arguments", "{}")
                                }
                            })


                    # Add assistant message with tool_calls if any were found
                    if tool_calls_found:
                        assistant_msg = {
                            "role": "assistant",
                            "content": "",
                            "tool_calls": tool_calls_found
                        }
                        input_data.append(assistant_msg)
                        logger.debug(f"[STATELESS PREP] Extracted assistant message with {len(tool_calls_found)} tool calls")
                    continue


                formatted_msg = dict(msg)
                
                # DeepSeek does not support the 'developer' role. Map it to 'system'
                if formatted_msg.get("role") == "developer":
                    formatted_msg["role"] = "system"
                
                if formatted_msg.get("type") == "function_call_output" or (
                    "output" in formatted_msg and "role" not in formatted_msg and not isinstance(formatted_msg.get("output"), list)
                ):
                    tool_call_id = formatted_msg.get("call_id") or formatted_msg.get("tool_call_id", "")
                    formatted_msg = {
                        "role": "tool",
                        "tool_call_id": tool_call_id,
                        "content": str(formatted_msg.get("output", ""))
                    }
                    logger.debug(f"[STATELESS PREP] Converted function_call_output to tool message with id: {tool_call_id}")
                input_data.append(formatted_msg)


        normalized_agent_type = (agent_type or "").strip().lower()
        if normalized_agent_type in SYNTHETIC_TOOL_RESPONSE_AGENT_TYPES:
            # Pre-validation: inject synthetic tool responses for tool calls that have no
            # matching tool result message. This must happen BEFORE _validate_tool_sequence so
            # that async tools (classify_lead, communicate_to_user) are not stripped by the
            # validator for the affected agent flow.
            patched_input: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
            for _idx, _msg in enumerate(input_data):
                patched_input.append(_msg)
                if _msg.get("role") == "assistant" and _msg.get("tool_calls"):
                    for _tc in _msg.get("tool_calls", []):
                        _tc_id = _tc.get("id", "")
                        _tc_name = _tc.get("function", {}).get("name", "unknown")
                        _has_resp = any(
                            _m.get("role") == "tool" and _m.get("tool_call_id") == _tc_id
                            for _m in input_data[_idx + 1:]
                        )
                        if not _has_resp:
                            patched_input.append({
                                "role": "tool",
                                "tool_call_id": _tc_id,
                                "content": f"Tool '{_tc_name}' completed.",
                            })
                            logger.debug(
                                f"[PREPARE MESSAGES] Injected synthetic tool response for "
                                f"tool={_tc_name} id={_tc_id} agent_type={normalized_agent_type}"
                            )
            input_data = patched_input


        # Validate and fix tool call sequences before returning
        validated_data = self._validate_tool_sequence(input_data, is_stateful_continuation=bool(previous_response_id))


        # Ensure we don't send empty messages
        if not validated_data:
            logger.warning("[PREPARE MESSAGES] Validation resulted in empty messages - using fallback")
            validated_data = [{"role": "user", "content": "Please respond to the user's previous message"}]


        # Add debug logging for message sequence
        logger.debug(f"[MESSAGE SEQUENCE DEBUG] Final messages being sent to DeepSeek:")
        for i, msg in enumerate(validated_data):
            logger.debug(f"  {i}: {msg.get('role')} - {list(msg.keys())}")
            if msg.get('role') == 'tool':
                logger.debug(f"    tool_call_id: {msg.get('tool_call_id')}")
            elif msg.get('tool_calls'):
                logger.debug(f"    tool_calls: {len(msg.get('tool_calls', []))}")


        return validated_data


    def create_response(
        self,
        model: str,
        messages: List[Dict[str, Any]],
        tools: Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
        previous_response_id: Optional[str] = None,
        agent_type: Optional[str] = None,
        session_id: Optional[str] = None,
        **kwargs
    ) -> LLMResponse:
        """
        Create a response using the DeepSeek core logic.
        
        Note: No longer makes HTTP calls - calls the function directly.
        
        Args:
            model: Model name (e.g., 'deepseek-chat')
            messages: List of messages from base_agent
            tools: Optional list of tool definitions
            previous_response_id: Optional response ID for stateful conversation
            **kwargs: Additional parameters (temperature, max_tokens, etc.)
            
        Returns:
            LLMResponse with response data
        """
        logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Making direct request (no HTTP call required)")


        # Process and format messages
        input_data = self._prepare_messages(messages, previous_response_id, agent_type=agent_type)


        # Build request payload
        # Use agent_type as usecase, fallback to usecase kwarg, then provider default
        usecase = kwargs.get("usecase") or agent_type or "base_agent_chat"
        payload = {
            "usecase": usecase,
            "messages": input_data,
            "model": model,
            "temperature": kwargs.get("temperature", 0.7),
            "max_tokens": kwargs.get("max_tokens", 8000),
        }


        # Add optional parameters
        if tools:
            # Normalize tools - handles format conversion and schema validation
            normalized_tools = normalize_tools(tools)
            payload["tools"] = normalized_tools


            # Log tool details for debugging MCP tool detection issue
            tool_names = []
            mcp_tool_count = 0
            for tool in normalized_tools:
                if tool.get('type') == 'function':
                    name = tool.get('function', {}).get('name', 'unknown')
                    tool_names.append(name)
                    # Check if this is an MCP tool (BigQuery or merchant-support MCP)
                    if name.startswith('bq_') or name.startswith('merchant_'):
                        mcp_tool_count += 1


            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] TOOLS: Passing {len(normalized_tools)} tools to DeepSeek API")
            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] TOOLS: Tool names: {tool_names}")
            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] TOOLS: MCP tools detected: {mcp_tool_count} (bq_*, merchant_*)")
        else:
            logger.warning(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] TOOLS: No tools provided to DeepSeek API!")
        if previous_response_id:
            api_prev_id = previous_response_id
            if api_prev_id.startswith("resp-"):
                api_prev_id = api_prev_id[5:]
            payload["previous_response_id"] = api_prev_id


        # Add other optional parameters
        for param in ['top_p', 'presence_penalty', 'frequency_penalty', 'stop', 'user']:
            if param in kwargs:
                payload[param] = kwargs[param]


        # Check if the most recent tool executions were entirely suppressed/skipped
        # This prevents DeepSeek from infinitely retrying a suppressed tool (like communicate_to_user)
        has_only_skipped_tools = False
        has_terminal_tool = False
        recent_tool_msgs = []
        for msg in reversed(payload["messages"]):
            if msg.get("role") == "tool":
                recent_tool_msgs.append(msg)
            elif msg.get("role") == "assistant" and recent_tool_msgs:
                if msg.get("tool_calls"):
                    terminal_tools = [ToolNames.COMMUNICATE_TO_USER, "respond_to_merchant", "mark_out_of_scope"]
                    for tc in msg.get("tool_calls", []):
                        if tc.get("function", {}).get("name") in terminal_tools:
                            has_terminal_tool = True
                            break
                break
            else:
                # E.g. user message -> not a pure sequence of assistant tool usage
                recent_tool_msgs = [] # Invalidate
                break
                
        if recent_tool_msgs:
            has_only_skipped_tools = True
            for tm in recent_tool_msgs:
                content_str = str(tm.get("content", ""))
                if '"status": "skipped"' not in content_str and "'status': 'skipped'" not in content_str and '"status":"skipped"' not in content_str:
                    has_only_skipped_tools = False
                    break
                
        if has_only_skipped_tools or has_terminal_tool:
            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Short-circuiting API to prevent infinite loop. Skipped tools: {has_only_skipped_tools}, Terminal tool invoked: {has_terminal_tool}")
            # Reuse the previous_response_id so this response chains to the actual last response
            # This way, the next request will continue from the real response, not a fake intermediate one
            response_id = previous_response_id if previous_response_id else None
            fake_response_data = {
                "id": response_id,
                "model": model,
                "choices": [{
                    "index": 0,
                    "message": {
                        "role": "assistant",
                        "content": ""
                    },
                    "finish_reason": "stop"
                }],
                "usage": {"prompt_tokens": 0, "completion_tokens": 0, "total_tokens": 0}
            }
            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Short-circuit response created with ID: {response_id} (reusing previous_response_id)")
            return self._convert_to_llm_response(fake_response_data)


        try:
            # logger.debug(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Request payload keys: {list(payload.keys())}")
            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Final message count: {len(payload['messages'])} and the session_id is {session_id}")
            
            # Log final message sequence for debugging
            logger.info(f"[FINAL API CALL] sessionid is {session_id}. Messages being sent to DeepSeek: ")
            for i, msg in enumerate(payload['messages']):
                msg_role = msg.get('role')
                msg_summary = f"role={msg_role}"
                if msg_role == 'tool':
                    msg_summary += f", tool_call_id={msg.get('tool_call_id', 'missing')}"
                elif msg_role == 'assistant' and msg.get('tool_calls'):
                    tool_ids = [tc.get('id', 'unknown') for tc in msg.get('tool_calls', [])]
                    msg_summary += f", tool_calls={len(msg.get('tool_calls', []))}, ids={tool_ids}"
                elif msg_role == 'user':
                    content_preview = str(msg.get('content', ''))[:50]
                    msg_summary += f", content_preview={content_preview}"
                logger.info(f"  [{i}] {msg_summary}")


            # Call deepseek core logic directly (no HTTP overhead)
            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Calling deepseek_core directly (no HTTP call) for session_id {session_id}")
            response_data, status_code = call_deepseek_chat(
                usecase=payload.get('usecase', 'base_agent'),
                messages=payload.get('messages', []),
                model=payload.get('model'),
                previous_response_id=payload.get('previous_response_id'),
                tools=payload.get('tools'),
                **{k: v for k, v in payload.items() if k not in ['usecase', 'messages', 'model', 'previous_response_id', 'tools']}
            )


            # Check for errors
            if status_code != 200:
                error_detail = response_data.get('error', 'Unknown error') if isinstance(response_data, dict) else str(response_data)
                logger.error(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Error {status_code}: {error_detail} and session_id is {session_id}")
                raise Exception(f"API request failed with status {status_code}: {error_detail} and session_id is {session_id}")


            logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Received response session_id {session_id} and response {response_data}")


            # Log if DeepSeek made any tool calls
            choices = response_data.get('choices', [])
            if choices and len(choices) > 0:
                choice = choices[0]
                message = choice.get('message', {})
                tool_calls = message.get('tool_calls', [])
                if tool_calls:
                    logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] DeepSeek made {len(tool_calls)} tool calls and session_id is {session_id}")
                    for tc in tool_calls:
                        tc_name = tc.get('function', {}).get('name', 'unknown')
                        logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Tool call: {tc_name} and session_id is {session_id}")
                else:
                    logger.info(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] DeepSeek did NOT make any tool calls (response has no tool_calls) and session_id is {session_id}")
            else:
                logger.warning(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Response has no choices or empty choices and session_id is {session_id}")


            # Convert to LLMResponse format
            llm_response = self._convert_to_llm_response(response_data)


            # Track metrics if agent_type provided (emit to Grafana like other providers)
            try:
                if agent_type:
                        from utility.metrics import increment_openai_response, increment_openai_token_usage
                        increment_openai_response(agent_type, model, 200)
                        # Create properly formatted response for metrics (with converted usage)
                        metrics_response = {'usage': llm_response.usage}
                        increment_openai_token_usage(agent_type, model, metrics_response, session_id or -1)
                        logger.debug(f"[METRICS] Emitted usage to Grafana: agent={agent_type}, tokens={llm_response.usage.get('total_tokens', 0)} and session_id is {session_id}")
            except ImportError as e:
                logger.warning(f"[METRICS] Could not import metrics functions: {e} and session_id is {session_id}")
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"[METRICS] Failed to emit usage metrics: {e} and session_id is {session_id}")


            return llm_response


        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"[INTERNAL DEEPSEEK] Request failed: {e} and session_id is {session_id}")
            raise


    def _convert_to_llm_response(self, api_response: Dict[str, Any]) -> LLMResponse:
        """
        Convert internal API response to LLMResponse format.


        Args:
            api_response: Response from our /deepseek endpoint


        Returns:
            LLMResponse object
        """
        # Safely extract response content and tool calls with defensive checks
        output = []
        choices = api_response.get('choices', [])


        if not choices:
            logger.warning("[RESPONSE CONVERSION] No choices found in API response")
            choice = {}
            message = {}
        else:
            choice = choices[0] if isinstance(choices, list) else {}
            message = choice.get('message', {})


        # Add text content if present
        content = message.get('content')
        if content:
            output.append({
                "type": "message",
                "content": [{
                    "type": "output_text",
                    "text": str(content)
                }]
            })
            logger.debug(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Added text content: {len(str(content))} characters")


        # Add tool calls if present - handle None case
        tool_calls = message.get('tool_calls') or []
        if tool_calls:
            logger.debug(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Processing {len(tool_calls)} tool calls")


        for tool_call in tool_calls:
            if not isinstance(tool_call, dict):
                logger.warning(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Skipping invalid tool_call (not dict): {type(tool_call)}")
                continue


            function_info = tool_call.get('function', {})
            if not isinstance(function_info, dict):
                logger.warning(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Invalid function info in tool call: {type(function_info)}")
                function_info = {}


            output.append({
                "type": "function_call",
                "call_id": str(tool_call.get('id', '')),
                "name": str(function_info.get('name', '')),
                "arguments": str(function_info.get('arguments', '{}'))
            })


            logger.debug(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Added tool call: {function_info.get('name', 'unnamed')}")


        # Extract and convert usage information to OpenAI format
        raw_usage = api_response.get('usage', {})
        if not isinstance(raw_usage, dict):
            logger.warning(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Invalid usage data: {type(raw_usage)}")
            raw_usage = {}


        # Map DeepSeek format to OpenAI format for consistent metrics
        usage = {
            'total_tokens': raw_usage.get('total_tokens', 0),
            'input_tokens': raw_usage.get('prompt_tokens', 0),
            'output_tokens': raw_usage.get('completion_tokens', 0),
            'input_tokens_details': {
                'cached_tokens': raw_usage.get('prompt_cache_hit_tokens', 0)
            },
            'output_tokens_details': {
                'reasoning_tokens': 0  # DeepSeek doesn't provide reasoning tokens
            }
        }


        logger.debug(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Mapped usage: {usage}")


        response_id = api_response.get('id')
        if not response_id:
            response_id = f"resp-internal_deepseek_{int(time.time())}"
            logger.debug(f"[RESPONSE CONVERSION] Generated fallback response ID: {response_id}")
        elif "resp" not in response_id.lower():
            response_id = f"resp-{response_id}"
            
        return LLMResponse(
            id=response_id,
            output=output,
            usage=usage,
            raw_response=api_response,
            model=api_response.get('model', 'deepseek-chat')
        )


    def get_provider_name(self) -> str:
        """Return the provider name."""
        return "internal_deepseek"


    def is_recoverable_error(self, error: Exception) -> bool:
        """409 from the proxy means previous_response_id not found — recoverable by retrying without it."""
        return "status 409" in str(error)


    def handle_recoverable_error(self, session_id: str, unset_response_id_callback) -> None:
        """Clear the stale response_id so the next call sends full history instead."""
        unset_response_id_callback(session_id)










- [services/llm/agent_gateway.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/services/llm/agent_gateway.py)
"""
Agent Gateway LLM client — routes agent requests to the self-hosted agent-gateway platform.


Instead of calling Azure/DeepSeek APIs directly, this client forwards requests to the
agent-gateway which runs CLI-based agents (Qoder CLI, Claude Code, Codex CLI) with
persistent sessions, tool access, and source code context.
"""


import os
import json
import logging
import re
import time
import requests
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from .base import BaseLLMClient, LLMResponse, LLMProvider


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# ── Chain-of-thought / reasoning leak sanitization ────────────────────
# CLI agents (deepseek, Qoder) sometimes output their internal reasoning
# as part of the response text. This is NOT meant for the merchant.


# Tag-based patterns — well-defined delimiters from known LLM providers
_COT_TAG_PATTERNS = [
    re.compile(r"<think>.*?</think>", re.DOTALL),
    re.compile(r"<reasoning>.*?</reasoning>", re.DOTALL),
    re.compile(r"\[THINKING\].*?\[/THINKING\]", re.DOTALL | re.IGNORECASE),
]


# Paragraph-level indicators — phrases that ONLY appear in chain-of-thought
_COT_PARAGRAPH_INDICATORS = [
    "MCP tools aren't available",
    "MCP tools are not available",
    "Let me work with what I have",
    "Let me think about",
    "Let me analyze",
    "Let me craft the response",
    "Now I have the key data",
    "I need to introduce myself",
    "I should open as",
    "Since this is an engagement",
    "This is an engagement template hook",
    "RECENT CONVERSATION is essentially empty",
    "RECENT CONVERSATION section",
    "Key facts from the data:",
    "system prompt",
    "none of the merchant-support tools are available",
    "tools are available in this context",
    "I don't have the actual performance data from tools",
    "I cannot fetch actual performance data",
    "Looking at the context more carefully",
    "appears to be a Vera-specific conversation",
]


def _sanitize_cot(text: str) -> str:
    """Strip chain-of-thought / reasoning leaks from CLI agent responses.


    Two-pass approach:
      1. Strip well-known tag-based blocks (<think>, [THINKING], etc.)
      2. Drop paragraphs containing known reasoning indicators.
    Safety net: if ALL content is removed, return original + log warning.
    """
    if not text or not text.strip():
        return text


    original = text


    # Pass 1: strip tag-based CoT blocks
    for pattern in _COT_TAG_PATTERNS:
        text = pattern.sub("", text)


    # Pass 2: paragraph-level indicator detection
    paragraphs = re.split(r"\n\n+", text.strip())


    has_reasoning = any(
        indicator.lower() in para.lower()
        for para in paragraphs
        for indicator in _COT_PARAGRAPH_INDICATORS
    )


    if has_reasoning:
        clean_paragraphs = []
        for para in paragraphs:
            para_lower = para.lower()
            is_reasoning = any(
                indicator.lower() in para_lower
                for indicator in _COT_PARAGRAPH_INDICATORS
            )
            if not is_reasoning:
                clean_paragraphs.append(para)
        text = "\n\n".join(clean_paragraphs).strip()


    # Safety net: if everything was stripped, return original
    if not text:
        logger.warning(
            "[AGENT_GATEWAY] CoT sanitization removed ALL text — returning original "
            "(len=%d). Preview: %s",
            len(original), original[:200],
        )
        return original


    if text != original.strip():
        logger.info(
            "[AGENT_GATEWAY] CoT stripped: original_len=%d, cleaned_len=%d",
            len(original), len(text),
        )


    return text


# Maximum number of messages to send in history (payload size guard)
MAX_HISTORY_MESSAGES = 200


# Default timeout for gateway calls (5 minutes — CLI agents can be slow)
GATEWAY_TIMEOUT = int(os.getenv("GATEWAY_TIMEOUT", "300"))


def _get_gateway_url() -> str:
    """Get the agent-gateway base URL from environment."""
    # Use internal VPC IP (10.140.48.120) instead of external IP (34.93.232.206).
    # External IP routes through Cloud NAT which intermittently drops connections
    # under port exhaustion, causing random LLM call timeouts (130s+ failures).
    # Internal IP uses direct VPC routing — no NAT, consistently <5ms connect.
    url = os.getenv("AGENT_GATEWAY_URL", "http://10.140.48.120:80")
    return url.rstrip("/")


def _extract_system_prompt(messages: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Extract the first system message (base persona prompt)."""
    for msg in messages:
        if msg.get("role") == "system":
            return msg.get("content", "")
    return ""


def _extract_context(messages: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Extract context data from system messages.


    Botops injects context as: {"role": "system", "content": "Order details: {...}"}
    """
    for msg in messages:
        if msg.get("role") == "system" and "Order details:" in str(msg.get("content", "")):
            content = msg["content"]
            # Extract JSON after "Order details: "
            if isinstance(content, str) and content.startswith("Order details:"):
                json_str = content[len("Order details:"):]
                try:
                    return json.loads(json_str)
                except (json.JSONDecodeError, TypeError):
                    return {}
    return {}


def _extract_intent(messages: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Extract subjected intent from system messages."""
    for msg in messages:
        if msg.get("role") == "system" and "Subjected intent:" in str(msg.get("content", "")):
            content = msg["content"]
            if isinstance(content, str) and content.startswith("Subjected intent:"):
                return content[len("Subjected intent:"):].strip()
    return "default"


def _extract_latest_message(messages: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Extract the latest user message from the messages array.


    Only extracts 'user' role messages — 'developer' role content goes
    into developerSignals.input, not as the user-facing message.
    """
    for msg in reversed(messages):
        role = msg.get("role", "")
        if role == "user":
            content = msg.get("content", "")
            if isinstance(content, str):
                return content
            elif isinstance(content, list):
                # Multimodal: extract text parts
                text_parts = [
                    part.get("text", "")
                    for part in content
                    if isinstance(part, dict) and part.get("type") == "text"
                ]
                return " ".join(text_parts)
    return ""


def _message_contains_image(msg: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
    """Return True when a message contains multimodal image parts."""
    content = msg.get("content")
    if not isinstance(content, list):
        return False
    for part in content:
        if isinstance(part, dict) and part.get("type") == "image_url":
            return True
    return False


def _extract_developer_input(messages: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
    """Extract the latest developer message for developerSignals.input.


    Returns the content of the last 'developer' role message, or empty string.
    """
    for msg in reversed(messages):
        role = msg.get("role", "")
        if role == "developer":
            content = msg.get("content", "")
            if isinstance(content, str):
                return content
            elif isinstance(content, list):
                text_parts = [
                    part.get("text", "")
                    for part in content
                    if isinstance(part, dict) and part.get("type") == "text"
                ]
                return " ".join(text_parts)
    return ""


class AgentGatewayClient(BaseLLMClient):
    """Routes LLM requests to the self-hosted agent-gateway platform.


    The gateway runs CLI-based agents (Qoder CLI, Claude Code, Codex CLI) that:
    - Maintain persistent CLI sessions with full conversation context
    - Have access to botops/MCP source code for tool discovery
    - Can execute MCP tool calls directly
    - Resume sessions across turns via native --resume flags


    This client implements the BaseLLMClient interface so it plugs into
    botops' existing agent flow without any changes to base_agent.py.
    """


    def __init__(self, gateway_url: Optional[str] = None):
        self.gateway_url = gateway_url or _get_gateway_url()
        logger.info(f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Initialized with gateway URL: {self.gateway_url}")


    def create_response(
        self,
        model: str,
        messages: List[Dict[str, Any]],
        tools: Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
        previous_response_id: Optional[str] = None,
        agent_type: Optional[str] = None,
        session_id: Optional[str] = None,
        phone_number: Optional[str] = None,
        from_number: Optional[str] = None,
        **kwargs
    ) -> LLMResponse:
        """Forward the request to the agent-gateway and return an LLMResponse.


        The gateway's /chat endpoint handles session routing:
        - If session exists on executor → warm start (latest message only)
        - If session is new → cold start (full history + context)


        Args:
            model: Model name (ignored — gateway decides which CLI tool to use)
            messages: Full message history (system prompts, context, chat history, user message)
            tools: MCP tool definitions the agent can call
            previous_response_id: Ignored — gateway handles session continuity via Redis
            agent_type: Agent class name (e.g., "CustomerAgent")
            session_id: Botops session/ticket ID (context_id)
            phone_number: Merchant/user phone number (the destination number)
            from_number: Sending WA business number (e.g. Vera's outreach line). Combined
                         with phone_number as "{from_number}-{phone_number}" to isolate
                         sessions per use-case when the same merchant is contacted by
                         different agents/numbers.
            **kwargs: Additional provider-specific parameters (ignored)


        Returns:
            LLMResponse with the agent's response
        """
        start_time = time.time()


        # Extract the latest user message separately from history
        user_message = _extract_latest_message(messages)


        # Build history excluding the latest user message — gateway receives
        # message and history as separate fields. However, if the latest user
        # turn is multimodal, keep it in history as well so the gateway still
        # sees the image attachment instead of only the extracted text.
        truncated = messages[-MAX_HISTORY_MESSAGES:] if len(messages) > MAX_HISTORY_MESSAGES else messages
        last_user_idx = None
        for i, msg in enumerate(truncated):
            if msg.get("role") == "user":
                last_user_idx = i  # track the last user message index


        history_messages = []
        for i, msg in enumerate(truncated):
            if i == last_user_idx:
                if _message_contains_image(msg):
                    history_messages.append(msg)
                continue
            history_messages.append(msg)


        # Build session ID: {from_number}-{phone_number} when both are present so that
        # separate use-cases (e.g. Vera merchant vs. customer acquisition) contacting the
        # same destination number get isolated CLI sessions. Falls back to phone_number alone
        # (legacy), then the botops ticket ID (always present).
        if from_number and phone_number:
            gateway_session_id = f"{from_number}-{phone_number}"
        else:
            gateway_session_id = phone_number or session_id


        payload = {
            "useCase": agent_type or "unknown",
            "sessionId": gateway_session_id,
            "sourceSessionId": session_id,
            "message": user_message,
            "history": history_messages,
            "tools": tools or [],
            "developerSignals": {
                "persona": _extract_system_prompt(messages),
                "context": _extract_context(messages),
                "intent": _extract_intent(messages),
                "input": _extract_developer_input(messages),
            }
        }


        logger.info(
            f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Sending request to {self.gateway_url}/chat: "
            f"useCase={agent_type}, sessionId={gateway_session_id}, sourceSessionId={session_id}, "
            f"from_number={from_number}, phone_number={phone_number}, history_len={len(history_messages)}, message_len={len(user_message)}, tools_count={len(tools or [])}"
        )


        # Debug: log the first few history messages to help diagnose payload issues
        if history_messages:
            preview = history_messages[:3]
            logger.debug(f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] First {len(preview)} history messages: {json.dumps(preview, ensure_ascii=False)[:500]}")
        if user_message:
            logger.debug(f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] User message preview: {user_message[:200]}")


        try:
            resp = requests.post(
                f"{self.gateway_url}/chat",
                json=payload,
                timeout=GATEWAY_TIMEOUT,
                headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"}
            )
            resp.raise_for_status()
            result = resp.json()


            duration = time.time() - start_time
            response_text = result.get("response", "")


            # Log warning if gateway returns a failure placeholder
            if not response_text or response_text.strip().lower() == "no response":
                logger.warning(
                    f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Gateway returned empty/placeholder response: "
                    f"useCase={agent_type}, sessionId={result.get('sessionId')}, "
                    f"turnCount={result.get('turnCount')}, "
                    f"full_response={json.dumps(result)}"
                )


            is_new_session = result.get("isNewSession", False)
            logger.info(
                f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Response received in {duration:.2f}s: "
                f"sessionId={result.get('sessionId')}, "
                f"isNewSession={is_new_session}, "
                f"turnCount={result.get('turnCount')}, "
                f"response_len={len(response_text)}, "
                f"response_preview={response_text[:100] if response_text else '(empty)'}"
            )


            if is_new_session:
                logger.info(
                    f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] NEW SESSION CREATED: "
                    f"sessionId={gateway_session_id}, "
                    f"sourceSessionId={session_id}, "
                    f"phone_number={phone_number}, "
                    f"useCase={agent_type}, "
                    f"gatewaySessionId={result.get('sessionId')}, "
                    f"history_len={len(history_messages)}, "
                    f"tools_count={len(tools or [])}, "
                    f"persona_len={len(_extract_system_prompt(messages))}, "
                    f"intent={_extract_intent(messages)}"
                )


            # Adapt gateway response to LLMResponse format
            # The gateway returns: {response, sessionId, isNewSession, turnCount}
            # Botops expects: LLMResponse(id, model, output, usage, raw_response)
            # Since CLI agents handle tool calls internally, output is the text response
            #
            # IMPORTANT: response.id must contain 'resp' prefix — botops validates this
            # in _set_response_id() and _extract_response_id(). CLI agents don't produce
            # OpenAI-style response IDs, so we generate a synthetic one keyed on turnCount.
            turn_count = result.get("turnCount", 0)
            gw_session_id = result.get("sessionId", session_id or "unknown")
            synthetic_response_id = f"resp_{gw_session_id}_turn{turn_count}"


            response_text = result.get("response", "")
            # Convert markdown/HTML links to plain URLs before any other processing.
            # The gateway's CLI agent sometimes returns [text](url) or <a href='url'>text</a>
            # which WhatsApp can't render. Convert to plain URLs so they're clickable.
            if response_text:
                response_text = re.sub(
                    r"<a\s+[^>]*href=['\"]([^'\"]+)['\"][^>]*>[^<]*</a>",
                    r"\1",
                    response_text,
                    flags=re.IGNORECASE,
                )
                response_text = re.sub(
                    r'\[([^\]]*)\]\((https?://[^\)]+)\)',
                    r'\2',
                    response_text,
                )
            response_text = _sanitize_cot(response_text)
            # 🥚 EASTER EGG: only reveal on the secret knock
            if user_message.strip().lower() == "who's driving?":
                response_text = (
                    f"🤖 *a CLI agent is.* turn #{turn_count}, session `{gw_session_id[:8]}…`\n\n"
                    + response_text
                )


            output = [{
                "type": "message",
                "content": [{
                    "type": "output_text",
                    "text": response_text
                }]
            }]


            return LLMResponse(
                id=synthetic_response_id,
                model="qodercli",
                output=output,
                usage={"total_tokens": 0, "input_tokens": 0, "output_tokens": 0},
                raw_response=result
            )


        except requests.exceptions.Timeout:
            duration = time.time() - start_time
            logger.error(
                f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Request timed out after {duration:.2f}s: "
                f"useCase={agent_type}, sessionId={session_id}"
            )
            raise
        except requests.exceptions.ConnectionError as e:
            logger.error(
                f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Connection failed to {self.gateway_url}/chat: {e}"
            )
            raise
        except requests.exceptions.HTTPError as e:
            # Log the full request payload and gateway error details for debugging
            logger.error(
                f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] HTTP error from gateway: {e.response.status_code}"
            )
            logger.error(
                f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Request payload (truncated): "
                f"useCase={payload.get('useCase')}, sessionId={payload.get('sessionId')}, "
                f"message_len={len(payload.get('message', ''))}, "
                f"history_len={len(payload.get('history', []))}, "
                f"tools_count={len(payload.get('tools', []))}"
            )
            logger.error(
                f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Gateway error response body: {e.response.text[:1000]}"
            )
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"[AGENT_GATEWAY] Unexpected error: {e}")
            raise


    def get_provider_name(self) -> str:
        return LLMProvider.AGENT_GATEWAY.value


    def is_recoverable_error(self, error: Exception) -> bool:
        """Gateway errors are not recoverable at the base_agent level.


        Connection/timeout failures are handled by the consumer-level retry
        mechanism (retry status + Kafka re-enqueue) rather than the
        base_agent's Azure-oriented recovery path.
        """
        return False


    def handle_recoverable_error(self, session_id: str, unset_response_id_callback):
        """No recovery action needed — gateway manages session state."""
        pass








- [services/llm/base.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/services/llm/base.py)


"""
Base classes and types for LLM providers.
"""


from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from enum import Enum
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass


class LLMProvider(Enum):
    """Supported LLM providers"""
    AZURE_OPENAI = "azure_openai"
    GEMINI = "gemini"
    DEEPSEEK = "deepseek"
    AGENT_GATEWAY = "agent_gateway"


@dataclass
class LLMResponse:
    """Unified response format from LLM providers"""
    id: str
    model: str
    output: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    usage: Dict[str, int]
    raw_response: Dict[str, Any]


    def model_dump(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Return response as dictionary (compatible with OpenAI response format)"""
        return {
            "id": self.id,
            "model": self.model,
            "output": self.output,
            "usage": self.usage,
            **self.raw_response
        }


class BaseLLMClient(ABC):
    """Abstract base class for LLM clients"""


    @abstractmethod
    def create_response(
        self,
        model: str,
        messages: List[Dict[str, Any]],
        tools: Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]] = None,
        previous_response_id: Optional[str] = None,
        agent_type: Optional[str] = None,
        session_id: Optional[str] = None,
        **kwargs
    ) -> LLMResponse:
        """
        Create a response from the LLM.


        Args:
            model: Model name/ID to use
            messages: List of message dicts with 'role' and 'content'
            tools: Optional list of tool definitions
            previous_response_id: Optional ID for conversation continuity
            agent_type: Agent type for metrics tracking (optional)
            session_id: Session ID for token tracking (optional)
            **kwargs: Provider-specific parameters


        Returns:
            LLMResponse with unified format
        """
        pass


    @abstractmethod
    def get_provider_name(self) -> str:
        """Return the provider name"""
        pass
    
    def is_recoverable_error(self, error: Exception) -> bool:
        """
        Check if an error is recoverable and should trigger conversation reset.
        Subclasses override this for provider-specific error detection.
        
        Args:
            error: The exception that was raised
            
        Returns:
            True if the error is recoverable and conversation should reset
        """
        return False
    
    def handle_recoverable_error(self, session_id: str, unset_response_id_callback):
        """
        Handle a recoverable error by performing provider-specific recovery actions.
        
        Subclasses can override to implement provider-specific recovery logic.
        Default implementation does nothing.
        
        Args:
            session_id: The session identifier
            unset_response_id_callback: Callback function to reset response state
        """
        pass










- [api/vera_core_api.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/api/vera_core_api.py)
"""
Vera Core API Routes


Flask Blueprint for Vera agent API endpoints.


Routes:
- POST /botops/api/vera/core/onboard - Onboard new subscriber
- POST /botops/api/vera/core/daily - Daily cron (reviews + metrics)
- POST /botops/api/vera/core/weekly - Weekly cron (content + posts)
- POST /botops/api/vera/core/monthly-report - Monthly presence report


Usage:
    from api.vera_core_api import vera_core_api
    app.register_blueprint(vera_core_api)
"""


import os
import logging
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from typing import Dict, Any
from agents.vera.agent import VeraAgent
from utility.metrics import increment_tool_call, observe_tool_duration
import time


logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


# Create Blueprint
vera_core_api = Blueprint('vera_core_api', __name__, url_prefix='/botops/api/vera/core')


# Singleton VeraAgent instance (shared across requests)
_vera_agent_instance = None


def get_vera_agent() -> VeraAgent:
    """Get or create VeraAgent singleton instance."""
    global _vera_agent_instance
    if _vera_agent_instance is None:
        _vera_agent_instance = VeraAgent(agent_id="vera_core_1")
    return _vera_agent_instance


def send_whatsapp_callback(
    merchant_id: str,
    message: str,
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = None
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Send WhatsApp message to merchant.


    This is a placeholder - actual implementation would integrate with
    WhatsApp API or messaging queue.


    Args:
        merchant_id: Merchant ID
        message: Message text
        metadata: Optional metadata


    Returns:
        Send result
    """
    # TODO: Integrate with actual WhatsApp API
    logger.info(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Sending WhatsApp to merchant {merchant_id}: {message[:100]}...")


    # Placeholder implementation
    return {
        "status": "success",
        "merchant_id": merchant_id,
        "message_id": f"wa_{merchant_id}_{int(time.time())}"
    }


@vera_core_api.route('/onboard', methods=['POST'])
def onboard_merchant():
    """
    Onboard a merchant to Vera GBP management.


    Request Body:
        {
            "merchant_id": "merchant123",
            "merchant_context": {
                "merchant_name": "Punjab Grill",
                "location": "Connaught Place",
                "category": "Restaurant",
                "cuisine": "North Indian",
                "phone": "+919876543210"
            }
        }


    Response:
        {
            "status": "success",
            "merchant_id": "merchant123",
            "onboarding_result": {...},
            "whatsapp_sent": true
        }
    """
    start_time = time.time()


    try:
        data = request.get_json()


        if not data or "merchant_id" not in data:
            increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "onboard", "error")
            return jsonify({
                "status": "error",
                "error": "Missing required field: merchant_id"
            }), 400


        merchant_id = data["merchant_id"]
        merchant_context = data.get("merchant_context", {})


        logger.info(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Onboarding merchant: {merchant_id}")


        # Get VeraAgent instance
        agent = get_vera_agent()


        # Execute onboarding workflow
        result = agent.onboard_merchant(
            merchant_id=merchant_id,
            merchant_context=merchant_context
        )


        # Send result via WhatsApp
        whatsapp_result = None
        if result.get("status") == "success" and result.get("response"):
            whatsapp_result = send_whatsapp_callback(
                merchant_id=merchant_id,
                message=result["response"],
                metadata={"workflow": "onboarding"}
            )


        increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "onboard", "success")
        observe_tool_duration("VeraAgent", "onboard", time.time() - start_time)


        return jsonify({
            "status": "success",
            "merchant_id": merchant_id,
            "onboarding_result": result,
            "whatsapp_sent": whatsapp_result is not None,
            "whatsapp_result": whatsapp_result
        }), 200


    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Onboarding failed: {e}", exc_info=True)
        increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "onboard", "error")
        observe_tool_duration("VeraAgent", "onboard", time.time() - start_time)


        return jsonify({
            "status": "error",
            "error": str(e)
        }), 500


@vera_core_api.route('/daily', methods=['POST'])
def daily_cron():
    """
    Execute daily review management for merchants.


    Request Body:
        {
            "merchant_ids": ["merchant123", "merchant456", ...],
            "batch_size": 10  (optional, default 10)
        }


    Or for single merchant:
        {
            "merchant_id": "merchant123",
            "merchant_context": {...}  (optional)
        }


    Response:
        {
            "status": "success",
            "processed": 123,
            "succeeded": 120,
            "failed": 3,
            "results": [...]
        }
    """
    start_time = time.time()


    try:
        data = request.get_json() or {}


        logger.info(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Daily cron triggered")


        # Get VeraAgent instance
        agent = get_vera_agent()


        results = []


        # Single merchant mode
        if "merchant_id" in data:
            merchant_id = data["merchant_id"]
            merchant_context = data.get("merchant_context")


            result = agent.daily_review_management(
                merchant_id=merchant_id,
                merchant_context=merchant_context
            )


            # Send via WhatsApp if successful
            if result.get("status") == "success" and result.get("response"):
                send_whatsapp_callback(
                    merchant_id=merchant_id,
                    message=result["response"],
                    metadata={"workflow": "daily"}
                )


            results.append(result)


        # Batch mode
        elif "merchant_ids" in data:
            merchant_ids = data["merchant_ids"]
            batch_size = data.get("batch_size", 10)


            logger.info(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Processing {len(merchant_ids)} merchants in batches of {batch_size}")


            for merchant_id in merchant_ids:
                try:
                    result = agent.daily_review_management(merchant_id=merchant_id)


                    # Send via WhatsApp if successful
                    if result.get("status") == "success" and result.get("response"):
                        send_whatsapp_callback(
                            merchant_id=merchant_id,
                            message=result["response"],
                            metadata={"workflow": "daily"}
                        )


                    results.append(result)


                except Exception as e:
                    logger.error(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Failed to process merchant {merchant_id}: {e}")
                    results.append({
                        "status": "error",
                        "merchant_id": merchant_id,
                        "error": str(e)
                    })


        else:
            increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "daily", "error")
            return jsonify({
                "status": "error",
                "error": "Missing required field: merchant_id or merchant_ids"
            }), 400


        # Count successes/failures
        succeeded = sum(1 for r in results if r.get("status") == "success")
        failed = len(results) - succeeded


        increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "daily", "success")
        observe_tool_duration("VeraAgent", "daily", time.time() - start_time)


        return jsonify({
            "status": "success",
            "processed": len(results),
            "succeeded": succeeded,
            "failed": failed,
            "results": results
        }), 200


    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Daily cron failed: {e}", exc_info=True)
        increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "daily", "error")
        observe_tool_duration("VeraAgent", "daily", time.time() - start_time)


        return jsonify({
            "status": "error",
            "error": str(e)
        }), 500

    """

        observe_tool_duration("VeraAgent", "weekly", time.time() - start_time)

@vera_core_api.route('/outreach', methods=['POST'])
def trigger_outreach():
    """
    Trigger proactive WhatsApp outreach.


    Request Body:
        {
            "merchant_id": "12345"  (optional, for single merchant)
        }
    """
    start_time = time.time()
    try:
        data = request.get_json() or {}
        merchant_id = data.get("merchant_id")


        from run_vera_outreach_cron import VeraOutreachRunner
        runner = VeraOutreachRunner(dry_run=False)
        runner.run(merchant_id=merchant_id)


        increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "outreach", "success")
        observe_tool_duration("VeraAgent", "outreach", time.time() - start_time)


        return jsonify({
            "status": "success",
            "stats": runner.stats
        }), 200
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[VeraCoreAPI] Outreach failed: {e}", exc_info=True)
        increment_tool_call("VeraAgent", "outreach", "error")
        return jsonify({"status": "error", "error": str(e)}), 500


@vera_core_api.route('/merchant/<merchant_id>/state', methods=['GET'])
def get_merchant_state(merchant_id):
    """
    Query merchant Vera state from Redis.
    """
    try:
        import redis
        import json as json_mod
        r = redis.Redis(
            host=os.getenv('VERA_REDIS_HOST', '10.140.1.234'),
            port=int(os.getenv('VERA_REDIS_PORT', '6379')),
            password=os.getenv('VERA_REDIS_PASSWORD', '8c6f0753-9e7f-4341-abe0-89b33d989f9f'),
            db=int(os.getenv('VERA_REDIS_DB', '0')),
            decode_responses=True
        )
        key = f"vera:merchant_state:{merchant_id}"
        data = r.get(key)
        if data:
            state = json_mod.loads(data)
            return jsonify({"status": "success", "merchant_id": merchant_id, "state": state}), 200
        else:
            return jsonify({"status": "success", "merchant_id": merchant_id, "state": None}), 200
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[VeraCoreAPI] State query failed: {e}")
        return jsonify({"status": "error", "error": str(e)}), 500


@vera_core_api.route('/template/usecase', methods=['GET'])
def get_template_usecase():
    """
    Return the routing use_case for a given WhatsApp template name.


    Used by message-server to route inbound merchant replies to the correct agent
    without maintaining a hardcoded template list.


    Query params:
        name (required) — template name, e.g. "vera_profile_visibility_v3"


    Response:
        200 {"use_case": "vera_merchant", "found": true}
        200 {"use_case": null, "found": false}   — unknown template
        400 {"error": "name param required"}
    """
    name = request.args.get("name", "").strip()
    if not name:
        return jsonify({"error": "name param required"}), 400


    try:
        from agents.vera.followup.template_registry import get_registry
        registry = get_registry()
        prefixes = registry.get_routing_prefixes()
        for prefix, use_case in prefixes.items():
            if name.startswith(prefix):
                return jsonify({"use_case": use_case, "found": True}), 200
        return jsonify({"use_case": None, "found": False}), 200
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("[VeraCoreAPI] template/usecase lookup failed: %s", e)
        return jsonify({"error": str(e)}), 500



@vera_core_api.route('/health', methods=['GET'])
def health():
    """Health check endpoint for Vera Core API."""
    return jsonify({
        "status": "healthy",
        "service": "vera-core-api"
    }), 200






- [tests/test_vera_conversation.py](/abs/C:/Users/ADMIN/botops/tests/test_vera_conversation.py)


"""
Emulate a multi-turn conversation with VeraSalesAgent.


Simulates a merchant chatting on Google Chat:
  Turn 1: merchant sends their ID (first contact)
  Turn 2: merchant asks a question / shows interest
  Turn 3: merchant pushes back
  Turn 4: merchant asks about pricing


Captures all responses and verifies chat history is retained across turns.


Usage: python tests/test_vera_conversation.py [merchant_id]
"""
import os
import sys
import json
import asyncio
from datetime import datetime


os.environ['VERA_MCP_SERVER_URL'] = 'http://10.140.1.119/mcp'
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))))


# Conversation turns to simulate
# First message includes merchant_id in text — just like real Google Chat via /vera_sales Hi 7182019
# Subsequent messages are follow-ups (merchant_id already extracted in turn 1)
CONVERSATION = [
    "Hi {merchant_id}",  # Turn 1: mimics "/vera_sales Hi 7182019" — merchant_id in message text
    "ye kya hai? mujhe koi review service nahi chahiye",
    "achha dikhao kya kar sakti ho",
    "pricing kya hai?",
]


class ConversationCapture:
    """Intercepts communicate_to_user and captures messages."""


    def __init__(self):
        self.messages = []  # list of (turn, user_msg, agent_response)
        self.current_turn = 0
        self.current_user_msg = ""


    def patch_agent(self, agent):
        """Monkey-patch agent to capture communicate_to_user responses."""
        original = agent._handle_tool_call
        capture = self


        async def patched(message):
            tool_name = message.get("name")
            tool_args = message.get("arguments", {})
            if tool_name == "communicate_to_user":
                msg_text = tool_args.get("message", "")
                capture.messages.append({
                    "turn": capture.current_turn,
                    "user": capture.current_user_msg,
                    "agent": msg_text,
                })
                from utility.message_protocol import MessageProtocol
                return MessageProtocol.create_tool_result(
                    agent.current_session_id, tool_name,
                    {"status": "success", "message": "Message delivered"}
                )
            return await original(message)


        agent._handle_tool_call = patched


async def main():
    mid = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else "7182019"


    print(f"{'='*70}")
    print(f"  VERA SALES CONVERSATION EMULATOR")
    print(f"  Merchant ID: {mid}")
    print(f"  Turns: {len(CONVERSATION)}")
    print(f"{'='*70}")


    # Clear Redis cache
    from utility.redis_config import get_redis_client
    try:
        redis_client = get_redis_client()
        redis_client.delete(f"vera:sales:{mid}")
        print(f"[OK] Cleared Redis cache for vera:sales:{mid}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[WARN] Redis clear failed: {e}")


    from agents.vera.sales_agent import VeraSalesAgent


    agent = VeraSalesAgent(f"convo-{mid}")
    capture = ConversationCapture()
    capture.patch_agent(agent)


    # Accumulate chat history across turns
    chat_history = []
    session_id = f"convo-{mid}-{int(datetime.now().timestamp())}"


    for turn_idx, user_msg_template in enumerate(CONVERSATION):
        turn_num = turn_idx + 1
        user_msg = user_msg_template.format(merchant_id=mid)
        capture.current_turn = turn_num
        capture.current_user_msg = user_msg


        print(f"\n{'─'*70}")
        print(f"  TURN {turn_num}/{len(CONVERSATION)}")
        print(f"  USER: \"{user_msg}\"")
        print(f"  Chat history length: {len(chat_history)} messages")
        print(f"{'─'*70}")


        # Match REAL Google Chat payload: NO merchant_id in context_data.
        # Agent must extract merchant_id from message text (like production).
        batch_input = {
            "type": "batch_agent_input",
            "session_id": session_id,
            "source_session_id": "",
            "messages": [
                {
                    "message": user_msg,
                    "metadata": {"source": "googlechat"},
                    "message_id": f"msg-{turn_num:03d}"
                }
            ],
            "metadata": {
                "context_data": {
                    "space_name": "spaces/test",
                    "thread_name": "spaces/test/threads/test",
                    "sender_email": "test@magicpin.in",
                    "sender_name": "Test User",
                },
                "subjected_intent": "default",
                "chat_history": chat_history,
                "agent_type": "VeraSalesAgent",
                "source": "googlechat"
            }
        }


        try:
            responses = await agent.handle_batch_input(batch_input)


            # Find the captured response for this turn
            turn_responses = [m for m in capture.messages if m["turn"] == turn_num]


            if turn_responses:
                agent_msg = turn_responses[-1]["agent"]
                print(f"\n  VERA: {agent_msg}")


                # Add both user and agent messages to chat history for next turn
                chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": user_msg})
                chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": agent_msg})
            else:
                print(f"\n  [WARN] No communicate_to_user captured for turn {turn_num}")
                # Still add user message
                chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": user_msg})
                # Try to extract from raw responses
                if responses:
                    for resp in responses:
                        if isinstance(resp, dict):
                            raw = json.dumps(resp, default=str)[:200]
                            print(f"  [RAW] {raw}")


            print(f"\n  [STATE] {agent._current_state}")


        except Exception as e:
            print(f"\n  [ERROR] {type(e).__name__}: {e}")
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": user_msg})


    # Final summary
    print(f"\n\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"  CONVERSATION SUMMARY — {len(capture.messages)} responses captured")
    print(f"{'='*70}")


    for msg in capture.messages:
        print(f"\n--- Turn {msg['turn']} ---")
        print(f"USER: {msg['user']}")
        print(f"VERA: {msg['agent']}")


    # Verify chat history was passed correctly
    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"  CHAT HISTORY VERIFICATION")
    print(f"{'='*70}")
    print(f"  Final chat_history length: {len(chat_history)} messages")
    print(f"  Expected: {len(CONVERSATION) * 2} messages (user + agent per turn)")
    if len(chat_history) >= len(CONVERSATION) * 2:
        print(f"  [PASS] Chat history accumulated correctly")
    else:
        print(f"  [WARN] Some turns may not have captured responses")


    # Show what was in the system prompt for the last turn
    print(f"\n  Last system prompt included chat_history_context: ", end="")
    if hasattr(agent, 'current_chat_history') and agent.current_chat_history:
        print(f"YES ({len(agent.current_chat_history)} messages)")
        for msg in agent.current_chat_history[-6:]:
            role = msg.get("role", "?").upper()
            content = msg.get("content", "")[:80]
            print(f"    {role}: {content}...")
    else:
        print("NO (empty)")


    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print(f"  DONE")
    print(f"{'='*70}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
